<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於如是所說道理不相違背示現宣說，是名為處；若此相違示現宣說，是名非處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果與前文所說四種道理不相違背，開示顯現宣說諸法，稱作處；如果與四種道理相違背的示現宣說，稱作非處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4575"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、明總合說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明總合說，全部合起來有八種處非處善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是四處非處，并前所說，合成八種處非處善巧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是以觀待道理、作用道理、證成道理、法爾道理四種處非處，還有前面成辦門、合會門、證得門、與現行門四門，以這八個角度來觀察蘊、界、處、緣起等一切法的處非處的道理，合起來共有八種處非處善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、問答差別2　子一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科問答差別，以問答方式說明緣起善巧與處非處善巧的差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：緣起善巧、處非處善巧何差別？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：緣起善巧和處非處善巧有什麼差別呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、答2　丑一、辨緣起善巧</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科辨緣起善巧，說明緣起善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：唯於因果生起道理正智顯了，名緣起善巧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：對於因果生起的道理，以聖人的智慧開示顯了，這是緣起善巧。因為緣起善巧，說明緣起的道理，此有故彼有，此無故彼無；此生故彼生，此滅故彼滅。及緣生法相無明乃至老死等差別相，這是佛陀以聖人的智慧徹底通達緣起法性，才能將複雜多變的緣起法相及甚深的法性，觀察入微、如實體證而善巧安立世出世間的因果，所以說於因果生起道理正智顯了，名緣起善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、辨處非處善巧</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨處非處善巧，說明處非處善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於一切無顛倒理正智顯了，名處非處善巧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於一切法無顛倒的道理包括觀待、作用、證成、法爾四種道理，一、何「事」是合於一切「理」的「處」，二、何「事」是不合於「理」（包括上述一切理）的「非處」，由聖人的智慧完全正確沒有錯誤的開顯發出來，稱為處非處善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　緣起善巧在於能具智慧了知因果生起道理，處非處善巧在於能具智慧，辨別一切緣起法是否合道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、略不說餘</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科略不說餘，處非處善巧要略說到這裡，不再多作分辨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘處非處善巧決擇，文不復現。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　處非處善巧要略說到這裡，其餘處非處善巧的決擇文不再顯現了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下面開始說根善巧，根據《大毘婆沙論》卷142所說，佛為什麼要說二十二根？是因為觀所度化的有情，聽聞二十二根的法，可以得到利益，為了眾生可以聞法得益，還要再分別二十二根。這話怎麼說呢？因為當時印度有很多外道，對於根也有種種的想法，例如離繫外道施設生命體有一根，稱作命根，普遍於內外物都有命根，外道安立這樣的理論：凡是相信離繫外道的人，都不可以喝冷水，也不可以砍生草，因為冷水和生草都是有生命的，這是離繫外道的觀點。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　另有一些外道於外物執有意根；有些於外物執有命根；有些於外物執有業根、意根等。又如外道波羅設利說：眼不見色、耳不聞聲，名聖修根。波羅設利有一個弟子名嗢怛羅，有一次曾經來拜訪佛，佛就問他：你的老師波羅設利，為你們說過修根的方法嗎？他說：我的老師說，眼不要見色，耳不要聞聲，稱為聖修根，因為無所取故。佛就難問他說：如果是這樣，那麼盲人看不見應名聖修根，這時阿難在佛旁為佛搖扇，也立刻難問他說：聾子就是聖人了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又如勝論者安立鼻舌眼身耳五根；數論者說五覺根、五業根、意根十一根，又有說一百二十根，就是眼根、耳根、鼻根各有二，共有六根，加上舌根、身根、意根、命根，苦樂憂喜捨五受根，信進念定慧五根，總共有二十根。一個人身上有二十個根，天、人、阿修羅、地獄、餓鬼、畜生，六趣眾生都有二十根，加起來全部應該是有一百二十根。根也是主的意思，外道說有一百二十主，如天主、龍主、阿修羅主及人主等，要受這一百二十處勝妙之身才能夠得到解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上都是外道的主張。因此，有外道來問佛：從一根到一百二十根，有種種說法，佛教到底安立幾根呢？佛陀說：我安立二十二根，就可以攝盡諸根，不增不減，攝諸根盡，多一個也不可以，少一個也不可以，就是這麼多，剛剛好二十二根。這是說到二十二根的緣起，這二十二根當然不是外道的境界，他們的說法都是不正確的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在說的二十二根，是本論的解釋。關於裡面的定義解釋，有一些地方與《大毘婆沙論》、《俱舍論》、及《成唯識論》，有少許的差別，如果有興趣可以對照著來看。本論〈攝事分〉卷98有說到根相應的部分，可以參考；《大毘婆沙論》卷142~145，總共有4卷一大段文都是說二十二根，它是代表部派佛教的重要思想，也很值得參考，其中將緣起說得很清楚。還有《俱舍論》卷3到分別根品中也說到二十二根，《成唯識論》卷7也說到二十二根，也可以參考。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛六、根善巧2　壬一、結前生後</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科根善巧，分二科；第一科結前生後，結束前文，生起後文。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4576"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是已說處非處善巧。根善巧我今當說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已經說過處非處善巧，現在將說一說根善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、決擇一切2　癸一、嗢柁南標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科決擇一切，決斷簡擇二十二根，分二科；第一科嗢柁南標，以偈頌標出決擇的要義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">總嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初義意建立　廣分別為後</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總說根善巧的整個內容，以偈頌標列出來，分成四大部分；二十二根的名義、目的、建立、廣分別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初義是說到二十二根的名義；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二義是安立二十二根的目的；為什麼說二十二根？安立二十二根的因緣，是前面說的那一段義，答外道所問，安立不同於外道的二十二根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三義是建立，說明如何建立二十二根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四義是廣分別，廣泛分別二十二根的種種情況為後。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總共分成四個部分來說明二十二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、長行別釋4　子一、釋名義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科長行別釋，用長行來各別解釋，分四科；第一科釋名義，解釋二十二根的名義，根的名字所含的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何等是根義？答：增上義是根義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼是根的義呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：一件事對於另一件事有強大的影響力量，是另一法生起的強大助緣，以此為依，幫助另一法的生起，這是增上義。〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷28，941頁說：「所趣義故、最勝義故，名為增上。」加強力量以助長趣向某種事物的生成或進展，名增上。以所趣義而言，如修淨戒能趣向於定，故名為增上戒學；又以修定心而趣向增上慧，故名增上心學；以修智見能趣向斷滅煩惱，名增上慧學。以最勝義而言，增上戒學、增上心學、增上慧學，唯獨於佛之聖教有這三種，不共外道，最為殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　據《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷142則提出八種根義，「問何故名根？根是何義？答：增上義是根義；明義是根義；現義是根義；憙觀義是根義；端嚴義是根義；最義是根義；勝義是根義；主義是根義。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、顯所為</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯所為，長行別釋二十二根的第二科顯所為，說明開顯二十二根的目的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：為顯何義？答：為顯於彼彼事彼彼法最勝義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為了顯示哪種道理而開顯二十二根？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：安立二十二根是為了顯示二十二根在各式各樣的事情、各式各樣的法中是最殊勝、最有力量的，所以安立二十二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、明建立2　丑一、長行辨2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科明建立，說明二十二根的建立，分二科；第一科長行辨，以長行說明，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="46429:45096"></a>云何建立二十二根？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼樣來建立二十二根？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋6　卯一、約作業差別辨6　辰一、眼等六根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋二十二根分成六個部分，包括二十二根的作業差別、受用安立、依止差別、有情差別、施設差別、修行次第，分六科；第一科約作業差別辨，依根的不同作用將二十二根分為六類：六內根、男女二根、命根、五受根、五善根、三無漏根，又分六科；第一科眼等六根，先說六根的建立義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4577"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂能取境增上義故，建立六根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼能取色境、耳能取聲境、鼻能取香境、舌能取味境、身能取觸境、意能取法境，以諸根對於取得各自的境界最有力量，所以建立眼耳鼻舌身意六根，這是以取境業用而建立六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科男女二根，說明男女二根的建立義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">安立家族相續不斷增上義故，建立二根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　家族能夠相續不斷，力量最強的就是男根與女根，所以建立這二根。這是以傳宗接代、受孕生胎的功能而建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科命根，說明命根的建立義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為活性命事業方便增上義故，建立一根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以作種種的事業為方便，為了使性命能夠存活相續，要生活下去，而建立命根。如果命都沒有，其他事情就不用談了。這是以存活性命事業的作用而安立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、苦等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科苦等五根，說明苦等五根的建立義。苦、樂、憂、喜、捨，就是苦等五受根。接觸境界時，會有種種的感受；例如身根接觸境界時，有苦受、樂受、捨受；意根接觸境界時，會有苦、樂、憂、喜、捨的感受出現。通常說的苦根與樂根，是指前五識的感受；苦、樂、憂、喜、捨特別安立為第六意識相應受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="8602:45106"></a>受用業果增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生命的一切現象都是業與業的果報，面對境界時，心裡生起種種的感受，覺得痛苦，或是快樂，這都是業果。例如，若造殺生業的人，就容易生病，苦果會多；如果受持不殺生戒，感得身體健康，色相端嚴；常常帶給人快樂，這一生就會活得很高興、很快樂；如果常常使他人憂傷，自己也很難不憂愁。生命中不如意或如意的境界都是業果，這些業果誰來受呢？就是由苦、樂、憂、喜、捨，五受根來受。因此以受用業果增上義而建立苦等五種受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、信等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科信等五根，說明信進念定慧五善根的建立義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">世間清淨增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於成就禪定證得世間清淨，最有力的是信進念定慧五善根，由此能成就禪定證得世間清淨的增上義，而建立信等五根。其實信等五根不只通於世間清淨，也通於出世間清淨。修學世間禪定或出世間聖道，都要先對此善法有信心，才能生善法欲，精進修學。正修禪定或聖道時，對所緣境一定要有明記不忘的念力。及依止定力決斷簡擇諸法成就智慧，如此五種善根成熟，才能成就世間及出世間的清淨。信等五根於世間清淨有增上力，依此增上世間清淨的作用建立五善根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、未知欲知等三根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科未知欲知等三根，說明未知欲知根、已知根、及具知根的建立義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">出世清淨增上義故，建立三根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於成就出世聖道斷除煩惱種子獲得清淨，最有力量的是未知欲知根、已知根、及具知根這三無漏根。以成就出世間清淨的作用而建立三無漏根。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈攝事分〉卷100解釋預流果向名未知欲知根，見道十六心中前十五心是預流果向，是未知欲知根。未知是指未知道聖道，未知道法，未證得法；欲知是指想要證得佛法真理的善法欲；廣義的未知欲知根是指從初發心修行追求聖道，尚未成就聖道的人，都可以有未知欲知根，雖然還沒有真的無漏，也安立在三無漏根中，因為行者畢定會朝向證得無漏。已知根是指預流果以上，或者是初地以上，初果以上乃至四果向的人，都有已知根，就是已經證得諸法的實相的聖人有已知根。具知根，具是圓滿，圓滿證得諸法實相，以二乘來說就是阿羅漢，阿羅漢屬於具知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4578"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》云何建立二十二根等者：謂眼根、耳根、鼻根、舌根、身根、意根、男根、女根、命根、苦根、樂根、喜根、憂根、捨根、信根、精進根、念根、定根、慧根、未知欲知根、已知根、具知根，是名二十二根。此以六門明建立義，隨應配屬，如文可知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前所列，眼根乃至具知根，稱為二十二根。以此眼等六根、男女二根、命根、苦等五受根、信等五善根、未知欲知等三無漏根共六個角度來建立二十二根，隨其所相應的來配屬，如前面的文所配屬；從能取境增上義建立眼等六根；安立家族相續不斷增上義建立男女二根、為存活性命事業方便增上義建立命根；受用業果增上義建立苦等五根；世間清淨增上義建立信等五根；出世清淨增上義建立未知欲知根等三根，以這樣來思惟，可以知道二十二根的建立義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、約受用安立辨2　辰一、第一義2　巳一、辨受用4　午一、眼等六根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約受用安立辨，以受用境界的不同來安立二十二根，有二種解釋，分二科；第一科第一義，先說第一種解釋，又分二科；第一科辨受用，以受用辨別二十二根的安立，又分四科；第一科眼等六根，說明眼等六根受用顯境增上義，而建立六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，受用顯境增上義故，建立六根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，受用色聲香味觸法等明顯的境界，最有力的是眼耳鼻舌身意六根，故安立眼等六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科男女二根， 說明受用隱境增上義故，建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受用隱境增上義故，建立二根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受用看不到的境界最有力量的是男根和女根，所以建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科命根，說明受用境界時分邊際增上義故，建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受用境界時分邊際增上義故，建立一根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受用境界時間的長短分量、邊際，最有力量的是命根，所以建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、苦等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科苦等五根，說明受用境界發生雜染增上義故，建立苦等五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受用境界發生雜染增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受用色聲香味觸法境界時，由於有苦樂憂喜捨等感受，而產生愛等種種的煩惱，對於引發煩惱雜染最有力量的是苦等五受，因此建立苦等五根。《長阿含經》卷10：佛告阿難，緣受有愛，假使一切眾生沒有樂受、苦受、不苦不樂受，就不會有愛的雜染。佛又告訴阿難，眾生緣受有愛，因愛有求，因求有利，因利有用，因用有欲，因欲有著，因著有嫉，因嫉有守，因守有護。阿難！由有護故，有刀杖、諍訟、作無數惡。《大智度論》卷98〈88 薩陀波崙品〉說：一切眾生皆求樂畏苦、貪愛其身，眾生受用境界時，為厭苦欣樂生起愛等煩惱雜染乃至生雜染，因為由愛有取，由取有有，由有有生，由生有老死憂悲苦惱純大苦聚，所以說苦等五受根對受用境界發生雜染最有力量，因此建立五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、明安立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明安立，說明安立信等五善根及三無漏根的八根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">安立清淨增上義故，建立八根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以對於證得禪定成就世間清淨，及證得聖道成就出世間清淨，最有增上力的是信進念定慧五善根，還有未知欲知根、已知根、具知根的三無漏根，而建立八根。信進念定慧是通世間、出世間清淨的資糧，有了信進念定慧為基礎，就能證入未知欲知根，以未知欲知根為依止能夠見道，以見道為依止，能夠證聖道果，成就已知根，以已知根為依止能夠令所修圓滿，證得具知根，這八根於安立清淨最為殊勝有力。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4579"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》受用隱境增上義故者：意地中說：由能感男女業故，一分有情男根生起，一分有情女根生起。遞相陵犯，起諸邪行，遂為他人之所訶訾，方造室宅以自隱蔽。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/02.htm#45125:1397">陵本二卷十三頁152</a>）此說受用隱境，其義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧意地〉卷2，67頁中說：器世間成就後，劫初有情最初從光音天來到世間，人的身上都有光明，那時還沒有家宅以及聚落，一切地面都很平正，從此以後由於諸多有情福業的力量，地上長出地味。漸次地餅林藤，不種粳稻自然出現，這些稻米沒有米糠等粗穀，接著又有有米糠等粗穀（粳米）的稻子出現，最後處處粳稻叢生，於是有情才取來受用。由受用地味等資生因緣，有情之類惡色便起，光明就滅。多食地味的人惡色愈增，身極沈重，這些有情就互相輕視毀辱，惡法現行，由此因緣所有地味等漸漸隱沒於地。又從此緣諸有情類互相觀看，便心生愛染，又由能感男女的業力，一部分有情生起男根，一部分有情生起女根，遞相陵犯，造諸邪行，於是被他人訶斥毀呰，才建造房子隱蔽自身。此處說受用隱境，是指有情於隱蔽處受用男女之事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、第二義2　巳一、辨受用4　午一、眼等六根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二義，第二種解釋，說明二十二根的建立，分二科；第一科辨受用，以諸根受用境界說明二十二根的建立，又分四科；第一科眼等六根，以內門受用境界增上義故，建立眼等六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，顯於內門受用境界增上義故，建立六根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，為開顯有情內身能夠受用境界，其中力量最強的是眼耳鼻舌身意六根，所以建立眼等六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科男女二根，說明以外門受用境界增上義故，建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顯於外門受用境界增上義故，建立二根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為開顯有情向外受用色聲香味觸及他身等外塵，其中力量最強的是男根及女根，所以建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科命根，說明以受用內身增上義故，建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受用內身增上義故，建立一根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為開顯有情受用內身，使身體能夠繼續存活，最有力量的是命根，所以建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、苦等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科苦等五根，說明以外境及與內身發生雜染增上義故，建立苦等五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">受用外境及與內身發生雜染增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為開顯有情受用外境色聲香味觸法，及內身的六根，而生愛等雜染，所以建立苦樂憂喜捨五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、明安立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明安立，以對治雜染、安立清淨增上義故，建立信等五根及未知欲知根等三根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">對治雜染、安立清淨增上義故，建立八根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以能對治煩惱雜染，安立世間及出世間清淨，最有力量的是信進念定慧五善根及未知欲知根、已知根、具知根三無漏根，因此建立八根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4580"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》顯於內門受用境界等者：眼等六根內六處攝，故名內門。思所成慧地決擇中說：若由此法增上力故，外色聲等處差別生，為所受用。如是名為由增上故，說名內法。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/66.htm#45137:52784">陵本六十六卷九頁5277</a>）其義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼耳鼻舌身意六根，是屬於內六處所攝，稱作內門。在〈思所成慧地〉的決擇文當中說：由於內六根需要受用境界的增上力，才會有外面的色聲香味觸法等差別相產生，為六根所受用，這是由增上故，說名內法，如〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷66，2115頁所說的道理，就可以知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、約依止差別辨6　辰一、眼等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約依止差別辨，以所依身的差別相說明二十二根的建立，分六科；第一科眼等五根，以依止端嚴增上義故，建立眼等五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，依止端嚴增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，為了使身體看起來端正、莊嚴，力量最強的就是眼耳鼻舌身這五根。如果沒有眼睛、沒有耳朵，看起來就不漂亮、不好看，為了使令身相看起來端正莊嚴，所以建立眼等五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、意根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科意根，說明建立意根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能令依止隨自在轉增上義故，建立一根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了能使令身體隨著心自在運轉，最有力量的就是意根，所以建立意根一根。《俱舍論》引《契經》說：心能導世間，心能遍攝受，如是心一法，皆自在隨行。心能夠引導世間，也能夠普遍攝受一切法，心這一法能夠驅使所依身自在活動，由此增上義故，建立意根。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此外，依止意根觸對法塵生起意識，由意識造作淨不淨業，能招感可愛及不可愛的果報，眾生所依的果報身隨意根所生意識的造作而有不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科命根，說明建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依止安住增上義故，建立一根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　令有情依止的根身能夠安住一段時期，如五十年、六十年，或七十年等，最有力量的就是命根，由此增上義故，建立一根，即是命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科男女二根，說明建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依止出生增上義故，建立二根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止出生有情身心，能夠傳宗接代等，最有力量的就是男女二根，由此增上義故，建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、苦等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科苦等五根，說明建立苦樂憂喜捨五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依止損益增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能令所依止的身體受到損害或增益，最有力量的就是苦樂憂喜捨五受根，而建立五受根。喜、樂二受能令身體健康、心情快樂，對所依止的身體能得到增長利益；憂苦二受使人免疫力下降，生出種種疾病，有害身心；捨受通於二種，損與益裡面都有捨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、信等八根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科信等八根，說明建立信進念定慧、未知欲知根、已知根、具知根等八根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4581"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依止解脫增上義故，建立八根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能夠使令身心成就解脫的功德，使煩惱及苦果之身寂靜，最有力量的就是信等五善根及未知欲知等三無漏根，所以建立八根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能令依止隨自在轉等者：謂由意根能發淨不淨業，愛非愛果諸所依身隨彼轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止意根觸對法塵生起意識，由意識造作淨不淨業，能招感可愛及不可愛的果報，眾生所依的果報身隨意根所生意識的造作而轉變，這是能令依止隨自在轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯四、約有情差別辨2　辰一、第一義6　巳一、眼等六根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科約有情差別辨，以有情的差別相說明二十二根的建立，有二種說法，分二科；第一科第一義，以第一種說法來分辨，又分六科；第一科眼等六根，建立眼等六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，顯有情事增上義故，建立六根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，為開顯有情三界五趣的果報體等種種事，最具有代表性的就是眼耳鼻舌身意六根，所以建立六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科男女二根，說明建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">生有情事增上義故，建立二根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　男女二根對於生出有情生命體數量增加這件事最有力量，所以建立二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科命根，說明建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">令有情事若住、若沒增上義故，建立一根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能使有情果報體在世間能夠安住存活或死沒，力量最強的是命根，所以建立一根，就是命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、苦等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科苦等五根，說明建立苦樂憂喜捨等五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顯諸有情受用境界增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為開顯、最能夠表達出有情受用境界的就是苦樂憂喜捨等五受根，所以建立五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、信等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科信等五根，說明建立信進念定慧等五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顯諸有情勝生方便增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了顯示有情成就一生比一生增上殊勝的生命，最有力量的是信進念定慧這五善根，所以建立五根。信進念定慧強的人，通常作善事多作惡事少，能夠使有情到人天領受好的果報，這是增上生，也名為勝生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》勝生方便增上義故者：增上生道，是名勝生方便應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　增上生道是指人天的果報，一生比一生好，名增上生。例如說，這一生是人，發願再來人間行菩薩道，由於信進念定慧不斷的在增強當中，下一生來會更好，也可以稱為增上生。倒不一定唯指從人到天，才是增上生，只要一生比一生更好，就名增上生。信進念定慧有這種功能，令有情得到增上生，所以說顯諸有情勝生方便增上義故，建立五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4582"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳六、未知欲知等三根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科未知欲知等三根，說明三無漏根能令有情得到決定勝，建立三根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顯諸有情定勝方便增上義故，建立三根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為開顯諸有情決定能夠趣證涅槃，不再領受生死苦果，成就決定殊勝的利益，最有力量的方法是成就三無漏根，因此建立三根。如果有了三界的果報，雖然是增上生，還是純大苦聚。如果能入涅槃了，再沒有三界的果報，就是決定勝。成就決定勝，最方便的、最重要的管道是漸次的修行，從資糧位、加行位、見道位、修道位，一直到無學位，因此以成就決定勝，最有力量的是三無漏根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》定勝方便增上義故者：決定勝道，名定勝方便應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　決定勝是涅槃，道是方便、方法的意思。成就決定勝涅槃的方法，稱為定勝方便應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、第二義5　巳一、眼等六根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二義，以第二種說法，建立二十二根，分五科；第一科眼等六根，建立眼等六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，顯有情事增上義故，建立六根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，為顯示有情事增上義故，建立眼耳鼻舌身意六根。這與第一義一樣，不過下面有一點差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科男女二根，說明建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顯了有情增長增上義故，建立二根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了顯示有情數量能夠增長，也必須有男女二根，由此有情增長增上義故，所以建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科命根，說明建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顯了有情壽漸損減增上義故，建立一根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了顯示能令有情的壽命漸漸損減，最有力量的是命根，所以建立命根這一根。其它法都可能增增減減，但有情的命根從出生開始，唯減無增，過一天就少一天，過一小時少一小時，這是命根的特性。《法句譬喻經》卷3〈19 喻老耄品〉佛為比丘們開示說：「命欲日夜盡，及時可勤力，世間諦非常，莫惑墮冥中，當學然意燈，自練求智慧，離垢勿染污，執燭觀道地。」有情的生命正日夜遞減中，好時不多，應當及時精進修道，世間諸事無常，不要迷惑墮入生死輪迴的黑暗，應當學習如理作意，點燃智慧的光明，遠離煩腦的塵垢，不要生起染污，依止光明的智慧，修學聖道，成就超越三界苦果的涅槃決定勝道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、苦等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科苦等五根，說明建立苦樂憂喜捨五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顯了有情興盛、衰損增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情興盛時，有喜根與樂根的活動；衰損時，有憂根與苦根的活動，捨根是通於興盛與衰損的，因此能夠顯示有情興盛，對衰損最有力量的是苦樂憂喜捨五受根，因此建立五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、信等八根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科信等八根，說明建立信進念定慧及三無漏根等八根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顯了有情功德、過失增上義故，建立八根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能夠顯示有情對治煩惱的功德，以及煩惱的過失，成就世間清淨的禪定及出世間清淨的聖道，最有力量的是信進念定慧五善根及三無漏根，因此建立八根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4583"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》功德過失增上義故者：世出世間能對治道，是名功德。所治煩惱，是名過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　世間道與出世間道能夠對治煩惱，都是有功德的。世間道是指禪定，初禪、二禪、三禪、四禪，乃至空無邊處定、識無邊處定、無所有處定、非想非非想處定，這些定能夠對治降伏欲界、色界、無色界的煩惱；出世間道指無漏的聖道，能對治斷除煩惱種子，乃至不再輪迴三界，這二種都是有功德的，所被對治的煩惱，就是過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯五、約施設差別辨2　辰一、在家品2　巳一、配建立4　午一、眼等六根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科約施設差別辨，以名言施設差別說明二十二根的建立，分二科；第一科在家品，以在家眾說明二十二根的建立，又分二科；第一科配建立，將名言施設配合二十二根的建立，又分四科；第一科眼等六根，說明依名建立六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，依如是名，建立六根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，依眼耳鼻舌身意這些名言施設，來建立六根。眼耳鼻舌身意也是假名安立的，是依如是名，而建立六根。這是依胎生有情於六處位諸根圓滿時，建立六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科男女二根，說明依種姓建立二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依如是種、如是姓，建立二根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依如是族姓，建立男女二根。《瑜伽論記》說，種姓是指父母種姓，即迦葉等種，剎帝利等姓，若以中國人的習慣，種類是指形相上的差別，族姓是張王陳李等姓。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、苦等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科苦等五根，以受用四食的差別建立五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依如是食、如是受苦樂，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依受用段、觸、思、識四食差別，能生喜、樂、憂、苦、捨等受，建立苦樂憂喜捨五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科命根，說明依壽量長短建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依如是長壽、如是久住、如是壽量邊際，建立一根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依壽量長短，有情是長壽、短壽、久住、或證得初果乃至阿羅漢等成就壽量邊際，依壽量差別來建立命根這一根。《瑜伽論記》卷9〈自他利品〉：圓測法師說：南閻浮提人五十歲以上名長壽，八十歲以上名久住，百歲以上名壽量邊際。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、結明依</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結明依，結束此十四根依在家品的施設建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此諸根，依在家品施設建立。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知以上所說眼等六根、男女二根、苦等五根及命根，這十四根，是依在家品施設安立。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷16解釋這段文說：「這是依八施設句而建立六根，依如是名為第一，指名中有體；種姓為第二，指父母種姓即迦葉等種剎利等姓也；如是食苦樂為第三，指依好飲食則受喜樂，依惡飲食則受憂苦等；如是壽為四；如是住為五；如是壽量為第六。以上依在家品施設。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依如是名建立六根者：由六處滿，名有情身生究竟故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　胎生有情在羯羅藍等處胎位時，眼等六處還沒有圓滿，等到六處圓滿時，即是有情果報身可受用究竟時，依眼等名建立六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、出家品2　巳一、配建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出家品，說明出家品之分二科二十二根，分二科；第一科配建立，依出家品說明二十二根中後八根的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4584"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依如是信、如是精進，乃至如是慧、如是向、如是果，建立八根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依對佛法有清淨的信心，有向上向善的精進力，有專注所緣的定力，有明記不忘的念力，還有決斷簡擇的智慧等五種善根；又由初果向建立未知欲知根，初果以上到四果向建立已知根，阿羅漢果建立具知根，所以建立五種善根及三無漏根等八根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、結明依</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結明依，結說明八根依出家品建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此諸根，依出家品施設建立。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知五種善根及三無漏根等八根，是依出家人修行的資糧及證果的次第而建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如是向如是果者：依此建立後三根應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止初果向建立未知欲知根，初果以上到四果向建立已知根，阿羅漢果建立具知根，名如是向、如是果建立三無漏根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯六、約修行次第辨6　辰一、眼等六根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科約修行次第辨，以修行次第說明二十二根的建立，分六科；第一科眼等六根，說明依修根律儀建立眼等六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，依修行者防護根門增上義故，建立六根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，佛陀常常告誡修行人，要防護眼根不要貪色、耳不要貪聲、鼻不要貪香、舌不要貪味、身不要貪觸、意不要貪法，依修根律儀防護根門最有增上力故，建立眼耳鼻舌身意六根。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷16解釋這段文說：眼等六根能生各種過失，發起根律儀防護，這是由能防護安立所防護六法為根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科男女二根，說明依男女二根正常，才能出家證沙門果，而建立二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">堪得出家證沙門果增上義故，建立二根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要能夠出家修道證果，男根和女根必須正常，如果沒有男女根，在《大毘婆沙論》說，男女根都不具足的人，不但不能造善，修十善業；也不能造惡，不會作十惡業，乃至不能斷善根，大善大惡、都不能作。因此依堪得出家證沙門果增上義故，建立男女二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科命根，依壽命長有助於善品的積集建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">積集善品增上義故，建立一根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生命在活的時候，才能夠積聚戒定慧等善品及修學世出世善，命不在的時候，不能積聚善品，依壽命長有助於善品的積集建立命根。《大方廣佛華嚴經》卷26〈入不思議解脫境界普賢行願品〉說：菩薩壽量具足故，能得長時無間修習，所有善根積集增長，能久住世自利利他，是為壽命圓滿之果。《成唯識論義蘊》卷1說：諸菩薩壽量具足，於長時無間積集善品，功德圓滿，不失正見，是名菩薩壽量具足果。可見命根長短也影響修行的成果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、苦等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科苦等五根，說明建立五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4585"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">正知而行增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修行人如果具足正知，隨時正確的知道自己內心的苦樂憂喜捨受，則不會被受所轉而生愛等雜染。煩惱多數隨感受而生，要能不生煩惱，必須保持與佛法相應的正念，觸對境界陷入苦樂憂喜捨等種種的情緒當中時，馬上能覺察了知，就是正知，若能正知就能保持正念。〈五識身相應地意地〉卷54決擇說：正知是住律儀者、精進行者所依止處，而正知的對象最主要是五受根，因此說以正知而行增上義故，建立五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、信等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科信等五根，建立信進念定慧五善根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">證沙門果諸方便道增上義故，建立五根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於證沙門果修學聖道，最有助益的是信進念定慧五善根，因此說以證沙門果諸方便道增上義故，建立五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、未知欲知等三根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科未知欲知等三根，建立三無漏根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">證沙門果增上義故，建立三根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以能夠證得聖道果，最有力量的是三無漏根。因為未知欲知根有助於見道位；已知根有助於修道；乃至到圓滿的具知根有助於現法樂住。所以以對於證沙門果增上義故，建立三根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、嗢柁南結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科嗢柁南結，以偈頌總結前文所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨境界轉等　由顯及內門　莊嚴二有情　假設防護等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　將前面六大科，以偈頌總結前文所說，由下之六類增上義，說明二十二根的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、以諸根作業差別，取境增上（六根）、家族相續（男女二根）、為活性命（命根）、受用業果（五受根）、世間清淨（五善根）、出世清淨（三無漏根）等建立二十二根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、以受用增上義，顯境（內門）（六根）、隱境（外門）（男女二根）、時分邊際（內身）（命根）、發生雜染（五受根）、安立清淨（五善根及三無漏根）等建立二十二根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、以依止差別增上義：莊嚴（五根）、隨自在轉（意根）、安住（命根）、出生（男女二根）、損益（五受根）、解脫（五善根及三無漏根）等建立二十二根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、以有情事差別有二義，其中第一義顯有情事（六根）、生有情事（男女二根）、若住若沒（命根）、受用境界（興衰）（五受根）、勝生方便（五善根）、定勝方便（三無漏根）等建立二十二根；第二義顯有情事增上義（六根）、顯了有情增長增上義故建立二根（男女二根）、顯了有情壽漸損減增上義故建立一根（命根）、顯了有情興盛衰損增上義故建立五根（五受根）、顯了有情功德過失增上義故建立八根（五善根及三無漏根）。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、以施設安立差別，依名（六根）、種姓（男女二根）、食、受苦樂（五受根）、長壽、久住、壽量邊際（命根）、出家修行所依五善根、向果（三無漏根）等建立二十二根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、以修行次第，防護根門（六根）、堪得果（男女二根）、積集善品（命根）、正知而行（五受根）、方便道（五善根）、證沙門果（三無漏根）等建立二十二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、廣分別2　丑一、初嗢柁南攝2　寅一、長行辨8　卯一、作業差別6　辰一、眼等六根2　巳一、舉眼根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科廣分別，詳細分別二十二根，分二科；第一科初嗢柁南攝，說明第一個偈頌所攝的內容，包括作業差別、假實差別、所攝差別、善等差別、異熟等差別、界繫差別、諸地差別、得捨差別八科，又分二科；第一科長行辨，以長行說明，又分八科；第一科作業差別，說明二十二根作業差別，又分六科；第一科眼等六根，先說明眼等六根作業，又分二科；第一科舉眼根，舉眼根為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：眼根作何等業？答：於諸色境已見、今見、當見為業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：眼根能夠作什麼事，有何作用呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：對於色的境界，過去已見，現在見到的，未來要見到的有見的功能。眼以見為業，前面說，眼識只能見現在色，不能見過去、未來色，此處是以眼根功能的範圍而言，過去的眼根能見過去色，未來的眼根能見未來色，就已見、當見。事實上，凡夫的眼根，只能緣現在的色法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、例餘根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘根，如眼根如是，其它的耳等根也是同樣的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是耳根乃至意根所有作業，如應當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如眼根如是，耳於諸聲境，已聞、今聞、當聞為業；鼻於諸香境，已嗅、今嗅、當嗅為業；舌於諸味境，已嚐、今嚐、當嚐為業；身於諸觸境，已觸、今觸、當觸為業；意於諸法境，已了、今了、當了為業，可推理了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4586"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於諸色境已見今見等者：謂過去法雖已謝滅，然彼無間為緣，熏習相續，能令當來餘法得生，由是義故，說彼眼根已見為業。又現在法能為現在眼識所依，由是說彼今見為業。又未來法因性未受，待緣當生，由是說彼當見為業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過去的眼根，雖然已消失、凋謝、滅除了，然而能無間為緣，由過去業力熏習到阿賴耶識的種子，使令眼根能夠繼續相續，將來還會生出另外一個眼根，由此道理，說眼根已見為業。又現在的眼根能為眼識所依，作眼識的增上緣，使眼識能了別色法為業用；又未來眼根雖然還沒有生起，可是已經有眼根的種子，只要有緣，就能為眼識所依了別色塵，故說當見為業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科男女二根，說明男女二根令有情互相攝受為業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：男根、女根作何等業？答：父母、妻子、親戚、眷屬互相攝受顯現為業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：男根、女根能夠作什麼業用？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：男女二根可以使父母，妻子、兒女、親戚，眷屬互相攝受顯現為業。由於有男女二根，使令有情互相攝受，繁衍後代，擴大家族成員。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科命根，說明命根能夠令諸有情繼續存活住持為業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：命根作何等業？答：令諸有情墮在存活住持數中為業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：命根能夠作什麼業用？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：命根能夠令諸有情入於（墮）繼續存活、安住、持續、有生命的種類（數）為它的功能。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、苦等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科苦等五根，說明苦等五根能領納興衰為業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：受所攝根作何等業？答：令諸有情領納一切興盛、衰損為業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：受所攝的苦樂憂喜捨五根，這五受根能夠作什麼業用？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：喜根與樂根令有情領納興盛為業；苦根與憂根令有情領納衰損為業；捨根是通於興盛與衰損，五受根能夠令諸有情領納一切興盛、衰損為其業用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、信等五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科信等五根，說明信等五根能生善趣及能圓滿涅槃資糧為業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：信等諸根作何等業？答：能生善趣及能圓滿涅槃資糧為業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：信進念定慧這五善根能有什麼業用？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有二個業用，第一增上生，五善根能使令有情生到人天的善趣；第二決定勝，能夠使有情修行圓滿涅槃的資糧，證得無漏的涅槃。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、未知欲知等三根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科未知欲知等三根，說明三無漏根能於現法趣證涅槃為業用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：最後三根作何等業？答：能於現法趣證涅槃為業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：最後三無漏根能有什麼業用？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：能夠使有情於現在的色受想行識趣向或證得涅槃，令有情趣向於決定勝的涅槃。三無漏根的前二根未知欲知根、已知根，可使有情分證涅槃趣向圓滿證得涅槃，具知根使令有情圓滿證得涅槃，因為具知根是阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4587"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、假實差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科假實差別，長行解釋初嗢柁南的第二科，從假有與實有，來分別二十二根的假實差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如是諸根幾是實有？幾非實有？答：十六實有；餘非實有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：這二十二根中，哪一些根是屬於實有？哪一些根是屬於假有的？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有十六根是實有的；餘其六根不是實有。若是實有的色、心、心所法，是屬實有，若依諸實法分位假立，是假有的。二十二根中屬於實有的，總共有十六個，包括眼耳鼻舌身意六根、苦樂憂喜捨五受根、信進念定慧五善根。其它六個屬於假法，包括男女根、命根及三無漏根。男女根為什麼是假？因為它是依附身根的分位，所以是假有。命根是心不相應行法，依過去業力所招感時量決定，於色心相續的時間、數量、分位上而假安立，無實自體，所以是假。最後三無漏根是意根、信進念定慧、樂喜捨等九個根的分位，所以是假法。修行證聖道的人應該會很歡喜、安樂，所以有喜受、樂受；因為沒有煩惱，可以捨除煩惱，也會有捨受，這五受根中，一定是樂喜捨，加上意根的分位，一定要用意根來修行，如此共四個，再加上五善根信進念定慧就有九個，所以三無漏根是這九根的分位。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》十六實有等者：眼乃至意，苦乃至捨，信乃至慧，如是十六體是實有。男女二根，及與命根、三無漏根，皆唯假立，故非實有。義如下說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼耳鼻舌身意六根，苦樂憂喜捨五受根及信進念定慧五善根，這十六個屬於實有。男女二根，不是實有，三無漏根是以喜樂捨意，與信進念定慧等九根為體，也是假立，不是實有，道理如下文所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、所攝差別2　辰一、總明攝5　巳一、色所攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科所攝差別，說明二十二根攝屬色法、心法、心不相應行法、有為、無為、善法、不善法等範圍的差別相，分二科；第一科總明攝，先總說各類根由何法所攝，又分五科；第一科色所攝，說明眼耳鼻舌身及男女七根屬於色法所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾色所攝？答：七。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中有哪些根屬於色法所攝？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：眼耳鼻舌身及男女二根，這七色根屬於色法所攝。</span></span></span></div>
