<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸二形者成就幾根？答：容有十九。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：諸二形者，同時有男女根的人，成就幾根？答：除三無漏根，其餘十九根都可能現行成就。由於二形者有男根，也有女根，但是不能修行證聖道，因此沒有三無漏根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》容有十九者：除三無漏，容有所餘，說有十九。以諸二形生者，定不成就無漏根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除三無漏根，其餘諸根都可能現行成就，因此說有十九。因為同時有男根與女根的人，一定不能成就無漏根，所以去掉三無漏根，剩下十九根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、斷善根等差別2　戌一、斷善根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科斷善根等差別，說明斷不斷善根者所成就的根差別，分二科；第一科斷善根，說明斷善根者所成就的根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：斷善根者成就幾根？答：除八，容有餘。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：斷善根這一類的人，成就幾根？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：除去信進念定慧及三無漏八根，其餘十四根都可能現行成就。本論卷1說；斷善根者是利根的人，成就上品諸惡意樂現行法；信順惡友；這類人的邪見煩惱極重圓滿到究竟；於一切惡現行中毫無畏懼；毫無哀愍；令善法不能現行名斷善根。《俱舍論》卷17記載，起上品之邪見，否定因果之理時，僅斷欲界與生俱有之善根，且九品（九階段）之善根係由九品邪見逆順相對，漸次而斷，並非一時之間頓斷，須彌四洲中，除北俱盧洲之外，其餘三洲之人皆有此斷善根。善根有五種是信進念定慧，三無漏根是五善根之果，除信進念定慧及三無漏八種，其餘十四根都可能現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》除八容有餘者：謂信等五及三無漏，是此所除。由斷善根者，現行善根相違相續，名斷善根。以是不能生起聖道，是故除之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　信進念定慧這五根，還有三無漏根，是此處所除之八根。由於斷善根的人，沒有現行的善根，善根也不能相續，名為斷善根。由於不能生起聖道，所以將信進念定慧五善根及三無漏根簡除掉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、不斷善根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不斷善根，說明不斷善根者所成就根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：不斷善根者成就幾根？答：容有一切。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：不斷善根的人成就幾根？答：二十二根都可能現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、凡聖差別2　戌一、異生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科凡聖差別，說明凡聖所成就根的差別，分二科；第一科異生，先說凡夫成就根，異生就是凡夫，凡夫的思想不同，相貌也不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸異生成就幾根？答：十九，除後三。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：諸凡夫成就幾根？答：諸凡夫有十九根現行成就，除後面三無漏根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4600"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、見諦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科見諦，說明見諦者所成就根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸見諦者成就幾根？答：容有一切。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：諸見諦的人成就幾根？答：二十二根都可能現行成就。諦是諸法如，諸法的實相名為諦。見到諸法實相的人，是見諦者，一切聖人可以通名見諦者，這裡諸見諦者，所成就根容有一切是總說，下面是別說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉五、學無學差別2　戌一、有學</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科學無學差別，說明四向三果之有學聖人及四果無學阿羅漢所成就根的差別，分二科；第一科有學，說明有學聖者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：有學成就幾根？答：容有二十一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：有學聖者成就幾根？答：除了具知根，二十一根都能現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》容有二十一者：謂除具知根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除具知根外，只有二十一根現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、無學</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無學，說明阿羅漢所成就的根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：無學成就幾根？答：容有十九。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：無學聖者成就幾根？答：除未知欲知根、已知根及憂根這三根之外，十九根都可能現行成就；包括眼等五根、男根、或女根、意根、命根、苦樂喜捨四受根，五善根及具知根。男女眾都能修學聖道證阿羅漢果，又因圓滿斷除三界愛見煩惱，三無漏根圓滿名為具知根。阿羅漢不會再造感得人天果報的善業，也不造感得三惡道的不善業，功德圓滿也不會有出離欲俱行憂，所以阿羅漢除掉憂根，唯有苦樂喜捨四受根，加上意根、命根及五善根、七色根及具知根，容有十九根都可能現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》容有十九者：謂除未知欲知根、已知根，及憂根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　容有十九根是指除掉未知欲知根、已知根及憂根三種，所以說只有十九根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉六、沙門果向差別4　戌一、預流果向</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科沙門果向差別，說明初果、二果、三果、四果及初果向、二果向、三果向、四果向聖者所成就根的差別，分四科；第一科預流果向，先說明預流果向的聖者成就根。預流是入於聖流，加入聖人的流類成為聖人這一類的初果聖人。初果向是指證入初果之前，正向於初果的聖人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：預流果向成就幾根？答：容有二十。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：初果向的聖人成就幾根呢？答：因為已知根是指初果以上的聖人，具知根是阿羅漢。除掉已知根與具知根外，眼等五根、男根、或女根、意根、命根、苦等五受根，信等五善根及未知欲知根，容有二十根都能現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》容有二十者：謂除已知根、具知根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　容許有二十根現行成是指除已知根和具知根的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、預流果等2　亥一、舉預流果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科預流果等，說明從初果到四果向聖者所成就的根差別，分二科；第一科舉預流果，舉初果聖者所成就根為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：預流果成就幾根？答：亦容有二十。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：初果的聖者成就幾根？答：總說容有二十根能現行成就，除了未知欲知根與具知根，其餘眼等五根、男根、或女根、意根、命根、苦等五受根，信等五善根及已知根二十根都能現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4601"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、例餘隨應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘隨應，以初果聖者所成就根為例，隨其他乃至三果向聖人也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如預流果，一來果向、一來果、不還果向，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如初果聖者成就二十根，一來果向，是二果向的聖人；一來果就是二果，因為一來人間天上往返一次，就可以證阿羅漢果，所以稱一來果；向於三果的不還果向聖人，也是一樣，總說容有二十根都能現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》亦容有二十者：謂除未知欲知根、具知根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　也容許有二十根現行成就，是指除掉未知欲知根及具知根的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、不還果等2　亥一、舉不還果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科不還果等，不還果是指斷盡欲界九品修惑，不來欲界受生的三果聖人。說明三果聖人及阿羅漢向所成就的根差別，分二科；第一科舉不還果，舉三果的聖者所成就根為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：不還果成就幾根？答：容有十九。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：不還果的聖者成就幾根？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：除掉未知欲知根、具知根及憂根不可得。其餘的眼等五根、男根、女根、意根、命根、苦樂喜捨四受根，信等五善根及已知根十九根都能現行成就。初果向的聖者才有未知欲知根，不還果的聖者超越未知欲知根，而尚未成就阿羅漢，所以沒有具知根，又因為完全斷除欲界分別起與俱生起的欲，因此也沒有憂根，因此去掉這三根，剩下十九根，這是三果聖人的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、例阿羅漢向</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例阿羅漢向，阿羅漢向聖者也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如不還果，阿羅漢向亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同不還果成就十九根，四果向的聖者也一樣，也是沒有未知欲知根、具知根，以及憂根，只有十九根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》容有十九者：謂除未知欲知根、具知根，及憂根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　容許有十九根，是指除未知欲知根、具知根，及憂根的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、阿羅漢果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科阿羅漢果，說明阿羅漢果所成就的根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：阿羅漢果成就幾根？答：容有十九。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：阿羅漢果成就幾根？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：除未知欲知根、已知根，及憂根不可得，有眼等五根、男根、女根、意根、命根、苦樂喜捨四受根，信等五善根及具知根等十九根能現行成就。因為阿羅漢已經超越未知欲知根及已知根，也絕對沒有欲界的憂了，所以除掉這三根，其餘十九根都能現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》容有十九者：謂除未知欲知根、已知根，及憂根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　容許有十九根，是指除未知欲知根、已知根及憂根的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、生色界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科生色界，說明生到色界的人所成就根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若生色界成就幾根？答：容有十八。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若生到色界的人，能夠成就幾根？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：除掉男根、女根、苦根、憂根，色界的人，有十八根，包括有眼等五根、意根、命根、樂喜捨三受根，信等五善根、未知欲知根、已知根及具知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4602"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》容有十八者：謂除男、女、苦、憂根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　容許有十八根，是指除男、女、苦、憂四根的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、生無色界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科生無色界，說明生無色界天的人所成就根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：生無色界成就幾根？答：容有十一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：生無色界的人成就幾根？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：無色界的人只有十一根，包括意根、命根、捨根、信等五根、未知欲知根、已知根及具知根。因為無色界的人無業果色，所以除去七色根，又因只有捨受相應，所以再除去苦、樂、喜、憂四受根，唯有十一根能現行成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》容有十一者：謂除眼等五根，及男、女、苦、樂、喜、憂根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　容許有十一根，是指除掉眼耳鼻舌身、男根、女根等七色根，苦樂喜憂四受根的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、明捨得2　巳一、約欲界沒生欲界辨2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明捨得，說明眾生死時及受生時得根的差別相，分二科；第一科約欲界沒生欲界辨，說明欲界眾生死了捨棄哪些根，以後又生到欲界時得到某些根的情況，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若欲界沒欲界生時，當言捨幾根，得幾根？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若欲界眾生死了又生到欲界時，應當說捨幾根，得幾根？　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答5　未一、色根2　申一、具闕得捨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分五科；第一科色根，先說色根，又分二科；第一科具闕得捨，說明具足色根或闕色根者，得捨諸根的情形。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：且約色根容有而說。或捨闕諸根，得闕諸根；或捨闕諸根，得具諸根；或捨具諸根，得具諸根；或捨具諸根，得闕諸根；</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：以這人有色根來說，有四種情形：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、是捨棄所闕諸根，又得到闕根的情形；比如這人在欲界時，色根有缺，可能眼根或耳根不具足，死後下一生再到欲界來受生時，也是缺諸根，下一生還是一樣色根不具足。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、是捨棄所闕諸根，得到色根具足；比如這人在欲界時，色根有缺，死後下一生再到欲界受生時，是色根具足。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、或捨棄圓滿具足的色根，又得到圓滿具足的色根；比如這人在欲界時，色根具足，下一生再到欲界受生時，也是色根具足。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、是捨棄圓滿具足的色根，得到闕根的果報。比如這人在欲界時，色根具足，下一生再到欲界來受生時，得到闕根的果報，色根不具足。他可能是做了一些惡事，如殺盜淫妄等，尤其是殺生，或是斷了某個動物的手與腳，可能下一生自己也會得這種果報，他捨掉圓滿具足的色根，得到缺諸根的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是以欲界異熟果報所得色根的捨與得而言，廣說通於善惡趣眾生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、勝劣得捨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科勝劣得捨，說明得捨諸根的殊勝或下劣差別。色根比較殊勝或是比較差。有的地方解釋，殊勝的五根是指人天善趣的五根，三惡趣的五根就比較下劣，事實上同一趣眾生諸根也有勝劣差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或捨劣諸根，得劣諸根；或捨劣諸根，得勝諸根；或捨勝諸根，得劣諸根；或捨勝諸根，得勝諸根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　得捨諸根的勝劣差別有四種情形：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、捨劣諸根，得劣諸根：今生死時捨掉品質比較差的五根，下生還是得到品質差的五根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、捨劣諸根，得勝諸根：譬如捨惡趣牛或狗的五根，下生再來欲界人天受生，得到殊勝的五根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、捨勝諸根，得劣諸根：捨棄欲界人天殊勝的五根，死後到三惡道受報，得到下劣的五根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、捨勝諸根，得勝諸根：本來是人天的諸根，死後到人天繼續去受報，得的也是殊勝的色根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、意根命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科意根命根，說明意根與命根得捨的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">意根、命根勝劣得捨，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　意根是有情的心，命根是有情的壽命。意根、命根勝劣得捨，也與前面一樣，或從劣到劣，或從劣到勝，或從勝到劣，或從勝到勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4603"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、受根2　申一、例隨應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科受根，說明受根勝劣得捨差別，分二科；第一科例隨應，以色根為例，受根隨其相應的也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸受根勝劣得捨，隨其所應亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若諸受根勝劣得捨，隨其受生處所相應的情形也同色根一樣；或從劣到劣，或從劣到勝，或從勝到劣，或從勝到勝。如果生到人天有殊勝的喜樂根；如果到三惡趣，有下劣的憂苦諸根。勝劣得捨，是以喜樂憂苦來說，隨眾生受生處所相應的捨與得的情況，得的感受也不一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋差別，解釋受根的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此約異熟果故有差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是以異熟果說有差別。如果等流果就不一定了，人天也有可能有劣的感受，畜生也有可能殊勝的感受，譬如說有福報的畜生，牠也有可能有樂受與喜受，前面曾分析過了。這裡是指異熟果，是以整體的總果報來說，若人天應是殊勝的；如果三惡趣則是下劣的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此約異熟果故有差別者：謂受差別，唯約業生異熟及異熟所生而為論故，非餘一切。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受的差別，這裡是指業所感生的三界五趣的異熟果，還有異熟果所生的受而言，不是指現前的境界所產生的苦樂憂喜捨。感生的異熟果就是阿賴耶識，異熟所生指阿賴耶識所生的五蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、信等五根2　申一、捨劣得勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科信等五根，說明信進念定慧五根勝劣得捨差別，分二科；第一科捨劣得勝，捨下劣的信等五根，得殊勝的信等五根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸善根約等流果，捨前前劣，得後後勝，非由生故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若信進念定慧五種善根，以等流果來說，若曾熏習過佛法，栽培過信進念定慧，每熏習一次，善根就增強一次，雖然隔生，只會生生增上，一生比一生殊勝，捨前前劣，得後後勝，這不是以業生異熟果來說，是以等流果來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、捨勝得劣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科捨勝得劣，信等五根也有捨勝得劣的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">捨勝得劣，後邪方便乃有斯義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　信等五根捨勝得劣的人，是因為有邪方便，就是斷善根的情況才有這種道理，不然的話，應該是捨前前劣，得後後勝；還有一種情況就是他本來是人或天，後來到三惡趣受生也有可能捨勝得劣，使他的信進念定慧不能增長。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、最後三根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科最後三根，說明三無漏根的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">最後三根，於一切位與生相違，是故不說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最後三無漏根於一切狀態，能令有情不再流轉生死，與受生相違，所以這裡不說這件事情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、約欲界沒生色界等2　午一、略說一切2　未一、舉從欲界沒生色界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約欲界沒生色界等，以從欲界五趣死的眾生，生到色界天或無色界天諸根得捨差別，分二科；第一科略說一切，要略說明一切，又分二科；第一科舉從欲界沒生色界，說明從欲界死生到色界天的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4604"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：從欲界沒色界生時，捨幾根，得幾根？答：容捨下地一切，容得上地一切。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：從欲界死的有情，生到色界時，會捨掉幾根，得到幾根呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：總相來說，捨掉下地一切諸根，前面說欲界有二十二根；容得上地一切諸根，上地是指色界，初、二禪天有十八根，三禪天有十七根，四禪天有十六根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例於欲界沒生無色等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例於欲界沒生無色等，以欲界沒，生色界為例，欲界沒，生無色界等也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如欲界沒色界生時，從欲界沒無色生時，從色界沒無色生時，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如在欲界死的有情生到色界去，或從欲界死以後，生到無色界天；或是從色界天死後生到無色界的情況，也是一樣。捨下地一切的根，得上地一切的根。生到那裡，隨著自己的業果，會具足所生那一地的根，捨下地一切諸根，得上地一切諸根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》容捨下地一切等者：前說若生欲界，容有一切根成就。若生色界，容有十八。此二一切，如彼當知。生無色界，容有十一。得彼一切，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說若生到欲界二十二根都可能成就，若生色界天有十八根。前面曾討論過，初禪天、二禪天有十八根，三禪天有十七根，如果生到四禪天有十六根。如果生到無色界天的空無邊處、識無邊處、無所有處，這三處裡面有十一根；如果生到非想非非想處天，只有八根。捨下地一切根，得到無色界天一切諸根，道理應當也是一樣，對照前文所說就知道情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、簡後三根2　未一、簡無異熟</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡後三根，簡別後三無漏根，分二科；第一科簡無異熟，簡別三無漏根沒有異熟果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">最後三根，由證沙門果方便而得，不由沒生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最後三無漏根是從哪裡得到？未知欲知根、已知根及具知根，是由於修行人證得成就沙門果的方便而得，經過沙門果的修行而得到這三無漏根。不會因為死亡以後而產生這些根，這三無漏根不是異熟所產生的，不是一種果報，是修行證果得來的無漏根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、顯彼增上2　申一、於等流果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯彼增上，開顯三無漏根也會增上，分二科；第一科於等流果，於等流果能增上。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">先修習力所任持故，後等流果轉盛而生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就等流果來說，因為過去的修習力，不斷的修習聖道所保任執持的緣故，後等流果，下一次再修行時，會展轉的強盛。例如若不斷的靜坐，或不斷的研讀經論，會一次比一次更加的進步，一次比一次更加的好。這是由先修習力所任持故，使後平等流類的等流果轉盛而生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、於異熟果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於異熟果，對於異熟果來說也有差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4605"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又能為緣，生異熟果，令轉明盛。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為有未知欲知根、已知根等三無漏根，一定不會到三惡道受生，一定會得到人天增上生的異熟果，因此三無漏根能為緣，生異熟果，令果報更加的光明殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、嗢柁南結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科嗢柁南結，中間舉出偈頌，將前面所說的諸根差別作一個總結。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業實有色等　善等異熟等　若界若諸地　及死生得捨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　中間的偈頌說：業、實有、色等，善等、異熟等、若界、若諸地，及死生得捨，總結共有八個部分已經討論過了；所對應的是指作業差別、假實差別、所攝差別、善等三性差別、分別異熟等差別、界繫差別、諸地差別、死生得捨差別，現在用簡單的幾個字，將前面所分析的結果表達出來。以上是以分八門來討論二十二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、第二嗢柁南攝2　寅一、長行辨6　卯一、境義差別3　辰一、總顯2　巳一、有義非有義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二嗢柁南攝，廣分別的第二嗢柁南攝，分二科；第一科長行辨，以長行來說明第二個偈頌，內容有境義差別、依處差別、證得等差別、相攝差別、長養差別、諸句差別，又分六科；第一科境義差別，首先說明境義差別，又分三科；第一科總顯，總合起來顯示，又分二科；第一科有義非有義，說明什麼是有義？什麼是非有義？《瑜伽論記》說有義是有境界；非有義是無境，說明有境、無境的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根由境界義名有義？幾非耶？答：二十一名有義，一非。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中有哪幾根，是由境界的義理，稱作有義？哪幾根不是？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：二十一根；二十二根中除了一個命根。命根不是有境界的，命根是由過去業力所引的，不能說是有境界。其他的都與受用境界有關，是由境界義名有義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由境界義名有義等者：謂若由根增上，能受用境，根望彼境，得有義名。命根一種，由依先業所引時量決定而建立故，唯是假有，故說一非。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若由根的增上力量，能受用境界，根相對於這些境界，能攝受境界，稱為有義。命根這一根是由過去生的業力所引生，有決定的時間、數量而建立，是五十歲、六十歲或七十歲等，命根是假有法，命根沒有境界，不是有義。眼耳鼻舌身根可以接觸境界，男女根一定有境界義；苦樂憂喜捨也是因為與境界接觸；信進念定慧是在善法境界上的種種情況，未知欲知根是趣向無分別的境界，已知根與具知根也是一樣，只有命根沒有境界，所以總說二十一根名有義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、色非色助伴2　午一、色於非色為助伴</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科色非色助伴，說明色法與非色法的助伴，是能幫助它生起的，稱為助伴，分二科；第一科色於非色為助伴，說明色法於非色法為助伴。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾於非色助伴義轉？答：七色根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根哪些是非色法的助伴，能夠這樣現前？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：七色根，就是眼耳鼻舌身，還有男女二根，這七色根是其他非色法的助伴。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾於非色助伴義轉等者：此中助伴，謂俱有相應，非同行相應，其義應知。眼等五根，男女二根，名七色根。此與非色心心所法俱有而轉，名於非色助伴義轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處助伴是指七色根與非色等俱有相應，不是指同時和合運轉的心心所法之同行相應，因為心心法於同一所緣展轉同行名同行相應，它的道理應當了知。眼耳鼻舌身五根，還有男根、女根，這是七色根。這裡的非色法包括意根，苦樂憂喜捨，信進念定慧這些心所法，還有三無漏根。七色根與這些非色法的心心所法同時一起活動，稱為助伴。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　俱有相應，依《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷5〈3 相應品〉：「俱有相應者，謂一身中諸蘊界處，俱時流轉同生住滅。&hellip; 同行相應者，謂心心法於一所緣展轉同行。」。《雜集論述記》卷7：「俱有相應者一身五蘊同起盡故、或四大相、或剎那相，諸有為五蘊是起盡必同，必無心法正生，色法正滅，必無此事，勢用等故，極迅速故」。本論卷1：「彼助伴者，謂彼俱有相應諸心所有法。所謂，作意觸受想思，及餘眼識俱有相應諸心所有法。又彼諸法同一所緣，非一行相，俱有相應，一一而轉。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　俱有相應是指諸法同時和合運轉，如前所舉五蘊同時生滅名俱有相應；又如〈五識身相應地〉卷1所舉五識助伴（心所與五識和合運轉）名俱有相應。同行相應是指心和心所法於一所緣展轉同行相應，如卷1，10頁所説「又彼諸法同一所緣，非一行相，俱有相應，一一而轉。」即是指心和心所法於一所緣展轉同行相應。然同行相應復有多義，由是再說非一行相、俱有而轉、一一而轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4606"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、非色於色為助伴</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科非色於色為助伴，說明非色法對於色法也有助伴義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾色非色為助伴耶？答：餘有義根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些非色法，是色法的助伴呢？　</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：其他有境界的根。命根不是有義根，不在這裡討論。除掉七色根以外，其他意根、苦樂憂喜捨、信進念定慧、還有未知欲知根、已知根與具知根，都有可能為色根的助伴。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾色非色為助伴等者：此中問意，謂幾非色為色助伴。是故答言：餘有義根。於二十一名有義中，除七色根，簡取餘根，名餘有義根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所問的是：哪些非色法是色法的助伴呢？回答說：除了命根外，其他的有義根。在二十二根中，除了命根、七色根以外，簡取其他的根，都是有義的非色根。二十一有義根中除掉七色根，還有十四根是所餘的有義根，能作為色根的助伴。以上是先總說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、別辨12　巳一、五色根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別說明諸根所取的境界，分十二科；第一科五色根，說明五色根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：五色根何義？答：色等五各別境。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：五色根為何說是有境界，是什麼義理？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：色聲香味觸的五境，是眼耳鼻舌身根各別緣取的境，五色根是以色聲香味觸這五塵，各別為境。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、第六根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第六根，討論第六意根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：第六根何義？答：一切法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：第六根，第六意識依止的意根，以什麼境界？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：意根以有為、無為等一切諸法為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、男女根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科男女根，討論男女根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：男女根何義？答：因欲相應，即觸所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：男女根為何說是有義？答：因為與欲相應，是屬於觸所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》因欲相應即觸所攝者：謂男女根依身所觸，名為有義，由是說言即觸所攝。此觸復以分別欲貪為因，是故說言因欲相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　男女根是依著身根的相觸而有的境界，名為有義，因此說是屬於觸所攝。會相觸是以分別的欲貪為因，所以說因欲相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、五受根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科五受根，討論五受根所取的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4607"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：五受根何義？答：隨順苦、樂、憂、喜、捨處，即六根義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：五受根是以什麼為境界？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由六根接觸色聲香味觸法，隨順於有苦、有樂、有憂、有喜、有捨的境界，會生起苦樂憂喜捨五種受，所以五受根就是六根的境界。苦、樂、捨是前五根的境界，五受是意根的境界</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、信根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科信根，討論信根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：信根何義？答：應得應捨所有境界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：信根是什麼境界？答：信根是以應得善、應捨惡所有的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳六、精進根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科精進根，討論精進根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：精進根何義？答：即於二種若得、若捨俱無所憚。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：精進根是什麼境界呢？答：二種，是指善或惡，希望得到善捨掉惡，或是得到惡捨掉善，很勇猛都沒有害怕，這是精進根。通常精進根是以得善捨惡來說，才是正精進，如果是邪精進，就是得惡捨善。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳七、念根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科念根，說明念根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：念根何義？答：於聞思修憶持不忘。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：念根的境界是什麼？答：對於聞思修的佛法能在心裡憶念、受持、明記不忘，就是念根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳八、定根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科定根，討論定根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：定根何義？答：奢摩他、毗鉢舍那。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：定根的境界是什麼？答：奢摩他的止和毗鉢舍那的觀 ，都是屬於定根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜阿含經》卷17：說修習於止，終成於觀，修習觀已，亦成於止，聖弟子止、觀俱修，得諸解脫界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳九、慧根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科慧根，討論慧根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：慧根何義？答：所知真實。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：慧根的境界是什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：所知真實是慧根的境界。慧根能通達第一義諦諸法實相的境界，這是所知真實。真實由淺到深有四種：一、世間極成真實，二、道理極成真實，三、煩惱障淨智所行真實，四、所知障淨智所行真實。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十、未知欲知根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科未知欲知根，討論到未知欲知根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4608"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：未知欲知根何義？答：修諦現觀者，從善法欲已去，於一切方便道中，即彼五根義當知是此義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：未知欲知根是什麼樣的境界？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：想要轉凡成聖，必須修諦現觀，修行人從有善法欲、發出離心，想出家修行開始，修五停心觀、別相念住、總相念住，乃至三十七道品等一切方便道中，所有的信進念定慧，都屬於未知欲知根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》即彼五根義當知是此義者：由前已說最後三根是五根分，故五根義即是此義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於前文說最後三無漏根，是信進念定慧的分位，因此信進念定慧的境界，是未知欲知根的境界，是相同的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十一、已知根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科已知根，討論已知根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：已知根何義？答：從預流果乃至金剛喻定，即彼五根義當知是此義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：已知根是什麼境界？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：證得從預流果一直到四果向金剛喻定之間，所成就的信等五善根的境界，都屬於已知根的境界。具已知根的聖人與未知欲知根都是信進念定慧五根，只是強度不同。金剛喻定，是指能破除最微細的煩惱的禪定，此定如同金剛能摧斷一切物，稱為金剛喻定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十二、具知根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科具知根，討論具知根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：具知根何義？答：從初無學道乃至無餘涅槃界，即彼五根義當知是此義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：具知根的境界是什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：從初證入阿羅漢果一直到入無餘依涅槃以前，信進念定慧等五善根的境界，就是具知根的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以下以諸門分別二十二根的差別相，若能掌握〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1841頁諸蘊分別中所說二十九法，包括：有色、有見、有對、有漏、有為、有諍、有愛味、依耽嗜、世間、墮界、過去、現在、未來、內、外、麤、細、劣、妙、遠、近、三界繫、三性、學、無學、非學非無學、見所斷、修所斷、無斷等的定義及解釋，就能幫助理解此處問答的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、料簡2　巳一、約諸門辨7　午一、有色有見有對等3　未一、有色等3　申一、有色為義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科料簡，詳細思考簡別二十二根的差別相，分二科；第一科約諸門辨，以七個角度來說明二十二根的差別相，分有色有見有對等、有漏有為有諍等、過去現在未來、三界繫及不繫、善不善無記、學無學非學非無學、及見斷修斷非斷七科，又分七科；第一科有色有見有對等，又分三科；第一科有色等，以有色有見有對等分別，又分三科；第一科有色為義，又以有色等分別，說明有色根及以有色根為義者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4609"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾有色，有色為義？答：七。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪一些是屬於有色法，以有色為境界？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：眼耳鼻舌身五根及男女二根，是屬於有色法的七根，以有色為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、有色無色為義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有色無色為義，說明無色法以有色無色為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾無色，有色無色為義？答：除命根，餘一切。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪一些是屬於無色法，以有色法與無色法為其境界呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：除掉命根與七色根外，還剩下十四根，包括意根，苦樂憂喜捨五受根，信進念定慧五善根，未知欲知根、已知根及具知根是屬於無色法，這些無色根是以有色法與無色法為它的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、非有色非無色為義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科非有色非無色為義，說明非有色非無色法以非有色非無色為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾非有色非無色，非有色非無色為義？答：即此命根，是假法故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪一些是屬於非有色非無色，它不是屬於色法，也不是屬於無色，但也是以非有色非無色為它的境界呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：就是命根這一法，命根是依色無色法安立的假法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾有色有色為義等者：謂七色根有色為義。一切無色以有色無色為義。二十二中除七色根，復除命根，名為餘故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七色根是眼耳鼻舌身根還有男女根，本身是有色，而且是以有色法為它的境界。第二個問題是問幾無色？一切無色法所緣的境界可以包括有色法與無色法。二十二根裡面除了七色根與命根之外，剩下的十四根是無色根，說名為餘，是以有色無色為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、有見等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有見等，說明有見法以有見為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾有見，有見為義？答：一切非有見。一有色以有見為義；及餘非有色一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些是屬於有見，是以有見為其境界？　</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：這裡分為依勝義與依世俗二種方式回答。一切非有見，是依勝義道理回答，因為一切法現前，如眼見色等，要由眾緣所生，現行之後剎那就滅，沒有真實的作用，無有一法真實存在過，不能說是眼根見色，還是眼識見色，故說一切非有見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若依世俗道理回答，眼根乃至意根等於見色乃至知法等是最主要的助緣，故可安立是眼見色。眼根所取、眼識所緣的色塵境界，就是有見義。因此安立眼根一有色，能夠以有見（可以看得見）的色塵為它的境界，及於諸無色法中一分與眼根一起活動的眼識（意根所攝）等也是以有見色為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1855頁所說可為引證：「問：如說眼見諸色乃至意了諸法，此為眼等是見者乃至是了者耶？為彼識耶？答：約勝義道理，非是眼等，亦非彼識。何以故？諸法自性眾緣生故，剎那滅故，無作用故。約世俗道理，眼等最勝，故可於彼立見者等。何以故？若有眼等諸根，識決定生，無所缺減」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　及餘非有色一分，廣說指14非色根中一分與眼根一起活動者，也是以有見為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4610"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾有見有見為義等者：此中問意，謂幾根能見，名幾有見。彼所行境，亦名有見，由是復言有見為義。思所成地勝義伽他中說：諸行皆剎那，住尚無況用。即說彼生起，為用為作者。眼不能見色，耳不能聞聲，鼻不能齅香，舌不能嘗味，身不能覺觸，意不能知法。於此亦無能，任持驅役者。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/16.htm#45506:13581">陵本十六卷七頁1389</a>）由是當知，約勝義諦，眼尚不能見色，何況餘根。是故答言：一切非有見。唯說眼根以有見為義，如是眼根，名一有色。又於諸無色中，簡取一分與眼根俱有轉者，名餘非有色一分，此與眼根同所行境，是故亦說有見為義。思所成慧地決擇有見諸法差別，亦說眼識所緣故。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/65.htm#45506:51718">陵本六十五卷九頁5180</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處問題的意思，指能見的根有幾個？彼所活動的境界，也稱作有見。因此又説以有見為義。〈本地分‧思所成地〉卷16，586頁的勝義伽他偈頌說：一切有為法都是剎那生、剎那滅，根本就不能安住，何況能有什麼作用呢？依世俗假說法的生起，假說有此作用，是此作者。然而，單獨只有眼根一法不能看到色塵；單獨只有耳根一法也不能聽聲音；單獨只有鼻根一法不能齅香；單獨只有舌根一法不能嘗味；單獨只有身根一法不能覺觸；單獨只有意根一法不能知法。在見色聞聲乃至了法時，眼等根不能單獨發生作用，也沒有另外的主宰者，驅使眼去見色等。由此可知，以聖人智慧所緣境界的真實義而言，眼根尚且不能見色塵，何況是其他的根呢？因此回答說：一切根都不是有見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以世俗諦而言，只說眼根以有見為境界，眼根稱為一有色，因為它本身也是色法。又於中非有色法，簡取其中一分與眼根同時活動的眼識（意根所攝）等，說名餘非有色一分，也與眼根同在一個境界上活動，所以也稱彼為有見為義。〈思所成慧地〉卷65，2084頁決擇有見諸法的差別中說：眼識所緣的境界，也名為有見法，與眼根同在顯色、形色、表色上活動所以眼識也以有見為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、有對等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科有對等，說明二十二根中屬於有對有質礙的色法，及以有對質礙的色法為境界者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾有對，有對為義？答：七有色及餘無色無對一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些是屬於有對質礙的色法，及以有對質礙的色法為境界？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：眼耳鼻舌身及男女根等七有色根，屬於有對礙的色法，以有對礙的色法為境界；及於無色無對法中，簡取其中一部分的五識（意根所攝）與七色根一起活動時，稱為相屬有對，也以有對礙的色法為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾有對有對為義等者：七有色根是有對，以有對為義。又無色無對法中，簡取一分與七色根俱有轉者，名餘無色無對一分。由與色根俱有而轉，是故亦說有對為義。思所成慧地決擇有對諸法差別，亦說一切皆為依清淨色識所緣故。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/65.htm#45509:51727">陵本六十五卷十頁5181</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼耳鼻舌身與男女根這七色根，是屬於有對有質礙的色法，以有對有質礙的色法為境界。又無色無對法中，簡取與七色根同時活動的識，也是以有對有質礙的色法為境界，稱為餘無色無對一分。由於無色無對法之諸識等與有色根同時活動，所以也說以有對為義。〈思所成慧地〉卷65，2084頁決擇當中說到有對諸法的差別時，也說一切依止清淨色根所產生的五識所緣慮的色境，名有對法。所以說無色無對法一分，與七色根同時活動時，也是以有對質礙的色法為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、有漏有為有諍等3　未一、有漏等2　申一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有漏有為有諍等，說明二十二根中屬於有漏有為有諍法，及分別以有漏有為有諍法等為境界者，分三科；第一科有漏等，說明二十二根中屬於有漏法及以有漏法為境界者，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾有漏，有漏為義？如是等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些是屬於有漏法，以有漏法為境界？如是等，包括其它三個問題是：哪些屬於有漏無漏，以有漏無漏為境界？哪些屬於有漏無漏，以有漏為境界？哪些屬於有漏，以有漏無漏為境界？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、答2　酉一、標差別4　戌一、有漏以有漏為義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標差別，標出四種差別，又分四科；第一科有漏以有漏為義，說明二十二根中哪些是屬於有漏法，以有漏法為境界？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4611"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：唯七。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：唯眼耳鼻舌身男女七色根是有漏法，也是取有漏法為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾有漏有漏為義等者：此中問意，謂幾唯有漏，唯以有漏為義。是故答言：唯七。謂七色根唯是有漏，唯取有漏為境故。於此問中，例後幾學，學為義等問，應置如是等言。以下所答，非唯分別幾有漏，有漏為義故。餘諸問中，隨其所應，例知亦爾，不復重述。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處問題的意思是：二十二根中哪些屬於有漏，而且是以有漏法為境界的呢？回答說：只有七種，唯七色根屬於有漏，也是取有漏法為境界。在此問題當中，還有三個問題沒有提出來，所以一直到問幾學，學為義等，都以「如是等」帶過，後面的問題就省略不說，因此安置「如是等」這句話。因為下面的回答不只包括幾有漏，有漏為義，還包括有漏無漏，以有漏無漏為義；有漏無漏，以有漏為義；有漏，以有漏無漏為義。其餘諸問題中，隨其所相應的，可以有二個、四個乃至很多個問答，來如理思惟，推例到後面，也是如此，則不再重述。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、有漏無漏以有漏無漏為義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有漏無漏以有漏無漏為義，說明二十二根中屬於有漏無漏，以有漏無漏為境界者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">除最後二及苦、憂根，餘有漏、無漏，以有漏、無漏為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了最後的已知根、具知根，這二根全部都是無漏的之外，剩餘的再除去苦根、憂根，苦根及憂根有另外特別的情況；再簡除唯有漏的七色根及假安立的命根，其餘的意根、喜樂捨三受根、信進念定慧五善根及未知欲知根共十根通於有漏、無漏，以有漏、無漏法為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》除最後二及苦憂根等者：此中為顯體通有漏、無漏，通有漏、無漏為義諸所餘根，是故說言除最後二及苦、憂根。由最後二體唯無漏，唯以無漏為義故，及苦、憂根亦非具通二種故，義如下說。當知諸所餘根，謂即意、樂、喜、捨，及信等五、未知欲知根；除七有色、後二無漏，及苦、憂根，名為餘故。命根非有義，此不應說之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處為了顯示哪些根的體性通於有漏法與無漏法，以有漏法、無漏法為境界的諸根。必須除去最後二個無漏的已知根、具知根，因為最後這二根，唯以無漏法為境界；還要除去苦憂根，由於苦根與憂根不是通於有漏無漏的，苦根有漏、無漏，以有漏為義，憂根有漏，以有漏、無漏為義，道理下面還會再說；又除掉有漏的七有色根，總共除掉了十一根。命根是假法，所以不列進去考慮。應當了知其餘諸根是意根、樂根、喜根、捨根，及信等五善根，還有未知欲知根這十根是通於有漏、無漏，又以有漏、無漏的境界。命根是假有，沒有所緣境界，於此處不應當說之。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　上文《披尋記》說最後二體唯無漏，唯以無漏為義故，若根據下文1886頁最後一行說：二不繫，一切繫不繫為義，也就是後二根體唯無漏，以有漏、無漏為義，與《披尋記》此處解釋不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、有漏無漏以有漏為義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科有漏無漏以有漏為義，說明二十二根中屬於有漏無漏，以有漏為境界者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知苦根有漏、無漏，以有漏為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知凡夫的苦根，自性唯是有漏，在阿羅漢身中的苦根通於無漏，合說苦根的自性通有漏無漏，以有漏法為境界。苦根是五識相應受，是果報體所產生的苦受，凡夫身體有病或被外物、或其他有情傷害時，苦受現前，不但有法執，還會對不可意境產生瞋等煩惱，故自性唯是有漏，以有漏法為境界。阿羅漢證有餘依涅槃，前一生有漏業所感得的果報體還在時，身體有病或被外物、或其他有情傷害時，苦受現前，如目犍連尊者被外道打爛身體，苦受還會生起，但是內心已不執取如幻五蘊為我我所，不會生起任何愛見煩惱，故說阿羅漢的苦根通於無漏，以有漏法為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、有漏以有漏無漏為義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科有漏以有漏無漏為義，說明二十二根中屬於有漏，以有漏無漏為境界者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4612"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">憂根有漏，以有漏、無漏為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　與第六意識相應的憂根屬有漏法，以有漏法及無漏法為境界。緣有煩惱境界時能令人心中憂愁，出家人放棄世間的五欲來修行，尚未成就聖道，此時緣聖道無漏法為境界，心裡會有一種出離欲俱行憂，擔心自己什麼時候才能夠證得聖道轉凡成聖，所以說憂根也以無漏法為境界。不過以無漏法為境界所生的出離欲俱行憂，是件好事，能令行者愛惜光陰精進修行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知苦根有漏無漏等者：苦根自性，唯是有漏，無學身起，義通無漏。五識相應，身受攝故，唯以有漏為義。憂根不爾，不在無漏，身起故唯有漏。亦於無上思慕愁慼，求欲證故，通以有漏、無漏為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦根的自性屬於有漏，在無學阿羅漢身上生起時，可以不受身受影響，能以無漏慧面對根，所以說通於無漏。苦根是五識相應的身受所攝，唯以有漏法為境而生。憂根就不是這樣，不會在無漏身上生起，無學身上不會再有憂了，其實三果以上的聖人就沒有憂了。凡夫因為對涅槃或無上菩提聖道的思求愛慕，心裡憂慮愁慼，希望證得涅槃或無上菩提，這是出離欲俱行憂相，是一種善法，所以說憂根通以有漏無漏為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨難釋，隨著比較困難的地方再解釋一下。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未知欲知根，若遠沙門果，世間行所攝，是有漏；若近沙門果，出世行所攝，是無漏。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從初善法欲以去，一直到成就聖道以前，都可以稱為未知欲知根，如果是距沙門果尚遠，包括資糧位及加行位的行者所修的戒定慧，離證果解脫還很遠時，屬於有漏；如果已接近沙門果，出世聖道所攝，如見道十五心時，是屬於無漏的範圍。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、有為等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有為等，說明二十二根中屬於有為法，以有為法為境界者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾有為，有為為義？如是等。答：一切是有為。八有為為義，餘有為、無為為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些屬於有為法，以有為法為境界？如是等，若依前推理應當還有三個問題，舉一句就可以了解二種狀況，所以不再多說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：一切二十二根都是有為。其中眼耳鼻舌身男女的七色根及苦根，這八根都是以有為法為境界；其餘非色根，包括意根，還有樂喜憂捨，五善根，與三無漏根，這十三個根是以有為、無為為境界。〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1842頁說：「從因已生及應生義名有為。」從種子生現行，及有所造作而熏習成種子，現在雖然還沒有現行，將來因緣具足一定會現行，也屬於有為法，命根是假法，屬不相應行法，也可以攝在有為裡面，所以說二十二根都是有為法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》八有為為義者：謂七色根及與苦根應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七色根及與苦根，是以有為法為境界應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、有諍等2　申一、舉有諍</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科有諍等，說明二十二根中屬於有諍等，以有諍等為境界者，分二科；第一科舉有諍，舉有諍為例。</span></span></span></div>
