<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾有諍，有諍為義？如是等。答：如說有漏，當知此亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些屬於有諍法，以有諍法為境界？能夠引起有情瞋心的，都可以屬於有諍。如是等類。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：如說有漏法，有四種情況，有諍也與有漏法同樣的道理，就不再說了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4613"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、例有愛味等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例有愛味等，以有諍為例，其他還有二十四種解釋，包括有愛味等道理也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如說有諍，當知有愛味、依耽嗜、世間、出世間等亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如說有諍法與有漏法同樣的道理，應知有愛味、依耽嗜、世間、出世間等依理類推，也是一樣，都可以比照安立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、過去現在未來3　未一、在過去過去為義2　申一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科過去現在未來，說明二十二根中屬於過去現在未來，以過去現在未來為境界者，分三科；第一科在過去過去為義，先說二十二根中屬於過去，以過去境界者，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾過去，過去為義？如是等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根哪些是過去，以過去為境界？如是等類，還可以再詳細思惟其他各種問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、答2　酉一、過去為義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科過去為義，說明屬於過去，以過去為境界者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：除有色根及苦根，餘有義一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：除掉七有色根與苦根，剎那生滅，屬於過去，七有色根與苦身根只能取現在境，不是以過去為境界；除去假法的命根，其餘有十三個非有色根，就是意根、樂喜憂捨根、五善根及三無漏根，這十三個非有色根是心心所法，可以緣過去、現在、未來三時境。現在所說是屬於過去，以過去為境界的，只是這十三根中，以三時中過去為境的這一分。五受根中唯苦根體是以有漏有為為境，其餘四受根可以與意識相應，以有漏無漏、有為無為為境。當意識以無漏無為為境時，唯苦根不與相應，因此將苦根與性質相同以有漏有為為境之七有色根合說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷15中有人問：為何根境同在現在能夠緣境，根住現在境先入過去嗎？窺基大師說：現在色塵先入過去，未來眼根入於現在。現在眼根入過去已，不能緣過去，又現在無識之根與色俱入過去，不能緣過去境。故七有色根及苦根，只能取現在境，不是以過去為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、非過去為義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科非過去為義，說明屬於過去，不是以過去境界者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有色根及苦根在過去，非過去為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中七有色根，還有苦根剎那滅已名為在過去，只能取現在境，不是以過去為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾過去過去為義等者：此中問意，謂有幾根體在過去，以過去為義。七有色根及與苦根剎那滅已，名在過去。然非過去為義，以彼行境唯現在故，是故除之。所餘非色意相應法，於去來今通緣三世，今說彼在過去，過去為義，名餘有義一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是在問二十二根中有幾根的體性已經過去，已經受用過因果了，而且以過去為它的境界呢？七有色根的眼耳鼻舌身男女根，還有苦根，剎那生、剎那滅，剎那滅以後，就是過去，但不是以過去為境，因為七有色根與苦身根活動的境界，只能緣取現在境，所以將它除去。命根是假法不算在內，所餘不屬色法與第六意識、意根相應的五善根、四受根及三無漏根等十三根，可以通緣過去、未來、現在三世境，現在色塵先入過去，未來意根入於現在，現在意根能緣過去，不同前面七色根及苦根已入過去，未來眼根入於現在，只能緣現在境，不能緣過去境，故與第六意識、意根相應的五善根、四受根及三無漏根等，是此處所說的根是已過去，又能夠以過去為境界，就是這裡所說的餘有義一分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、在過去現在為義等2　申一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科在過去現在為義等，說明二十二根屬於過去，能以現在為境界，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4614"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾過去，現在為義？如是等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些流落到過去，屬於過去，能以現在為境界？如是等類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、答2　酉一、指前說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科指前說，指前文所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：即如所說一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：就如前文所說除七有色根及苦根，除命根是假法不算在內，所餘不屬色法與第六意識、意根相應的信等五善根、樂喜憂捨四受根及三無漏根，流落到過去，屬於過去，因為意識可以通緣過去、未來、現在三世境，這裡所說的一分是能以現在為境界的這一分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》即如所說一分者：謂如前說除有色根及苦根，餘有義一分當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前文所說除七有色根及苦根，餘有義一分，即意根、信等五善根、樂喜憂捨四受根及三無漏根等十三根，如前解釋應當知道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、例當知</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例當知，以前文所說推理即可了知其他狀況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知即此在過去，以未來為義。又即此在現在，以過去、未來為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知，就是與意識、意根相應的樂喜憂捨四受根、信等五善根、三無漏根等十三根，體性是在過去，而以未來為境界，道理也是一樣。又這些與意識、意根相應的樂喜憂捨四受根，信等五善根、三無漏根等十三根，體性是在現在，能以過去、未來為境界。唯識學說，過、未不真實，現在才是真實。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》的解釋緣於過去，是指根在現在緣慮過去，稱為在過去。由於有色根本身不可能緣慮過去，所以說七色根跟苦根，就不能以過去為境界。這裡要強調的是七色根只能緣現在境；而意根是以過去、現在、未來為境界，因此與第六意識、意根相應的信等五善根、樂喜憂捨四受根及三無漏根可以是在過去，以過去為境的這一分；在過去，以現在為境的這一分；在過去，以未來為境的這一分；在現在，以過去、未來為境。由此簡別出七色根及苦根這八根與意根相應的只有以現在法為義，有這樣的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知即此在過去等者：謂如前說，一分在過去，亦以未來為義。此并前說在過去，過去為義；在過去，現在為義；當知非有色根於過去世三世為義可得。如是於現未世，當知亦爾，如下自說。即此在現在，以過去、未來為義，亦以現在為義。又在未來，以過去、未來為義，亦以現在為義。又在未來，以過去、未來、現在為義。總略而言，非有色根於去來今通緣三世，非七色根及與苦根。由七色根唯取現境；及彼苦根唯與五識相應，亦取現境故；不應說過去、未來為義。於三世分別中，唯許現在為義，如下自說應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前文已說，與意根相應的非有色根於過去，以未來為境界為一分，加上前面說的在過去，以過去為境界為一分；在過去，以現在為境界的一分；當知非有色根在過去時，能夠以過去、現在、未來三世為境界。如是在現在世或在未來世都是一樣，下面還會再說。這些與意根相應之非有色根，在現在能夠以過去、未來為境界，也能夠以現在為境界。如果是在未來，也可以以過去與未來，還有現在的法為境界。總體概要來說，非有色根這些法，不論是在過去、現在、或未來，都能夠緣慮過去、現在、未來三世的法。但是通緣三世不是七色根的眼耳鼻舌身、男女根與苦根的境界，因為這七色根只能取得現在的境界。苦根一定只是與眼耳鼻舌身五識相應，也是只取現在的境界。所以苦根與七色根，都不能說以過去、未來為境界，在過去、現在、未來三世中，只能准許以現在為境，如下文所說可以了解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、在現在現在為義等2　申一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科在現在現在為義等，說明二十二根中在現在，以現在為境界，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾現在，現在為義？如是等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些是屬於在現在，以現在為境界呢？如是等，下面就不再多說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4615"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、答2　酉一、明現在</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明現在，說明現在。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：一切有色根及苦根，并前所說一分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：一切有色根及苦根，還有前面所說的與意根相應之非有色根一分，都可以說是在現在，以現在為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、例未來2　戌一、約無色諸根辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例未來，以現在為例，未來也是一樣，分二科；第一科約無色諸根辨，先說無色諸根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此一分在未來，以過去、未來、現在為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又此與意根相應之非有色根，如果在未來將會現起時，能夠以過去、未來、現在為境界。文非常詳細說這件事情，其實只有一個道理。就是非色的意等根在三世可以緣三世義，不論是過去、現在、未來的情況都能夠緣過去、現在、未來。這七色根與苦根，只能於現在以現在為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、約有色及苦根辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約有色及苦根辨，其次以有色根與苦根來說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸色根在未來，非未來為義。苦根亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七色根如果在未來才會現行，也不能以未來為境界，苦根也是一樣。其實唯識學都是站在現在說的，一般人的想法就將它跳過去說，在現在現在為義，應該也可以在過去過去為義，因為過去與過去，就是現在與現在，一樣的意思。可是這裡不是這個意思。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》解釋緣於過去，稱為在過去；根緣過去、現在或未來，稱為在過去、在現在、或在未來。它的重點在以後面來解釋前面，若就過去、現在或未來為義而言，唯與意根相應之非有色根一分，七色根與苦根只能在現在、以現在為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、三界繫及不繫2　未一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科三界繫及不繫，說明二十二根中三界繫及不繫，以三界繫及不繫為境界等，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾欲界繫，欲界繫為義？如是等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些是屬於欲界繫，而且以繫屬於欲界的法為境界？如是等類，省略不再說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、答7　申一、苦憂男女四根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分成七個部分，現在只有問一個問題，如是等下面還有六個問題沒有提出來，不過文都回答出來了，分七科；第一科苦憂男女四根，說明苦根、憂根、男根與女根，這四根是欲界繫，而且以欲界繫為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：四。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有四個；苦根、憂根、男根與女根這四根繫屬於欲界，也是以欲界的色聲香味觸為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4616"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、鼻舌二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科鼻舌二根，說明鼻舌二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二，欲、色界繫，欲界繫為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二問題是：二十二根中哪些是通於欲界的眾生及色界的眾生，也是以欲界繫為它的境界的呢？答：鼻根與舌根這二根，欲界有情與色界有情都有，只有欲界有情是以欲界的香與味為境界，色界天人雖然有鼻根與舌根，不過他們不用的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、眼耳身三根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科眼耳身三根，說明眼耳身三根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三，欲、色界繫，欲、色界繫為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三個問題是：二十二根中哪些是欲界與色界有情都有，而且在欲界與色界都能夠有作用，以欲色界繫為境界呢？答：眼、耳、身這三根，欲界與色界有情都有，《八識規矩頌》說：眼耳身三二地居。在五趣雜居地、離生喜樂地，這二地的有情都有眼、耳、身三根，也都有作用。色界天人五根具足，但唯有初禪離生喜樂，眼、耳、身三根才有作用，二禪以上都是意識相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、喜樂二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科喜樂二根， 說明喜樂二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二，欲、色界繫及不繫，欲、色、無色界繫及不繫為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四問題是：二十二根中哪些屬於欲、色界繫、及不繫屬於三界，以欲、色、無色界繫及不繫為境界？答：喜根與樂根，欲界的有情也有，色界初禪、二禪、三禪的有情也有，無漏聖道相應時也有喜根與樂根，能夠以欲界、色界、無色界，還有不繫為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申五、信等五及意捨七根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科信等五及意捨七根，說明信等五善根及意捨七根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七，欲、色、無色界繫及不繫，彼義亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五個問題是：二十二根中哪些屬欲、色、無色界繫、及不繫，以欲、色、無色界繫、及不繫為境界？答：信等五善根及意、捨，這七根屬欲、色、無色界繫，能夠以欲、色、無色界繫及不繫為境界。前文說喜與樂，屬欲、色界繫，捨根的範圍包括最廣，因為無色界有情尚未出離捨根（意識相應捨受），所以說無色界眾生也有捨根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申六、未知欲知根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科未知欲知根，說明未知欲知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一，色界繫及不繫，一切繫不繫為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六個問題是：二十二根中哪些屬於色界繫及不繫，一切繫不繫為境呢？答：前文說修諦現觀者從善法欲已去名未知欲知根，這是通取遠近方便說。從發善法欲順解脫分的行者就有未知欲知根，此處就近方便順決擇分以後說，修諦現觀者入順決擇分時，至少有未到地定才能引發無漏聖慧，所以說未知欲知根屬色界繫及不繫，能以一切繫不繫為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　關於未到地定是屬於哪一界地？若大乘，初禪未至定，即屬初禪攝，乃至上地皆然。若成實論師，是經部師宗，主張：初禪未至，即欲界攝，第二禪未至，即初禪攝，乃至已上地皆然。大乘小乘法等對論說：初禪未至定，能離欲界染，上地斷下地染法。既汝初禪未至，即欲界攝，如何欲界自地法，能離欲界自地染？故知不是。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4617"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申七、已知具知二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科已知具知二根，說明已知根與具知根這二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二，不繫，一切繫不繫為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七個問題是：二十二根中哪些屬於不繫，一切繫不繫為境呢？答：已知根與具知根二根屬於無漏法，能以三界繫及不繫為境界。初果以上的有學聖人及初地以上的諸菩薩有已知根，阿羅漢或佛有具知根，可以緣於三界有漏的境界，也可以緣於無漏的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾欲界繫欲界繫為義等者：男、女、苦、憂四根，欲界繫，欲界繫為義。鼻、舌二根，欲、色界繫，欲界繫為義。眼、耳、身三，欲、色界繫，欲、色界繫為義。喜、樂二根，欲、色界繫及不繫，欲、色、無色界繫及不繫為義。信等五根、意根、捨根，如是七根，欲、色、無色界繫及不繫，亦以欲、色、無色界繫及不繫為義。初一無漏根，色界繫及不繫，一切繫不繫為義。後二無漏不繫，一切繫不繫為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　男、女、苦、憂四根，是欲界繫，以欲界繫為境，這是第一個答案；第二個答案是鼻、舌二根屬於欲界、色界繫，以欲界為境界；第三個答案是眼、耳、身三根屬於欲界、色界繫，是以欲、色界繫為境界；第四個答案是喜、樂二根是屬於欲界、色界繫及不繫，是以欲界、色界、無色界繫及不繫為境界；第五個答案是信進念定慧五善根及意根、捨根，這七根屬於三界繫及不繫，所緣境也通於三界繫與不繫；第六個答案是未知欲知根屬於色界繫與不繫，以一切三界繫與不繫為境界；第七個答案是最後二無漏根，已知根與具知根屬於無漏法，體性是不繫，以三界繫及不繫為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《品類足論》卷6，7頁說：不繫法云何？謂一切無漏法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午五、善不善無記2　未一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科善不善無記，說明二十二根中屬於善法、不善法、與無記法，以善法、不善法、與無記法為境界等差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾善，善為義？如是等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些屬於善法，以善法為境界？如是等類，下面就省略不問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、答5　申一、信等五及三無漏八根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分五科；第一科信等五及三無漏八根，說明信等五善根及未知欲知根、已知根、與具知根八根以善、不善、無記為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：八，唯善，善、不善、無記為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：信等五善根及未知欲知根、已知根與具知根這八根唯屬善法，以善、不善、或是無記三性為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、苦樂喜捨及意五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科苦樂喜捨及意五根，說明苦樂喜捨及意五根以善、不善、無記為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五，善、不善、無記，善、不善、無記為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦樂喜捨及意這五根通於善、不善、無記三性，也以三性法為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、憂根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科憂根，說明憂根以善、不善、無記為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一，善、不善，善、不善、無記為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　憂根一根通於善、不善，沒有無記，以善、不善、無記為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4618"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、鼻舌身男女五根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科鼻舌身男女五根，說明此五根以無記為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">五，無記，無記為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　鼻舌身男女這五根是無記，而且以無記為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申五、眼耳二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科眼耳二根，說明眼耳二根以善、不善、無記為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二，無記，善、不善、無記為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼根與耳根二根屬於無記，以善、不善、無記三性為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　據《瑜伽論記》卷16，窺基大師說：這是根據表業假法而言。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾善善為義等者：信等五根、三無漏根，如是八根唯善，善、不善、無記為義。苦、樂、喜、捨及意五根，善、不善、無記，善、不善、無記為義。憂受一根唯善、不善，不通無記，善、不善、無記為義。鼻、舌、身、男、女五根無記，無記為義。眼、耳二根無記，善、不善、無記為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　信等五根、三無漏根，這八根全部都是純善，屬於善法，不論是世間清淨或出世間清淨都有，以善、不善、無記為境界；苦、樂、喜、捨及意五根通善、不善、無記三性，以善、不善、無記三性為境界；憂受一根只有通於善與不善，不通無記，但是也是以三性為境界；鼻、舌、身、男、女五根屬於無記，以無記為境界；眼、耳二根是無記，無記是根據表業來說的，表業是假法，是心動了，然後才眼見耳聞，所以說是無記，眼耳通於善、不善、無記三性為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午六、學無學非學非無學2　未一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科學無學非學非無學，說明二十二根中屬於學、無學、非學非無學，以學、無學、非學非無學為境界等差別。〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1844頁中說，學是方便善義，無學是究竟善義，非學非無學是離前二種所有善、染汙、無記法，分二科；第一科問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾學，學為義？如是等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些屬於有學，以有學為境界呢？如是等類，底下很多的問題省略，以回答方式反顯可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、答6　申一、意喜樂捨及信等五九根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分六科；第一科意喜樂捨及信等五九根，說明意、喜樂捨三受及信等五善根，總共有九根，以三種為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：九，學、無學、非學非無學，以三種為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：意、喜樂捨三受根及信等五善根，共有九根屬於學、無學、非學非無學，以此三種為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4619"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、眼等七色根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科眼等七色根，說明眼耳鼻舌身及男女根等七色根，以非學非無學為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七，非學非無學，即以此為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼耳鼻舌身及男女根等七色根屬於非學非無學，也是以非學非無學為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、苦根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科苦根，說明苦根以非學非無學為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一，通三種，非學非無學為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦根通於有學、無學、非學非無學，因為唯凡夫會因苦根而生貪瞋癡，聖人則不會再因苦根而生貪瞋癡，因此苦根以非學非無學為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、憂根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科憂根，說明憂根，以三種為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一，學、非學非無學，以三種為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　憂根通於有學、非學非無學，以有學、無學、還有非學非無學三種為境界。初、二果的有學聖者的憂根是指出離欲具行憂，擔憂自己不能證得涅槃，所以說憂根通於有學及凡夫以三種為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申五、未知已知二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科未知已知二根，說明未知、已知二無漏根，以三種為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二，學，以三種為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　未知欲知根、已知根這二個無漏根屬於有學，以有學、無學、還有非學非無學三種為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申六、具知根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科具知根，說明具知根，以三種為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一，無學，以三種為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　具知根是無學，以有學、無學、和非學非無學三種為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4620"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾學學為義等者：意、喜、樂、捨，及信等五，如是九根，學、無學、非學非無學，以三種為義。七有色根，非學非無學，即以此為義。苦受一根，通學、無學、非學非無學，非學非無學為義。憂受一根，學、非學非無學，以三種為義。初二無漏是學，以三種為義。後一無漏是無學，以三種為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　意根、喜根、樂根、捨根，還有信進念定慧，這九根是通於有學、無學、非學非無學，而且以三種學為境界；眼耳鼻舌身、男女這七色根，屬於非學非無學，也以非學非無學為境界；苦受一根與五識相應，通於有學、無學、和非學非無學，都是以非學非無學為境界；憂受一根，通於有學與非學非無學，以三種學為境界；初二無漏就是未知欲知根及已知根是有學，以三種學為境界；後一無漏具知根是無學，以三種學為境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午七、見斷修斷非斷2　未一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科見斷修斷非斷，以下是三斷門，說明二十二根中屬於見斷、修斷、非斷，以見斷、修斷、非斷為境界的差別相，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾見所斷，見所斷為義？如是等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些屬於見道所斷，而且是以見道所斷為境界呢？如是等類，底下很多的問題省略，以回答方式反顯可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、答2　申一、標差別3　酉一、七色五受及命意十四根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標差別，標出種種差別，又分三科；第一科七色五受及命意十四根，說明七色根、五受根，還有命根與意根，這十四根一分見所斷，一分修所斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：十四，一分見所斷，一分修所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：七色根、五受根、命根及意根，這十四根一部分是屬於見道位所斷除；一部分是修道位所斷除。七色根與命根，如果是惡趣根是見道位所斷除的，因為見道位以上就不到三惡道去了；如果是善趣根是修道位要斷，修道位要入無餘依涅槃才究竟圓滿，所以即使生到人天善趣也應該斷除。五受根苦樂憂喜捨及意根，如果是惡趣因，或是惡趣果，也是見道位所斷的，善趣因或善趣果，就是修道位所斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、五受意信等五未知欲知十二根2　戌一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科五受意信等五未知欲知十二根，說明五受根、意根，信進念定慧五善根與未知欲知根十二根，一分修所斷，一分非所斷，分二科；第一科標，先標出來整個意思。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">十二，一分修所斷，一分非所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有十二根一部分是修道要斷除，一部分是不再需要斷除的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋十二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂即十四中六及餘六。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　即前十四根中的意根及五受根，以及其餘的六根，就是信等五善根，還有初無漏未知欲知根，合有十二根一部分是修道要斷除，一部分是不再需要斷除的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、已知具知二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科已知具知二根，說明已知根和具知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4621"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">餘二非所斷。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　餘二的已知根與具知根，初果以上的已知根，還有阿羅漢的具知根，都屬於非所斷的範圍。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋略義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋略義，要略的解釋其中的義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中有色諸根，見、修所斷為義；無色諸根，三種為義，謂見、修所斷，非所斷義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這當中有色諸根是通於見道位和修道位所應該斷除的境界；無色諸根，通於見道、修道，還有非所斷。有色諸根若惡趣根是見道位所斷，若善趣根是修道位所斷；無色諸根中五受根的苦根，如果是惡趣苦根是見道所斷，善趣苦根是修道所斷；無學身中的苦根是非所斷；不善憂根與見惑相應是見所斷，善憂根與修惑相應是修所斷；喜樂捨根與意根，與見惑相應是見所斷，與修惑相應就是修所斷；信進念定慧五根與未知欲知根，有漏的是修所斷，無漏的就是非所斷，已知根與具知根都是非所斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾見所斷見所斷為義等者：七有色根、意根、命根，及五受根，如是十四，一分見所斷，一分修所斷。即十四中，意及五受六根，并餘信等五根及初無漏，如是十二，一分修所斷，一分非所斷。後二無漏唯非所斷。為義差別，如文易知。於為義中，應不說有命根，以彼命根非有義故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七色根、五受根、命根及意根，這十四根中有一部分屬於見所斷，一部分屬於修所斷。其中七色根與命根，一分惡趣根是見所斷，一分善趣根是修所斷。五受根與意根，惡趣苦根是見所斷，善趣苦根是修所斷。十四根中的意根及五受根，這六根加上信進念定慧五根，與最初的未知欲知根，總共有十二根，有一部分是修道位要斷除的，一部分是非所斷，是不必斷除的。已知根與具知根，是屬於非所斷的範圍。為見、修或非所斷的境界，有種種的差別，如文很容易就明白了。於有境界當中，不應該說有命根，因為命根是假有法，是前生的業力所招感的異熟住時壽量，沒有所取的境界差別，所以命根不在討論的範圍。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、約斷知辨3　午一、雜染捨所顯</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約斷知辨，知道觀察雜染的過失，才能斷除雜染，說明二十二根中雜染捨所顯、顛倒差別及觀察義過失等，分三科；第一科雜染捨所顯，說明二十二根中屬於應捨之雜染。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根於義雜染捨所顯？答：除諸善根，以諸善根於義清淨捨所顯故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：說明二十二根中哪些於境界雜染捨所顯？雜染的意思就是不清淨。雜染不淨是要將它捨除、捨棄的，是所應棄捨的對象。雜染共有三種，包括煩惱雜染、業雜染、與生雜染。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：除信進念定慧五善根及三無漏根，這些善根是屬於清淨的境界，能夠捨除雜染，而且能夠對治雜染。除掉這八善根，還有十四個屬於雜染捨所顯，包括眼耳鼻舌身五根及意根六根、男女根、五受根及命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》除諸善根者：除信等五及三無漏應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除諸善根，是指除了清淨的信等五善根及三無漏根應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顛倒差別攝4　未一、顛倒義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顛倒差別攝，說明二十二根種種顛倒差別所攝，分四科；第一科顛倒義，說明顛倒的境界。顛倒是碰到境界時，生出常樂我淨或貪瞋癡等染著心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根顛倒義？答：除諸善根，所有六根義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些能於境界生起顛倒，屬顛倒的境界所攝呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：除了上面所說的這八種善根以外，意根與五受根這六根，能於境界生起貪瞋癡等染著心。意根與五受根也可能與善根相應，除掉與八種善根相應的意根與五受根之外，一分不與善根相應的就是顛倒的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》除諸善根所有六根義者：此中六根，謂意、五受應知。由除善根相應一分，是故說彼顛倒為義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說的六根，是指意根與五受根，除掉與八種善根相應時外，其他時候於境界不應貪而貪，不應瞋而瞋與顛倒相應，稱為顛倒為義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4622"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、顛倒所依</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顛倒所依，說明生起顛倒的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根顛倒所依？答：七色根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些是生起顛倒的依止處？答：眼耳鼻舌身及男女二根，是生起顛倒的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、顛倒自性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顛倒自性， 說明顛倒的自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根顛倒自性？答：六少分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些是顛倒的自性？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：意根與五受根除掉與八種善根相應外，這六根少分與貪瞋癡等雜染相應時，名顛倒自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》六少分者：謂除善根相應意及五受一分應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六少分是指除與善根相應外，意根與五受根一分與貪瞋癡等雜染相應時，就屬於顛倒自性，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、顛倒對治</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科顛倒對治，說明能對治顛倒之善根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根顛倒對治？答：八根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中哪些能對治顛倒？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：信等五善根及三無漏根八根能對治顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾根顛倒對治等者：謂信等五及三無漏，如是八根，能為一切顛倒對治應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　信等五及三無漏，這八根能對治一切顛倒，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、觀察義過失2　未一、略標舉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科觀察義過失，說明二十二根中哪些能觀察一切有為法的境界有過失，生起厭離心，分二科；第一科略標舉，要略的標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根觀義過失？答：或八、或五、或一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中，哪些能觀察一切有為法的境界有過失，而生起厭離心？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：假法與實法通論的話，或八是指信等五善根及三無漏根；或五是就實法為論，指信等五善根；或意根一根是就勝為論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4623"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或八或五或一者：謂信等五及三無漏，是名或八。唯信等五，是名或五。唯取意根，是名或一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　假法與實法通論的話，信進念定慧與三無漏根，能夠使令有情在心裡厭離這一切有為法，是名或八。就實法來說只有信進念定慧這五善根，是名或五。或一是意根，因為意根最強，修行要從意根下手，依意根生意識，能觀察一切有為法的境界有過失而生起厭離心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、釋妨難4　申一、舉難問4　酉一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋妨難，解釋外道的妨礙難問，分四科；第一科舉難問，舉出外道的難問（外道對佛教的說法有一些微詞），又分四科；第一科標，標示出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若彼諸行亦有四德相應可得，云何唯觀為過失耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果遷流不息的有為法，有四種殊勝的德行相應，不應該說有為法都是有過失，應該也有好處與功德，為什麼只有觀全部都是過失呢？所謂的功德，是指常樂我淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若彼諸行亦有四德相應等者：此中四德，如次配屬常、樂、我、淨應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這個四種殊勝的功德，如其次第配屬常樂我淨，應當了知，常樂我淨稱為四德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何者四德？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪四德？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、堅住德；謂如一蘊住經百年，若正將御，或有過者。二、勢力德；謂能生樂，及現清淨。三、轉變德；謂牽引、修治、受用、棄捨自在轉故。四、可樂德；謂依彼處生種種著故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、堅住德，是常德。外道這樣認為，譬如說色蘊，好好照顧身體，每天注意飲食、運動等，可以安住經百年之久，才滅壞御除，甚至超過百年，這就是堅住，佛法怎麼說是無常的呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、勢力德，是執著有樂德。外道執著色受想行識如果緣取好的色聲香味觸，也能夠產生快樂，這種樂受在現法裡面就是一種清淨，認為有為法也是有樂，有使令快樂的勢力功德。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、轉變德，就是執著有「我」德，外道執著有「我」牽引這個身體，牽引自己的心去造作種種的業，可以修治身與心：保養自己的身體、修禪定使令心裡快樂，修治以後，可以受用快樂的境界，受用完以後，也可以棄捨掉，可以自在運轉，就是執著有「我」，認為「我」是可以轉變身心，有為法也有可以自在運轉的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、可樂德，執著所依境界清淨有淨德。依止各式各樣的境界，產生種種相似清淨快樂的感受，或認為禪定就是清淨的，認為有為法的另外一種功德，稱為可樂德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結說外道計著諸行有四德相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名諸行有四德相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這就是外道計著這一切有為法，也有四種功德的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》牽引修治等者：謂於諸行計我自在。能牽引彼，或復修治，能受用彼，或復棄捨，隨欲轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於這一切有為法，外道計著有我能在自在運轉，能牽引身心，或修治身心，也能受用身心，不要也可以棄捨，能隨我內心的欲望，想要怎麼樣就怎麼樣，佛法怎麼會觀察有過失呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4624"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋義答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋義答，解釋觀察諸行過失的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：雖有世間於彼諸法取為功德，然彼一切皆諸過失之所隨逐。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：雖然有世間的人，對一切有為法認為有功德，可是一切有為法，都有種種的過失所隨逐。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、更徵問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科更徵問，再細問過失義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何等名為諸過失耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪些法名為種種的過失呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、別辨答2　酉一、辨4　戌一、無堅住德</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科別辨答，各別辨明回答，分二科；第一科辨，說明，又分四科；第一科無堅住德，佛法主張一切有為法沒有堅住的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：雖少時住，非究竟故，愛變無常現可得故，死沒無常現可得故，當觀諸行離初功德。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：雖然這一切有為法雖有少時間可以安住，但不是究竟可以安住，總是要死，活到一百歲也要死。有人說彭祖活到八百歲，也是要死。可愛的事物很快的就變化、就無常了，現前都可以觀察得到。死的無常，也都很容易可以觀察得到，所以不論是愛變無常或死沒無常，由種種的無常，可以知道這一切有為法是沒有堅住功德的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》愛變無常現可得故者：聲聞地說，內事變異有多差別，或有顯色所作變異，或有形色所作變異。顯色所作變異者，謂自或他，先有妙色，肌膚鮮澤；後見惡色，肌膚枯槁。形色所作變異者，謂如顯色前後變異無常，如是形色由肥瘦故，應知亦爾。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/34.htm#45667:27528">陵本三十四卷四頁2743</a>）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈聲聞地〉卷34，1094頁說，根身內事有種種的變化差異，或有青黃赤白等顯色所作變異，或有長短方圓等形色所作變異。顯色所作變異，是指自己或他人，原先妙色端嚴，肌膚鮮白潤澤，後來或因病因老而轉成惡色，肌膚變成枯黃憔瘁。形色所作變異，是指如自己或他人，顯色前後變異無常，有時候原本高挑挺直的身形，也會產生變異，變成彎腰駝背、腦滿腸肥或瘦骨嶙峋的樣子，道理也是一樣。由此說有為法性不堅住，如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷34，1089~1103頁說十種無常行，應可了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、無勢力德</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無勢力德，有為法並沒有令有情快樂的勢力功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又能發生種種苦惱現可得故，種種不淨現可得故，當觀諸行離第二德。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這一切有為法，能夠使令發生種種的苦惱與種種不淨，現前可得故，並沒有外道所說的勢力德，不能令有情常常快樂，而是常常令生起苦惱，常常不淨。由此應當觀察有為法，沒有第二種令有情快樂的勢力功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、無轉變德</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無轉變德，有為法沒有自在轉變的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於老病死等不隨所欲現可得故，當觀諸行離第三德。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在《志公禪師勸世念佛文》中說：生老病死苦，為人哪個無。這世上沒有人喜歡老病死苦，可是誰也不能避免這種苦，有為法遷流不息，逼得人不得不老病死，不能隨心所欲，這是眼睜睜的事實，應當觀察有為法沒有自在轉變的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4625"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、無可樂德</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無可樂德，有為法沒有清淨可令人樂著的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸糞蟲及豬犬等亦極樂著糞穢不淨現可得故，當觀諸行離第四德。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這個譬喻很實際，人就像糞裡面的蟲，還有豬與狗這些畜牲，也是很歡喜糞穢、不清淨的境界，現前就可以觀察得到。應當以此方法來觀察一切有為法都是不清淨的，沒有外道所執著的清淨可令人貪樂耽著的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結說有為法只有過失，沒有四種功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由彼諸行離諸功德，是故一切過失相應，故應觀彼具諸過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於這一切有為法遠離四種功德，與一切過失相應，應該觀察它具足種種的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、依處差別3　辰一、明為依13　巳一、眼根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依處差別，分三科；第一科明為依，說明二十二根為其他法的所依，又分十三科；第一科眼根，說明眼根為見色依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：眼根誰所依處？答：見色依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：眼根是誰的依止處？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：眼根是見色的依止處。所依根、所緣境、空間、光明、種子、作意、分別依、染淨依、根本依，此九緣具足時，眼識依止眼根能了別色塵，所以說眼根是眼識見色的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、耳鼻舌身意根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科耳鼻舌身意根，其他耳鼻舌身意根也是一樣，能夠為聞聲、嗅香、嚐味、覺觸、知法等的依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：乃至意根誰所依處？答：各取自境之所依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：耳鼻舌身乃至意根是誰的所依處呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：各別取相對應的自境之所依處。耳根為耳識聞聲的依止處，鼻根是鼻識嗅香的止依處，舌根是舌識嚐味的依止處，身根是身識觸境的依止處，意根是意識知法的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、男女二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科男女二根，說明男女二根為習欲依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：男女二根誰所依處？答：習欲依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：男女二根是誰的所依處？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：男女二根是世間人習近男女欲的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、命根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科命根，說明命根為生有與本有的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4626"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：命根誰所依處？答：乃至死有，為前時有之所依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：命根是誰的依處呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：命根是死有之前，生有與本有的依止處。剛投生時那一剎那是生有，生有以後的第二剎那一直到死有以前是本有，正在死時，這時的五蘊稱作死有。因此命根是死有之前，生有與本有的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》為前時有之所依處者：死有以前，本有乃至生有，名前時有應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知死有以前的本有，以及生有，稱為前時有。投胎那一剎那是生有，從投胎的第二剎那以後都是本有，生有與本有都是依止命根而有的，如果沒有命根，五蘊就就不能存活。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、五受根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科五受根，說明五受根是於可意、不可意的境界，若愛、若恚等的所依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸受根誰所依處？答：於諸境界可意、不可意，若愛、若恚等之所依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：五受根是誰所依處？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：五受根是對於境界可意或不可意，產生貪愛或瞋恚的依止處。一般沒有修行的人於可意境，容易生起喜樂二受，而引發內心的貪愛；於不可意境，容易生起苦憂二受，而引發內心的瞋恚；遍於苦樂憂喜時都有捨受，因此說五受根是於諸境界可意、不可意，若愛、若恚等之所依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳六、信根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科信根，說明信根是趣入善法之所依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：信根誰所依處？答：趣入善法之所依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：信根是誰的所依處？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：信根是趣入善法的依止處。《大乘起信論義疏》卷1說：「若有信人，入佛法寶，隨分修行得解脫樂。若無信人，雖遇佛法，空無所獲。」信為道源功德本，有信才能夠趣入善法，所以說信是趣入善法之所依處。我們能夠修學善法也是因為對於佛法有信心，對於善法有信心，才能夠修學善法。信很重要，一直到成就聖人以上才能夠得到四證淨（四不壞信），是永遠不會退轉的清淨信心，大乘菩薩稱為清淨增上意樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳七、精進根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科精進根，說明精進根是恆常修習善法之所依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：精進根誰所依處？答：已入善法，恆常修習之所依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：精進根是誰的依止處？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：要進入佛法的大門先要有信，信了以後，才能契入善法，以後還要恆常精進修習，所以說精進根是恆常修習善法的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳八、念根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科念根，明記是念，修學佛法明記不忘很重要，說明念根是正知而行之所依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：念根誰所依處？答：正知而行之所依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：念根是誰的依止處？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：念根是正知而行的依止處。對身語意三業正在作什麼，都能夠明明白白、正確的了知，要有明記不忘的念力。如果懈怠忘聖言，就不能正知而行。佛很久以前作的事情、說過的話，想過的念頭永遠都記得。凡夫很快就忘記，這是由於念力還不夠。如果常常有正念的人，會記得什麼時間作過什麼事情，隨時都知道，隨時都能夠安住在當下，這都是念根的力量。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4627"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳九、定根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科定根，說明定根是智見清淨之所依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：定根誰所依處？答：智見清淨之所依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：定根是誰的依止處？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：定根是明白過去、未來、現在諸法實相的智見清淨的依止處。《大智度論》卷17〈1 序品〉說：「常樂涅槃從實智慧生，實智慧從一心禪定生。譬如燃燈，燈雖能照，在大風中不能為用；若置之密室，其用乃全。散心中智慧亦如是，若無禪定靜室，雖有智慧，其用不全；得禪定則實智慧生。」又〈本地分‧修所成地〉卷20說：「定心中慧於所知境清淨轉故。」依止禪定修毗鉢舍那能引發無漏智見，令智見清淨，因此定根是智見清淨的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十、慧根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科慧根，說明慧根是煩惱永斷之所依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：慧根誰所依處？答：煩惱永斷之所依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：慧根是誰的所依處？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：慧根是永斷煩惱的依止處。若只有定不能斷煩惱，要有智慧才能夠斷煩惱。定與慧這二種修法是不同的，印順法師說依定發慧，並不是說只要得定就有智慧，假如這樣說，外道很多都有得定，為什麼沒有無漏的智慧？他們還有種種的邪見，是因為沒有修毗鉢舍那的觀慧，沒有修慧根。真正能斷煩惱，要學習佛法，有了定為基礎，還要在定裡面修觀，觀是毗鉢舍那的智慧，才能將煩惱永遠斷除，因此說慧根是煩惱永斷之所依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十一、未知欲知根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科未知欲知根，說明未知欲知根是證初、第二、第三沙門果之所依處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：未知欲知根誰所依處？答：證初、第二、第三沙門果之所依處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：未知欲知根是誰的所依處？</span></span></span></div>
