<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依信等五善根、三無漏根及意根，這九根可以善思所思；如前說九根，再加上舌根，如是十根善說所說。如前說九根，再加上眼、耳、身、樂、喜、憂、捨，這十六根善作所作。惡思所思，依止一個意根就可以了；惡說所說，依止意根及舌根；惡作所作，依眼、耳、身、苦、樂、憂、喜及男女根九根，應該要加一個意根，因為身語意三業都不能離開意根，所以應該要加上意根，沒有意根，不能分別是不會去作惡事的，這些差別應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、依惑業辨3　午一、辨最勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科依惑業辨，辨別煩惱、業與二十二根的關係，分三科；第一科辨最勝，說明最殊勝的惑業依處是哪幾個根？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根最勝惑業依處？答：九。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪幾根是惑業的最勝依處？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：七色根、意根及命根這九根，如果沒有這些根，是不會起惑造業的。這是強調依處（所依的果報），強調整個生命體。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、辨生起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨生起，說明幾根生起煩惱及業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依幾根處起煩惱業？答：五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依幾個根處生起煩惱造業？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：就是五受根。這是強調能生起煩惱造業的因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、辨能斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科辨能斷，說明幾根能斷煩惱及業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依幾根處斷煩惱業？答：最後八。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依幾根斷煩惱及業？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：最後信進念定慧五善根與三無漏根，這八根能夠斷除煩惱與惡業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾根最勝惑業依處等者：眼等六根、男根、女根、命根，此九最勝惑業依處。依五受根起煩惱業。依信等五、三無漏根斷煩惱業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼耳鼻舌身意六根，還有男根、女根、命根，這九根是煩惱和業的最勝依止處；依五受根生起煩惱和業；依信等五善根及三無漏根能斷煩惱與業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4643"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、依吉祥等辨2　午一、略辨相3　未一、領納吉祥</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科依吉祥等辨，分辨吉祥與二十二根的關係，分二科；第一科略辨相，要略說明吉祥的相貌，又分三科；第一科領納吉祥，說明領納吉祥與二十二根的關係。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：由幾根故，領納一切世出世間所有吉祥？答：除二。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：由幾根故，可以領納一切世出世間所有吉祥的事？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：受以領納為相，若就受的自相而言除去苦與憂二個根，只有喜樂捨三根，能領納一切世出世間所有吉祥。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、領納吉祥敗壞</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科領納吉祥敗壞，說明領納吉祥敗壞與二十二根的關係。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：由幾根故，領納一切吉祥敗壞？答：十一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：由哪幾根領納一切吉祥敗壞？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由七色根、意根、命根，還有憂根與苦根，這十一根領納一切吉祥敗壞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、能引吉祥</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科能引吉祥，說明能引吉祥與二十二根的關係。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根能引所有吉祥？答：最後八。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪幾根能引發所有吉祥？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：最後八個，那是肯定的。信進念定慧五善根與三無漏根，能成就世間與出世間清淨，決定是吉祥的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》領納一切世出世間等者：於五受中，除苦、憂二，餘喜、樂、捨通漏無漏，唯說自相領納一切世出世間所有吉祥。即前所除苦、憂二種不通無漏，兼說所依，領納一切吉祥敗壞，故成十一。謂彼苦根眼等為依，憂根以意為依，異熟生苦命根為依，男女二根身根所攝，亦說為苦所依故。信等五根、三無漏根，能引所有吉祥。於此三問答中，初答除二，當知謂三，義如前釋。次答十一。後答謂八。如是分別二十二根，數無減增，故作斯釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於五受根中，除苦、憂二根，其他的喜樂捨根通於有漏與無漏，這是就受的自相說領納一切世出世間所有吉祥。除前所說苦、憂二種不通無漏，兼說所依七色根、意根及命根，有十一根能領納一切吉祥敗壞；苦是色身的問題，依止著五根而有，憂根是心裡的問題，依止意根而有，果報體的苦，以命根為依止，男女二根是屬於身根的一種，也是苦根所依止，當領納吉祥敗壞時，是這十一根。信進念定慧這五善根，還有三無漏根，能引發世間與出世間所有吉祥之事。在這三個問答中，第一個問題，回答除苦憂二根，受以領納為相，若就受的自相而言有喜樂捨三根，能領納一切世出世間所有吉祥，道理如前所說；其次回答十一根，能領納一切吉祥敗壞；最後回答八根能引發世間與出世間所有吉祥之事，這樣分別二十二根，在三個問答中，數目不增不減剛好二十二個，所以這樣解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、廣釋經3　未一、引經言</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣釋經，詳細解釋經中所說的吉祥法，分三科；第一科引經言，引經所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4644"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，如世尊言：諸受欲者，略有五種作吉祥法。謂忍辱、柔和、觀人而捨、行賢善行，及不放逸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如佛所說：諸多受用欲塵的有情，要略而言有五種作吉祥法：一、忍辱，二、柔和，三、觀人而捨，四、行賢善行，五、不放逸，要有這幾個條件才有吉祥。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、別釋義4　申一、忍辱柔和2　酉一、辨行相2　戌一、忍辱3　亥一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋義，各別解釋經中所說的道理，分四科；第一科忍辱柔和，又分二科；第一科辨行相，說明忍辱柔和的相狀，又分二科；第一科忍辱，說明忍辱的相狀，又分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何忍辱？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作忍辱？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋3　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科標，標出忍辱有三種行相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂由三種行相應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　忍辱有三種行相應該了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列舉出來忍辱的行相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4645"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、不忿怒，二、不報怨，三、不懷惡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一不忿怒，碰到任何人事的境界都不會憤怒；第二是不報怨，有人對自己不好，自己不會報復，沒有報復的心情；第三不懷惡，不會懷惡心或不懷好心。這是忍辱的行相，這樣的人就有忍辱，應觀察自己作到幾點？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、廣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科廣，廣泛的分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若別分別，乃有十種。一、已受怨害忍，二、現前怨害忍，三、慮恐怨害忍，四、饒益怨憎忍，五、損害親友忍，六、一切怨害忍，七、一切因怨害忍，八、受教怨害忍，九、擇力怨害忍，十、自性怨害忍。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若各別分別，忍辱的行相有十種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、已受怨害忍：過去受的怨害能夠忍。於過去受到人、事的怨害，能夠有忍辱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、現前怨害忍：於現前的怨害，自己能夠忍辱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、慮恐怨害忍：擔憂恐懼未來可能會有怨害，對自己有所不利，明知會這樣，也能夠忍辱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、饒益怨憎忍：對方去利益自己所不喜歡、怨恨的人，也能夠有忍辱心，稱為饒益怨憎忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、損害親友忍：有人損害自己所愛的親友，能夠忍下來，這也是一種忍辱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、一切怨害忍：這是約果相說，只要有怨害，不論誰加諸怨害都能夠忍，稱為一切怨害忍，逢怨就是忍。前面五種忍是別說，此處是總說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、一切因怨害忍：這是約因相說，是想要修怨害忍的正念之心。不敢生起一念想害人的心。菩薩畏因，知道起怨害心，異熟果報是不得了的。或者說凡有想要忍的事中都能忍，也可名一切因怨害忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、受教怨害忍：受到他人法的教導，佛法告訴我們要忍辱，因此忍這個怨害，由聞慧勤修法受，稱作受教怨害忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、擇力怨害忍：有思惟簡擇力，能夠思惟簡擇不與他人結怨，學佛的人要廣結善緣，未成佛道先成佛緣，思擇力能夠使令我們忍辱。由思慧勤修法受，稱作受教怨害忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、自性怨害忍：有修慧相應時，才能有自性怨害忍。即是自性堪忍怨害，遍於一切皆悉堪忍、 普於一切皆能堪忍。由無染心，純悲愍故，能有堪忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧菩薩地〉卷42曾說到這一段話。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結名耐違害忍。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是一切，總說名為耐違害忍。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上能夠忍耐他人違害，總說稱為耐違害忍。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》饒益怨憎忍等者：於己怨憎他作饒益能堪忍故，名饒益怨憎忍。於己親友他為損害能堪忍故，名損害親友忍。於怨親中、劣等勝品、有樂有苦、具德具失諸有情所，能忍一切怨害之苦，名一切怨害忍。本地分說：菩薩了知不忍非愛異熟，由怖畏故，勤修行忍。於諸有情有哀憐心、有悲愍心、有親愛心，由親善故，勤修行忍。於其無上正等菩提猛利欲樂，為圓滿忍波羅蜜多，由是因緣，勤修行忍。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/42.htm#45900:33567">陵本四十二卷十二頁3451</a>）是名一切因怨害忍。又說：如世尊說：夫出家者，具忍辱力。由是因緣，不應出家受具足戒而行不忍，由法受故，勤修行忍。是名受教怨害忍。又說：知一切法遠離有情，唯見諸法無戲論性，諦察法故，能修行忍。是名擇力怨害忍。又說：種性具足，先串習忍，於今現在安住自性，故能修忍。是名自性怨害忍。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧菩薩地〉中菩薩怎麼樣修六度，裡面分別得很清楚，要作菩薩也不容易，若未認清楚，有時覺得自己很忍辱，其實沒有在忍。對於與自己有怨憎關係的人，他人利益他，這個也要忍耐，稱為饒益怨憎忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼看仇人得到殊勝的利益，自己能夠忍辱嗎？心裡高興嗎？能夠隨喜嗎？如果對方得到好處，自己也能夠隨喜，就很有忍辱心了。能真誠的祝福他過著幸福快樂的日子。他人來損害自己的親友，自己也能夠忍耐、忍辱，稱為損害親友忍。這個很難，不過經典上有教導這樣想：不要認為這一生的父母親、或者兄弟姐妹，才是自己的父母親與兄弟姐妹，如以無始劫來說，哪一個不曾是自己的父母親與兄弟姐妹呢？為什麼只認今生，不承認前生與以後的呢？如果這樣想，較能夠作到損害親友忍，不然會覺得只有這一生的親友是自己的親友，這一生的父母親才是自己的母親、父親，其他的人都不是。《菩薩戒經》裡說，一切男子是我父，一切女人是我母。同樣是父親傷害父親，就只好忍了，如果認為這是我的父親，那不是我的父親，這人害了那人，就不能忍。經典上是有這樣提到，修忍的方法有很多，可以再參考不同的說法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於與自己有怨、有親或非怨非親的有情，條件比自己下劣、相等、或殊勝的有情，福報大有樂受、或福報小有苦受的有情，具足功德或具諸過失的有情，沒有分別對象，能忍耐以上所說各類有情一切怨害之苦，稱為一切怨害忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈菩薩地〉卷42說：菩薩了知不忍非愛異熟。菩薩知道不忍會得到不可愛的果報，由於害怕得到不可愛的果報，不但不能修行，不能布施，也不能作種種的功德，所以菩薩畏因，就要修行忍。菩薩對於有情真實的有哀憐心、有悲愍心、有親愛心，由於親愛有情，能夠很精進的修習忍。菩薩對於無上正等菩提有猛利欲樂，為了圓滿忍波羅蜜多，由於這個因緣精勤修行忍辱，在〈本地分‧菩薩地〉卷42，1426頁中有廣說這一段，稱為一切因怨害忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又如佛說：出家的人要有忍辱的功德力，由此因緣，出家受具足戒當了比丘、比丘尼，不應該行不忍。由於受教於佛法，應該精進修行忍辱，稱作受教怨害忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又說：知道一切法遠離有情，根本沒有真實的有情存在，能見到諸法無戲論性，仔細真實觀察諸法唯識無義，觀察依他起、法非實有非全無、如夢幻泡影、如露亦如電等，而見到諸法無戲論性，由於這個因緣，能夠修行忍辱，由思擇力，稱為擇力怨害忍。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又說此人過去生有修，一次又一次的修習忍，具足忍辱的種子，現世不用特別修行，也能夠忍辱。有些人一點點不如意境就不能忍，有些人天生就比較忍辱，受得了很多不如意境，這種自性怨害忍也是過去修來的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　忍辱可以引導自己有吉祥，一個忍辱的人就會有吉祥。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、柔和2　亥一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科柔和，說明柔和的相貌，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4646"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何柔和？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為柔和？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷25說：「謂如有一於大師等，具足成就慈愍身業，具足成就慈愍語業，具足成就慈愍意業。與諸有智同梵行者，和同受用應所受用，凡所飲食無有私密，如法所獲如法所得，墮在鉢中、為鉢所攝而為受用，同戒同見成就如是六種可樂、可愛、可重、無違諍法，易可共住，性不惱他，與諸有智同梵行者，共住一處常令歡喜，是名柔和。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋2　天一、標義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標義，標出柔和的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂性賢善，由身語意將護於他，令無惱害。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這人的心性賢善，很賢能，很善良，身語意三業都要保護他人，使他人不受惱害，稱作柔和。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷25說：「謂如有一遠離顰蹙、舒顏平視、含笑先言、常為愛語、性多攝受善法同侶、身心澄淨、是名賢善。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、辨相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨相，說明賢善的相狀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若他所有無罪喜樂，未生令生，生已隨護；有罪憂苦，若未生者遮令不生，若已生者方便令脫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　柔和的人心性賢善，對於他人所有的沒有罪過的喜樂（善的喜樂），如修行五戒十善乃至修戒定慧，於此未生的善法能令其生起，已生起的善法能鼓勵他繼續保護它，繼續增長；於造惡所引生有罪的憂苦，如果還沒有產生，遮止它令不生起，如果已經產生了有罪的憂苦，能透過懺悔等方法令其解脫，這樣的人稱為柔和。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、簡差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡差別，簡擇柔和與忍辱的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中忍辱，耐他違害；柔和，於他不作違損。如是名為二種差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在這當中忍辱是被動的，就是能夠忍耐他人的違害；柔和是主動的，對於他人不作違損的，而且能夠保護他人令無惱害。總之，自己對於他人不惱害稱為柔和；自己能夠忍辱他人惱害，稱為忍辱，這是二種差別。柔和的人，大家都喜歡跟他在一起，因為知道他一定不會作違損事的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、觀人而捨2　酉一、觀人2　戌一、標列二時</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科觀人而捨，領納吉祥的第三個方法稱為觀人而捨，分二科；第一科觀人，觀察他人，又分二科；第一科標列二時，標列二個時候觀察他人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知觀人二時差別。一、攝受時，二、處置時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知觀察他人有二種時間不一樣，第一種是攝受時，以無染及慈悲心，無有顛倒，與作依止，稱為攝受，菩薩初發心時，就頓攝一切眾生為自己的親友，稱為攝受時；第二種是處置時，對方是屬於哪一類的人，就將他安排在哪一類的有情當中，稱為處置時。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、別辨五相2　亥一、於攝受時2　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨五相，各別說明五種相狀，是以五種相貌觀察他人，然後再來攝受他，分二科；第一科於攝受時，說明如果要攝受某人時要如何觀察他，又分二科；第一科標，標出以五相觀察其人，然後攝受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於攝受時，應以五相觀察其人，然後攝受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於攝受眾生時，應該以五種相貌來觀察，然後才來攝受他。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4647"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、由歸誠，二、由技能，三、由智慧，四、由行跡，五、由廉儉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由歸誠：觀察這個人是否能對三寶歸敬忠誠；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由技能：觀察這個人的技藝才能；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由智慧：觀察這個人的智慧；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、由行跡：觀察這個人的行為跡象；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、由廉儉：觀察這個人的是否清廉節儉。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果一個人能對三寶歸敬忠誠、有特殊技藝才能、有智慧、行為端正、不貪而且勤儉，就可以攝受這個人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由行跡者：謂能行履正行跡故，離邪行故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行跡是指觀察對象所作的事情都是符合佛法五戒十善的正行，遠離邪惡的行為，這樣的人可以攝受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、於處置時2　天一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於處置時，處置人時，也用五種相貌來觀察，分二科；第一科標，標出以五相觀察其人，然後處置。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於處置時，亦以五相觀察其人，然後處置。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要安排處置人時，也要由五種相貌來觀察對象，然後才做安排處置。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、堪處事業，置事業中；二、堪處思業，置思業中；三、堪處和業，置和業中；四、堪處護身財業，置護身財業中；五、堪處法業，置法業中。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、堪處事業，置事業中，如果這人能夠承辦事情，就請他去管事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、堪處思業，置思業中，如果這人能夠善於思考，有需要思考的事情，就請他去作；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、堪處和業，置和業中，這人善於處理他人的煩惱，能夠令人和合，就請他作知客師或公關；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、堪處護身財業，置護身財業中，他能夠保護身體、財產，就安排他作醫生、護士或掌管財產作會計等；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、堪處法業，置法業中，這人能夠修學佛法，喜歡聽經、念佛、靜坐，就護持他，專門讓他去修戒定慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》堪處事業等者：功用所作，是名事業。思量所作，是名思業。修和敬業，是名和業。法隨法行，是名法業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由人有承辦事情的功用所作，稱為事業；思考衡量事物的作用稱為思業；修身和同住、口和無諍、意和同悅、戒和同修、見和同解、利和同均之六和敬業，是名和業；修八正道趣向涅槃的法隨法行，是名法業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、捨3　戌一、標數</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科捨，說明捨的相貌，分三科；第一科標數，標出數目。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">捨略有五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　捨，要略而言有五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、列類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列類，列出五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4648"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、田地捨，二、財物捨，三、隨宜捨，</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種是田地捨，將田地捨出來；第二種是財物捨，施捨財物；第三種是隨宜捨，就是在適當時，布施應該要布施的東西。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》隨宜捨者：謂所宜物，隨應施與故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對方最需要什麼，隨所相宜的物品，應時布施。比如對方最需要錢財，就給他錢財；這時對方需要一個微笑，給他一個微笑就是布施；這時對方需要的是問候，就去問候他，稱為隨宜捨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">四、飲食捨，五、最勝捨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四種是飲食捨，對方沒有東西吃，給他食物；第五種是最勝捨，布施最殊勝的物品或法給對方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》最勝捨者：謂捨金銀等珍寶故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《披尋記》解釋最勝捨是指捨金銀等珍寶物；但是《瑜伽論記》解釋是法施才是最勝捨，因為法施可以改變人的思想，思想改變，身語意業就改變，才能夠得到究竟的快樂，所以法施才是最勝捨；窺基大師認為，最勝捨就是布施自己的身體，稱為最勝捨，因為這一種布施最難。同一個簡短的文，因為玄奘大師沒有再翻譯，裡面沒有解釋，學習者的解釋都不一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、釋名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋名，解釋捨的名字。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中捨相、捨具名捨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這當中捨的相狀、捨的資具，稱為捨。〈聲聞地〉卷25說無貪俱行思，造作心意業，及此所起身業、語業，稱為捨相。有了無貪俱行思就能發動身語二業，做種種布施成就捨相；捨具是指捨的內容物，如前面所說的田地捨、財物捨、隨宜捨、飲食捨、最勝捨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此中捨相捨具名捨者：聲聞地說何相施、用何施，如彼別釋應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/25.htm#45934:21042">陵本二十五卷十五頁2131</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷25，875頁說何相施，就是無貪俱行思，造作心意業，及此所起身業、語業，稱為捨相；用何施，用什麼物品布施，用有情如奴婢、牛羊、男女、自己的頭目手足等布施給他人，或者是無情的物品，如穀米、茶杯等布施給他人，這稱作用何施，如〈聲聞地〉卷25中所解釋應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、行賢善行2　酉一、總標舉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科行賢善行，說明行賢善行，分二科；第一科總標舉，總相標示舉出行賢善行的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">賢善行者，為性於他無所違負、無所欺誑。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有賢善行的人，心性對於他人，既不會違背辜負，也不會欺騙誑惑他人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨難釋，困難的地方再說明一下。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4649"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無所違負，復有五種。一、無顛倒違負，二、無委信違負，三、無承事違負，四、無契約違負，五、無他方便違負。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不違背辜負他人，有五種情況。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、無顛倒違負，《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷15窺基大師說：「詐取他物，執為己有名顛。」也就是不會用矯詐欺騙的方法，將他人寄托自己的東西，占為己有；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、無委信違負，不會違背辜負人委託信用於己的事物；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無承事違負，不會本來答應要恭敬承事他，要伺候他，結果說一說又沒作了；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、無契約違負，不會違背辜負與人訂下的契約，不會說契約只是一張紙，事後不認帳；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、無他方便違負，不會想出其他各種方法來違背辜負他人。能做到這樣的人就是賢哲善良行的人。這個文寫得很好，無他方便就將所有其它的情況，沒有說的都包括在裡面，有各式各樣的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、不放逸2　酉一、總標舉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科不放逸，說明不放逸的相貌，分二科；第一科總標舉，總相標示舉出不放逸的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="51253:45942"></a>不放逸者，謂修習諸善法，防護不善心。因果相屬故，俱應為彼相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為不放逸？不放逸是精進的修習種種善法，防護不善心，例如修戒、根律儀等。以斷惡修善為因，能成就可愛的果報，因果相屬，都屬於不放逸的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、廣種類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣種類，說明不放逸的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復有五種應知。一、求財不放逸，二、守財不放逸，三、護身不放逸，四、護名不放逸，五、行法不放逸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不放逸又有五種應當了知：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、求財時不要放逸；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、守財時，也不可以放逸，不可以有惡心，而且要正正當當；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、護身不放逸，保護自己的身體也不能太過放縱；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、護名不放逸，為保護自己的名譽而修不放逸；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、行法不放逸，不斷精進修習善法，維持無貪、無瞋、無癡的善心而修不放逸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、顯力能2　申一、標列2　酉一、五力</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顯力能，開顯忍辱等五法的力用功能，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出五力能生吉祥，又分二科；第一科五力，說明五力。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是一切，總有五力能生吉祥。一、善尸羅力，二、善朋友力，三、無弊吝力，四、可委信力，五、法力。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說忍辱、柔和、觀人而捨、行賢善行、不放逸五法，總共有五種力量能夠產生吉祥：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、善尸羅力，忍辱柔和能成就戒的善尸羅力；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、善朋友力，由善觀察能成就善知識的善朋友力；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無弊吝力，由捨能成就沒有弊下慳吝的無弊吝力；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、可委信力，由行賢善行有可值得委託信賴的可委信力；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、法力，由不放逸能具足各種善法的法力。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》總有五力能生吉祥等者：當知此中，善尸羅力，由忍辱柔和故有；善朋友力，由觀人故有；無弊吝力，由捨故有；可委信力，由行賢善行故有；法力，由不放逸故有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總共有五種力量能夠產生吉祥：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、善尸羅力，就是戒的力量，是由忍辱與柔和能夠作到的；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、善朋友力，會觀察人，能夠有善朋友力，如果有好的朋友能夠使令產生吉祥；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、無弊吝力，沒有慳貪就是捨，捨的力量能使人產生吉祥；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、可委信力，是行賢善行會吉祥。此人可以委託、可以信得過，這是可委信力；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、法力，由善法力能生吉祥。善法力是從不放逸來，說這人法力高強，因為他非常不放逸，才會法力高強。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、吉祥</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科吉祥，解釋五種吉祥的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4650"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知吉祥亦有五種。一、眾所愛樂，二、富貴自在，三、怨敵退伏，四、饒益所依，五、往諸善趣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知吉祥也有五種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、眾所愛樂，大家都歡喜好樂親近；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、富貴自在，饒具財富身心自在；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、怨敵退伏，怨家敵人能退開降伏；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、饒益所依，能令所依身心獲得利益；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、往諸善趣，來生不墮惡趣，能到人天善趣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、配釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科配釋，配合五力解釋吉祥。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前四種力，總能生起四種吉祥；第五一力，能生第五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前四種力，包括善尸羅力、善朋友力、無弊吝力，還有可委信力，這四種力都能夠得到四種吉祥，就是眾所愛樂、富貴自在、怨敵退伏、饒益所依；第五種善法力能夠往諸善趣。　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、證得等差別2　辰一、略配屬3　巳一、由為緣4　午一、先煩惱業為緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　決擇根善巧，廣分別第二嗢柁南，以長行解釋，其中的第三科證得等差別，說明證得等與二十二根相應的差別相，分二科；第一科略配屬，先略配屬，而後再廣決擇，略配屬是略說明煩惱業等與二十二根的配屬，又分三科；第一科由為緣，說明由什麼為緣產生二十二根，又分四科；第一科先煩惱業為緣，說明七色根與命根八根由先煩惱業為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根先煩惱業之所感得？答：八。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪幾根是過去的煩惱與業所感得的呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有八根，由過去生的煩惱業為緣，產生現在的七色根與命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、名色為緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科名色為緣，說明意根以名色為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根名色為緣？答：一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：幾根是以名色為緣？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：意根一根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、觸處為緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科觸處為緣，說明五受根以觸緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根觸為緣？答：五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：幾根以觸為緣？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：苦樂憂喜捨這五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、策勵為緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科策勵為緣，五善根與三無漏根以策勵為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根策勵為緣？答：八。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：幾根以策勵為緣呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：信進念定慧，與未知欲知根、已知根、及具知根這八根；五善根與三無漏根要靠後天的努力才能夠得到的，由策勵精進的修道才能夠得道，因此是以策勵為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾根先煩惱業之所感得等者：七有色根及與命根，如是八根，先煩惱業之所感得，以彼一切異熟攝故。意根一種，名色為緣。苦等五根，由觸為緣。最後八根，策勵為緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七有色根及與命根，這八根是過去煩惱業所感得的，屬於變異成熟的果報所攝。意根一種是以名色為緣。苦等五受根是以觸為緣。最後信進念定慧五善根與三無漏根八根，必須精進修行才有，所以是策勵為緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4651"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、由應修4　午一、應防護</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由應修，幾根應修防護等，分四科；第一科應防護，七有色根與命根應防護。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根應防護？答：八。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪幾根是應該要防護的？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：七有色根與命根這八根要防護它，不要讓它去攀緣外境；命根也要保護好，才能夠修行，這是應防護的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、應調靜</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科應調靜，說明幾根能調伏、遠離煩惱，令心寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根應調靜？答：一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：幾根應該要調靜的？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：意根一，不要讓意根一直心猿意馬，到處亂跑，應調伏意根，使遠離煩惱令心寂靜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、應寂止</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科應寂止，說明幾根應該寂止。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根應寂止？答：五。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪幾根應該寂靜、止息？　</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：五受根，若無苦樂憂喜捨的干擾，能令心常處於寂靜、止息，不會產生喜怒無常而造業，所以應該寂止這五受根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、性調順等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科性調順等，幾根自性是調順等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根自性調順、寂靜、寂止，復能調伏、寂靜、寂止？答：八。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪幾根自性是調順、寂靜、寂止，又能調伏、寂靜、寂止？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有八根，就是五善根與三無漏根。當修行人內心不被色聲香味觸貪瞋癡男女等十相所干擾，呈現調順時，或遠離五蓋、八種尋思的障礙，趣向寂靜的禪定，乃至心住一趣而寂止得定時，才能成就五善根與三無漏根的功德，所以說這八根的自性是調順、寂靜、寂止，又能調伏、寂靜、寂止。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾根應防護等者：此中或八、或一、或五、或八，例如前說應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處文中所說或八、或一、或五、或八，可以如前所說例推應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、由類別2　午一、有漏攝4　未一、捨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由類別，二十二根捨等有漏無漏的種類差別，分二科；第一科有漏攝，說明有漏所攝，又分四科；第一科捨，諸根捨的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何諸根捨？謂同分界地諸根滅，餘生起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是諸根捨呢？這個人在同分界地的諸根滅了，在另一個同分界地的諸根又生起了。如欲界有情死歿後，屬於欲界的諸根滅，在欲界又生起另外一個果報體的諸根，可能是人，可能是畜生，可能是餓鬼，仍是在同一個欲界內，這是同分界地。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、棄</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科棄，棄捨諸根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4652"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何諸根棄？謂不同分界地諸根滅，餘生起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是諸根棄呢？就是這個人在一個界地的諸根滅了，而另一個不同分界地的諸根生起了。譬如說在欲界死歿，欲界的諸根滅了，感生到色界或者無色界果報的諸根生起，這是棄捨前一個界地的諸根，而生起其餘不同界地的諸根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、斷</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科斷，諸根斷。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何諸根斷？謂斷彼繫縛一切煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是諸根斷呢？是指斷除繫縛諸根的一切煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、退</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科退，諸根退。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何諸根退？謂世間興盛若定、若生所有失壞。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為諸根退呢？世間的興盛、富貴吉祥、或者得到禪定、或者是生到色界天去等，如果又再退失了，這是諸根退。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是解釋捨棄斷退的定義，這些都屬於有漏的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、無漏攝2　未一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無漏攝，以下屬於無漏的情況，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：聲聞、獨覺、菩薩諸根，有何差別？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：聲聞、獨覺、菩薩的諸根有什麼差別？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、答2　申一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標列，標列出五種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：當知差別略有五種。一、品類差別，二、任持差別，三、羂索差別，四、正行差別，五、證得差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應當知道聲聞、獨覺與菩薩的諸根差別，要略而言有五種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、品類差別；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、任持差別；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、羂索差別，羂是束縛，拘束。羂索，被繩索或它物束縛於某處義。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、正行差別；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、證得差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、隨釋5　酉一、品類差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分五科；第一科品類差別，解釋品類差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">品類差別者，諸菩薩根，其性上品；聲聞、獨覺所有諸根，軟品、中品。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　品類差別是指菩薩的根器是屬於上品，聲聞是軟品的根器，獨覺是中品根器。以根性的不同，說明品類差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4653"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、任持差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科任持差別，說明任持差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">任持差別者，諸菩薩根，一切明處善巧任持；聲聞、獨覺所有諸根，一分明處善巧任持。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一切明處就是五明，包括內明、因明、聲明、工巧明、還有醫方明。菩薩於一切明處都有善巧的智慧，都能任持具足；而聲聞、獨覺所有諸根，只要將五明中的內明一分，做好即可以，他的大事已畢，不要學那麼多，不像菩薩要法門無量誓願學。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、羂索差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科羂索差別，說明羂索差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">羂索差別者，諸菩薩根，大悲所羂；聲聞、獨覺根不如是。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　羂索差別方面，是指菩薩的根性為大悲所羂，羂在哪裡？羂在眾生的生死中，菩薩發願無量劫中在生死度眾生，這是菩薩的根性。聲聞、獨覺則不是，他們希望早入無餘依涅槃；這世間太苦，不想再來，想要早點離去。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　菩薩有二種：一、發願生生世世再來人間，為佛法的正覺之音而努力，為了度眾生，願意繼續再來人間受生，很多團體也有這樣提倡。二、像中國佛教，有一大部分提倡到極樂世界，成就不退轉功德，再回來度眾生，也還是不離生死。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、正行差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科正行差別，說明正行差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">正行差別者，諸菩薩根，自利利他正行現前；聲聞、獨覺所有諸根，自利現前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　正行差別是指菩薩的根性，不但要自利也要利他。以自利利他而言分為三種人：上品人能夠自利利他；中品的人只有利他；下品的人是只有自利。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　菩薩是自利利他正行現前；聲聞、獨覺所有諸根，急求了脫生死苦惱，能很快的了生死，自利現前。這是正行的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉五、證得差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科證得差別，說明證得差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">證得差別者，諸菩薩根，證得無上大菩提果；聲聞、獨覺所有諸根，證得下中二菩提果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　證得果位的差別；菩薩諸根證得無上大菩提的佛果，是最圓滿的；聲聞的諸根證得阿羅漢是下品的菩提果，獨覺證得辟支佛是中品的菩提果。這是分別菩薩與聲聞獨覺證得果位差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是說明證得等差別的略配屬，以下是廣決擇。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、廣決擇2　巳一、清淨諸根攝2　午一、約諸根體業辨2　未一、唯辨喜根2　申一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣決擇，詳細廣泛的決擇清淨與雜染諸根證得差別，分二科；第一科清淨諸根攝，先說清淨諸根所攝證得差別，又分二科；第一科約諸根體業辨，以諸根的體性與功能來說，又分二科；第一科唯辨喜根，只說明喜根，再說其他諸根，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若補特伽羅依未至定修諦現觀，彼得果時，起初靜慮喜根現前，為不起耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若有一類人依止未到地定，修四諦現觀，在證果時，會不會有初靜慮的喜根現前呢？還是喜根不生起呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依未至定修諦現觀等者：初靜慮近分，未至定所攝。唯此近分能為依止，修諦現觀，得沙門果，非餘上地諸近分定，由是依此偏問喜根。然復當知，喜有多別。謂如經說：此身離生喜樂之所滋潤、遍滋潤、遍充滿、遍適悅、遍流布者，是名初靜慮近分。又如經說：即此身中一切處，無有少分離生喜樂所不遍滿者，是謂初靜慮根本。今此問義，謂此根本之所攝喜，為起不起，非彼近分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初靜慮的近分是屬於未至定所攝。近分就是靠近，四禪八定都有近分定，只有初禪前的未到地定才能夠直接修諦現觀證得沙門果，並非其他上地（二禪、三禪、四禪）的諸近分定可以證得沙門果，因此依止這個情況來問喜根。然而應當知道，喜有很多種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如經上說：離欲界煩惱生出歡喜快樂，身體為歡喜快樂之所滋養潤澤，而且歡喜快樂徧身滋潤、徧身充滿、徧身適悅、徧身流布，這是初靜慮的近分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又如經典上說：就在此身體上沒有一個地方不被離欲界煩惱生出的喜樂所徧滿的，這是指得到初禪時。現在是問初禪的喜有沒有生起？並不是指近分定的喜。只是要討論此人依未到地定修諦現觀，證果時，初禪的喜根會不會現前？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4654"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、答2　酉一、標差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標差別，標示出差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：有一能起，有一不起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有的人能生起喜，有的人不能。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有一能起有一不起等者：此中答意，謂有差別。非定不起，亦非定起。由有一類利根能現起故，一類鈍根不能起故。顯揚論說有四種行，謂苦遲通行、苦速通行、樂遲通行、樂速通行。苦遲通行者，謂鈍根者，未得現法樂住，為盡諸漏若道若行。苦速通行者，謂利根者，餘如前說。（顯揚論二卷十七頁）此說有一能起，謂即苦速通行。有一不起，謂即苦遲通行。如是差別應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處的回答，是指這裡面有差別，不是決定喜不會生起，也不是決定生起。有一類利根的人如果這樣修，能夠現起初靜慮喜根；有一類鈍根的人就不能生起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《顯揚聖教論》卷2說有四種修行的狀況；苦遲通行、苦速通行、樂遲通行、樂速通行，修行人分成四大類。苦是指沒有得到根本定者，身心未能領受樂受；樂是指已得到根本定者，能領受樂受；遲是指信進念定慧屬鈍根者；速是指信進念定慧屬利根者；通是通達，通達諸法實相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦遲通行，是指沒有得到初禪以上，只有得到未到地定，善根屬於鈍根性者，為斷盡各種煩惱的聖道修行，在這較低的定中修無漏的四諦觀而見諦；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　苦速通行是指沒有得到根本靜慮，只有得到未到地定，卻是利根的這一類的人；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　樂遲通行是指有初靜慮等根本靜慮的鈍根行者；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　樂速通行是指有得初靜慮等根本靜慮，而且也是利根的行者。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處說有一類人能生起初禪的喜根，是指苦速通行的利根行者，有一類人不能生起初禪的喜根，是指苦遲通行的行者。這是苦遲通行與苦速通行的差別。</span></span></span></div>
