<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋因緣，解釋因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有利根，眾多善本之所資助；彼能現起，非餘。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是利根的行者，有眾多信進念定慧的善根、二道資糧圓滿為本做為資助，所以能夠現起喜，其他鈍根的人就不能。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4655"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》眾多善本之所資助者：謂如成就戒律儀、成就根律儀、於食知量、初夜後夜悎寤瑜伽、正知而住，如是乃至成就所有沙門莊嚴，如是種種定資糧法應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈本地分‧聲聞地〉的卷21與卷22說到修行的情況，卷22，799頁有二道資糧的偈頌：自他圓滿善法欲，戒根律儀食知量，悎寤正知住善友，聞思無障捨莊嚴，這幾樣事情都作到，這個人就是利根，積聚了很多的資糧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修行人若自身的內緣圓滿，外善知識外緣圓滿，有善法欲出家修行，持戒清淨有戒律儀，也有根律儀、於食知量，飲食是為了修行，知道什麼該食，什麼不該食，有悎寤瑜伽，悎就是覺悟，隨時想要起來，二十四小時都想要修行，連睡覺也是正知而住，隨時身語意三業作什麼，都明明白白的。而且具備善知識、善友性的多種功德、能聽聞佛法，思惟佛法，並且沒有煩惱障、業障，報障，還能夠布施，又成就沙門莊嚴的功德，這些資糧條件都具足了，在未到地定修毗鉢舍那，證果時，會有喜根現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、通辨諸根2　申一、配屬證得2　酉一、證得諸定3　戌一、初二靜慮2　亥一、舉初靜慮</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科通辨諸根，通說二十二根的證得與業用，分二科；第一科配屬證得，將二十二根配屬諸定及聖果證得，又分二科；第一科證得諸定，二十二根配屬諸定，又分三科；第一科初二靜慮，說明幾根入初、二靜慮，又分二科；第一科舉初靜慮，舉初禪為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根入初靜慮？答：八。後三，一分能入，一分不能。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中有哪幾根可以入初禪？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有八個根可以入初禪，就是意根、喜根、樂根、還有五善根。後三是三無漏根，這是意根、喜根、樂根、捨根、信等五善根這九根的分位，其中一部分能入初禪，這一分是意樂喜與信進念定慧可以入。一部分不能入的就是捨根，由於初禪沒有捨的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、例第二靜慮</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例第二靜慮，以初禪為例，二禪也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如初靜慮，第二亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如初靜慮如是，第二禪也是一樣。也是八根能入，捨根不能入於二禪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、第三靜慮</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第三靜慮。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4656"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第三亦爾，然非即彼。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三禪也一樣有八根能入，但與前有所不同。三禪的功德是捨、念、正知、樂與心一境性，而無喜根，一分不能入的就是喜根。一分能入是其他的意根、樂根、捨根、還有五善根八根可以入三禪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、第四靜慮及無色定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第四靜慮及無色定，說明第四靜慮及無色定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第四靜慮及無色定，七根能入。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四禪及無色定，信進念定慧五善根與意根、捨根七根能入。後三無漏根的九根分位中，有一分不能入的就是喜根與樂根，其餘能入的是指信進念定慧，還有意根與捨根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾根入初靜慮等者：謂意、喜、樂及信等五，如是八根入初靜慮。後三無漏，即九根分，除其捨分，餘分能入，是名一分能入；捨不能入，是名一分不能。第三靜慮亦八根入，故言亦爾。然應除喜取身，說非即彼，由於彼地離喜寂靜，領受身樂故。第四靜慮及無色定，唯信等五及與意、捨七根能入。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　入初靜慮與二靜慮時，是信進念定慧，還有意根、喜根、樂根是這八根的作用。後三無漏就是未知欲知根、已知根與具知根，這三根是意根、樂根、喜根、捨根及五善根等九根的分位，除了捨根，因為初禪沒有捨的功德，初禪是尋、伺、喜、樂、心一境性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二靜慮是內等淨、喜、樂、心一境性，四支中捨的功德也還沒有，所以捨根不能入，除掉捨根，其餘八根能入，稱作一分能入；捨不能入，稱作一分不能入。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三靜慮也是八根能入，應該除掉的是喜根，因為三禪是離喜妙樂地，有念、正知，樂、捨、心一境性五支功德，遠離二禪喜的踴動，領受身樂的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四靜慮以上與四空定，只有信進念定慧五善根、意根與捨根七根能入，因為這時最寂靜，樂也沒有了只有捨受，故說七根能入。 　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">後三，有一能入，有一不能。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　後三無漏根的支分中，有一類聲聞能入，即信進念定慧五善根、意根與捨根七根能入。有一分不能，是指若入定深慧淺的無色定，難以增長與修行信等五善根、意根與捨根，此時一類菩薩七根不能入。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》後三有一能入有一不能者：此中唯約入無色定為論。一類聲聞，於後三中七根能入。一類菩薩不能。由諸菩薩住菩薩法，性遠離無色修靜慮故。義如顯揚論說。（三卷十五頁）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處唯就入無色定而說，一類聲聞人於後三無漏根中七根能入。一類菩薩不能，因為諸菩薩安住菩薩法，不修無色定，因為無色定的人定深慧淺，根本不可能修學佛法，義理如《顯揚聖教論》3卷15頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、證得聖果3　戌一、初二果2　亥一、辨差別2　天一、預流果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科證得聖果，以證得聖果來說二十二根，分三科；第一科初二果，先說初果與二果，又分二科；第一科辨差別，說明證得聖果的差別，又分二科；第一科預流果，說明幾根得初果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根得預流果？答：或一、或八。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪幾根得預流果？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：或者有一個未知欲知根，這是約假法而說的；或是八個，是五善根，加上意根、樂根及捨根，這是約實法而說的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4657"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、一來果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科一來果，說明成就幾根得二果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或二、或九得一來果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　約假法而言，有未知欲知根與已知根這二根；或是約實法而言，有意根、樂根、捨根、五善根及未知欲知根、已知根其中一個，這二種情形可以得二果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、簡取捨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡取捨，簡別取捨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">憂根雖道所依，非道攝故，此中不取。喜根非堅住故，此亦不取。若通取者，當增其數。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　擔心修行沒有成就恐怕墮落，有出離欲俱行憂時而精進修行，此時憂根雖然是修道所依，可是不是聖道所攝，所以不將憂根算在裡面；若在未到地定證得聖道，喜根是不堅住的，像有一類鈍根，得到初果但沒有喜，此處也不將喜根算在裡面；如果要通取憂根與喜根，應當增加根數。這裡是將憂根與喜根簡別掉，這是簡取捨，簡別哪些要取，哪些要捨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、不還果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不還果，說明不還果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根得不還果？答：或十一、或二。憂根道理，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根裡面有哪幾根是得不還果？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：或是十一根；意根、樂根、喜根、捨根、信等五善根、未知欲知根、已知根；或二根就是未知欲知根與已知根，憂根不算在內的道理如前文所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、阿羅漢果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科阿羅漢果，說明幾根成就阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾根得阿羅漢果？答：或一、或十。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪幾根得阿羅漢果？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：或是具知根一根；或是十根；意根、樂根、喜根、捨根、信等五善根這九根，再加上具知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4658"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》幾根得預流果等者：或說一根得預流果，謂未知欲知根。或說八根得預流果，謂意、樂、捨及信等五。未知欲知根中，除喜分故。或說二根得一來果，謂未知欲知根及已知根，頓漸差別容有二故。或說九根得一來果，初二無漏隨應或一，及意、樂、捨并信等五，總合說故。或說十一根得不還果，謂意、樂、喜、捨，及信等五，并未知欲知根、已知根，頓漸種類總合說故。或說二根得不還果，謂未知欲知根及已知根。或說一根得阿羅漢果，謂具知根。或謂十根得阿羅漢果，謂具知根、意、樂、喜、捨及信等五，總合說故。當知此中，分別諸根或假或實、或別或合、或減或增，義不齊等。言假實者，三無漏根非實有法，是名為假；所餘諸根實有法故，是名為實。言別合者，或假實法差別為論，如於初預流果；或復總合為論，如後三果。一來果中，隨取一未知欲知根或已知根，亦名為別；不還果中，兼取二根，亦名為合。言減增者，謂彼喜根，初二果中不取，於不還果則復取之，是名減增。此復云何？由前已說，未知欲知根，證初、第二、第三沙門果之所依處。若依初靜慮近分證彼果時，喜根有動，名非堅住，由或能起、或不起故。今約彼類，是故不取，然不應說唯初二果。若依初靜慮根本證彼果時，喜根堅住，應皆取之，此亦不應唯說不還。今於文中，不取或取差別為論，義非決定，或減或增，隨應說故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或說一根得預流果，是指未知欲知根。或說八根得預流果，是指意樂捨根，與信進念定慧五根。未知欲知根中，除喜的部分，因為喜根唯利根的初果聖者才有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或說二根得一來果，是指未知欲知根及已知根，由於有頓證與漸證的差別，有些人在未知欲知根就頓證二果，乃至也有頓證三果的；或者說九根得一來果，指未知欲知根與已知根隨其所相應的其中一根，頓證者取未知欲知根，漸證者取已知根，加上意、樂、捨及信進念定慧這八根，總合說有九根。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或說十一根得不還果，是指意、樂、喜、捨，及信等五善根與未知欲知根、已知根，將頓證與漸證的人合起來說，有十一根得不還果；或約假法說二根得不還果，包括未知欲知根及已知根，頓證者取未知欲知根，漸證者取已知根，這是頓證與漸證的人合起來說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或說一根得阿羅漢果，就是具知根；或說十根得阿羅漢果，指具知根，加上意、樂、喜、捨及信等五善根，總說與別說合起來說。其實具知根的成分也是意、樂、喜、捨，與信進念定慧五善根。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡分別諸根假與實；有時分別說、有時合起來說；有時減、有時增，涵義不齊等。說到假實，三無漏根不是真實有的，而是假有，是九根的分位；其他的根是實有法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　分別說或合起來說，是指假法與實法差別為論，如於初預流果，說或一未知欲知根得預流果，這是以假法而言；若依實法而說，則為八根，指意樂捨根與信進念定慧五根，未知欲知根中，除喜的部分；若將假法與實法合起來說，如後面三個果，二、三、四果；一來果當中，後面或九，隨取其中的未知欲知根或已知根之一，也稱為別說；不還果中，將未知欲知根或已知根二種合在一起都算在內，稱作合說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說到減或增是指喜根，初、二果中不取喜根，在不還果時增加上去，有減有增，稱作減增。這又怎麼說呢？因為前面有說，在未知欲知根可以證初果、二果，還有三果，如果依初靜慮近分定證果時，喜根就有動，不是堅住的，因為利根的人喜根能起，鈍根的人喜根不起；現在以那個種類的喜根有動所以不取，然而不應該說唯初、二果有無喜根的情況；若是依初禪根本定證果時，喜根堅住，都應該將喜根放進去，這裡不應該只有將喜根算在不還果中。在文裡面這樣不取或者是取，依種種的差別而論，道理並不決定，到底是減或增，根數有多少，要隨其所相應的來解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處韓居士說：若依初靜慮根本證彼果時，喜根堅住，應皆取之，此亦不應唯說不還。韓居士這句話應當修正，因為依根本定入諦現觀應直證三果，所以本論原文所說還是對的。《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷25說：「見道依九處身，謂人三洲除北俱盧及六欲天，此九皆能入見道故。」意指唯依欲界人天能入見道證初果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C57-01.htm">二十二根區分與諸差別相對照表</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、建立業用2　酉一、憂根攝3　戌一、引經</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科建立業用，建立二十二根的作用，分二科；第一科憂根攝，介紹憂根所攝，又分三科；第一科引經，引經典上所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如經言：於上解脫希、求、憂、慼。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如經上說：有情對於能夠解脫煩惱這一件事情，心裡希望、追求、憂慮、悲慼。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、釋名4　亥一、希</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋名，解釋希、求、憂、慼的名相，分四科；第一科希，說明希的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何希？謂修行者作如是念：是處眾聖能具足住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是希？修行人心裡這樣想：涅槃是所有的聖人都能夠圓滿安住的處所，希望自己也能夠成就解脫的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4659"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、求</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科求，說明求的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">求云何？謂修行者作如是念：我於是處當具足住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是求？修行人心裡這樣想：我應該具足安住到無住涅槃，應該努力追求解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、慼</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科慼，說明慼的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">慼云何？謂於下劣不生喜足。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是慼？修行人對所證得的下品境界心理憂慼不生歡喜滿足，覺得只有這樣修行還不夠，不會得少為足。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥四、憂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科憂，說明憂的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">憂云何？謂於無上心生思慕。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是憂？修行人對於最圓滿的，不能再超過了的境界，如大乘人對於成佛，小乘人對於得阿羅漢果，心裡生出思惟仰慕，擔心自己不能成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4660"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》是處眾聖能具足住者：本地分中修所成地說：為趣究竟，於現法中心極思慕。彼由如是心生思慕，出離樂欲數數現行。謂我何當能具足住如是聖處，如阿羅漢所具足住。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/20.htm#46049:17630">陵本二十卷二十三頁1797</a>）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧修所成地〉卷20，753頁說：為了到達究竟圓滿，在現在的色受想行識當中，心裡非常的思惟仰慕究竟圓滿，由於有這種思惟仰慕，出離的樂欲會數數現行，心想：我什麼時候能夠具足安住在這聖境之中，如阿羅漢所具足安住的一樣。如卷20所說，可以準照那裡解釋了解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、料簡2　亥一、初二果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科料簡，思惟簡別初、二、三果憂根的差別相，分二科；第一科初二果，說明初果與二果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中，預流、一來，於一切種皆圓滿故，建立憂根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在這當中，初果與二果都有希、求、憂、慼的心情，而建立憂根，又稱為出離欲俱行憂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、不還果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不還果，說明不還果之憂根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若不還果，雖有初二，餘二無故，不立憂根，唯善法欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果是不還果，為什麼不立憂根？因為三果聖者希望、追求成就阿羅漢果，但是已經離欲界欲，不會有憂，自知只要願意努力就可以很快證得阿羅漢果，所以沒有慼，也不會憂，因此不立憂根，只有善法欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於一切種皆圓滿者：此一切種，謂即前說希、求、慼、憂一切差別應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此一切種，是指前文所說希、求、慼、憂這四種心情差別應當了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、喜等根攝2　戌一、辨依捨3　亥一、喜為依</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科喜等根攝，說明喜等根所攝，分二科；第一科辨依捨，分別辨明依捨，又分三科；第一科喜為依，說明以喜為依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：頗有依止喜根，能捨喜根、憂根、捨根耶？答：有。謂依出離喜根為依止故，捨依耽嗜三根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：有沒有依止喜根，能捨喜根、憂根，還有捨根呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有，如果有出離心為依，所生起的依出離喜，就可以捨離愛著五欲引起的依耽嗜喜、依耽嗜憂及依耽嗜捨三根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、憂為依</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科憂為依，以憂根為依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：頗有依止憂根，捨憂根耶？答：有。謂依出離為依止故，捨依耽嗜。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：有沒有依止憂根捨離憂根呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有，就是以出離心為依止，能捨離愛著五欲引起的依耽嗜憂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、捨為依2　天一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科捨為依，以捨根為依，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4661"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：頗有依止捨根，捨捨根耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：有沒有依止捨根來捨離捨根？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、答2　地一、依一性捨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科依一性捨，說明依止一性來捨種種性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：有。謂依一性捨為依止故，捨依種種性捨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有，就是依四空定來捨除色界種種捨。空無邊處定只有緣空為境界；識無邊處定以識為境界；無所有處定以無所有為境界；非想非非想處定就是去除無所有再往上，這四種定稱為一性捨。依一性捨為依止故，捨離色界色乃至法等種種性捨。窺基大師說：無色界捨唯緣法塵，名一性捨。色界境多，名種種捨。緣無心，名無所依捨。緣有心，名一性捨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、依無所依捨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依無所依捨，無所依層次更高了，就是真的出離了捨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無所依捨為依止故，捨依一性捨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以出世間無所依捨為依止，能捨離依一性捨。捨的層次有很多種，就世間而言，最高的就是依四空定的一性捨。若就出世間而言，依無相心三摩地或是滅盡定就是無所依捨，可以捨離四空定的一性捨，究竟出離捨根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、簡差別2　亥一、未知欲知根攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡差別，無所依捨的差別，分二科；第一科未知欲知根攝，說明未知欲知根所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">得預流果時，未知欲知根亦滅亦捨，非起而棄，非斷非退。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修行人證初果時得到已知根，未知欲知根就滅了，也捨了；得到已知根以後，未知欲知根不會再現起，這是非起而永遠的棄捨；證初果並不是說將未知欲知根斷除了，只是轉變而已，由於已成就另一個不同的境界，未知欲知根也是信進念定慧，意、樂、喜、捨九根的分位，與已知根的內容是一樣，只是層次不同，所以也不會退失，因為已經證得擇滅了，證得諸法實相以後，所有的善根都不會退失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、已知根攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科已知根攝，已知根的情況也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">得阿羅漢果時，已知根道理，應知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　得阿羅漢果時，已知根亦滅亦捨，非起而棄，非斷非退的道理，應當知道也是一樣。其實三無漏根內容都是一樣，只是層次不同，轉變得更圓滿而已。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依一性捨等者：謂依虛空無邊處，乃至依非想非非想處，是名依一性捨。若依於色，乃至依於法，是名依種種性捨。義如顯揚論說。（五卷十二頁）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依虛空無邊處，乃至依非想非非想處，稱為依一性捨；若是依於色聲香味觸法所生的捨，是名依種種性捨。道理如《顯揚聖教論》卷5所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、約補特伽羅辨2　未一、根性差別2　申一、聲聞2　酉一、明練根2　戌一、辨有無2　亥一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約補特伽羅辨，約人的根性差別及圓滿差別與二十二根的關係，分二科；第一科根性差別，說明根性差別，又分二科；第一科聲聞，說明聲聞的情況，又分二科；第一科明練根，說明什麼是練根，又分二科；第一科辨有無，分別有沒有練根的情況，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4662"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：幾補特伽羅有練根耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：哪一些人有練根呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、答2　天一、標有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標有，標出有學及五種無學都有練根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：一切有學；及無學五，退、思、護、住、堪達種性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：一切有學的初果、二果向、二果、三果向、三果及四果向的聖者，及五種鈍根無學聖者；退法、思法、護法、住法、堪達種性之無學都有練根。見道及不還果之人之「欲界經生」者等，則無練根之義。此因見道係速疾而不修加行，故不須修練根；而「欲界經生」之聖者等既已究極其根性而熟習，故亦不修練根。修行人藉由道力的熏修，令善根相續，或捨下品而得中品，或捨中品而得上品，漸次增勝，稱為練根。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《成唯識論疏義演》卷8說：大乘中練根通於有漏無漏。於有漏練根中，若過去是鈍根就多修學法義，令善根純熟；也有言語遲鈍之類就學習論議決擇，或聽聞法義披尋經論，都名為練根；於無漏練根類，以無漏道熏有漏定，使定根由下、中根轉成上品，或從有漏定轉成無漏定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　本論說阿羅漢有二類，一類鈍根者，要有好的條件才會解脫，就是時解脫阿羅漢，又分為退法、思法、護法、住法、堪達種性五種；另一類利根者，不論哪一個時間，不限於哪一個地點，哪種情況都可以成就解脫，稱為不時解脫阿羅漢，又名不動法阿羅漢。阿羅漢既已斷除三界愛見煩惱，為什麼還要練根，練什麼根呢？阿羅漢的聖道不會退，但這五種鈍根的阿羅漢他的禪定還會退失，所以必須再修練根，常常以無漏道夾雜熏修禪定，練習入住出禪定，不然禪定也會退，所以此處說無學五，退、思、護、住、堪達種性有練根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》退思護住堪達種性者：阿羅漢果根有鈍利，成六差別。一、退法，二、思法，三、護法，四、住不動，五、堪能通達，六、不動法。如顯揚論別釋應知。（三卷十二頁）此中前五，皆鈍根攝，是故說彼有練根義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿羅漢果根有鈍有利，有六種差別。一、退法，二、思法，三、護法，四、住不動，五、堪能通達，六、不動法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《顯揚聖教論》3卷12頁有各別解釋。前五種都屬鈍根，鈍根阿羅漢才需要練根，如果根性已經很利，就不用再練根了，如第六種不動法阿羅漢是利根，能不退現法樂住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、簡無</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡無，簡除獨覺、菩薩因為利根所以沒有練根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">非諸獨覺，亦非菩薩，性利根故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不是獨覺，也不是菩薩有練根，因為獨覺與菩薩是利根，不用修練根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、辨修證2　亥一、預流2　天一、得證一來果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨修證，分別修證的情況，分二科；第一科預流，說明初果聖人練根的結果，又分二科；第一科得證一來果，說明初果聖人練根以後，能證一來果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若預流者修練根時，既得練根，亦證一來果耶？答：證。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果初果聖人修習練根，既然能夠練根，能不能證得二果呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：可以證得二果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、不證不還果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不證不還果，說明初果聖人修習練根，不能證不還果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：亦證不還果耶？答：不證。對治難得故，所應得義極廣大故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：初果聖人修習練根以後，也證不還果嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：不會證三果，由於欲界的貪欲與瞋恚很難對治，要證得三果的聖道很廣大，不容易斷欲瞋證得，因此初果聖人修了練根以後，最多證二果，不能證三果。若已對治欲界的貪欲與瞋恚就可證得三果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4663"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》對治難得等者：此中對治，謂修四無量定，由能永斷欲界貪欲及與瞋恚，故名難得。言得義者，略有二種。一者、證得沙門果義，二者、證得聖神通義。如本地分思所成地中釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/18.htm#46086:15425">陵本十八卷十三頁1574</a>）今說不還，名應得義。證八解脫，離諸愛味，名極廣大。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說的對治，是指慈悲喜捨四無量定，由於修了慈悲喜捨四無量定，能夠永遠斷除欲界的貪欲與瞋恚，因此說難得。所謂的應得義，要略而言有二種，一者、證得聖道果，二者、證得聖人的神通境界。如〈思所成地〉卷18，659頁中所解釋。現在說不還果，名為所應得義。證得八解脫，成就四禪八定及滅盡定，遠離欲界、色界、無色界愛味，稱為極廣大，這不是初果修練根就可以得到的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、不還2　天一、得進離欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不還，分二科；第一科得進離欲，說明不還果的聖人修練根的情況，能進一步離欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若不還者修練根時，既得練根，亦進離欲耶？答：進。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若三果聖人修練根時，既然能夠練根，也能夠進一步離欲嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：可以。這是指依未到地定修聖道證得三果的人，假如繼續修，一定可以離欲得到禪定的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、不證阿羅漢果2　地一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不證阿羅漢果，不還果的聖人修練根不能證阿羅漢果，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：亦證阿羅漢果耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：也可以證得阿羅漢果嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、答2　玄一、由前因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科由前因，由於前因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：不證，由前因故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：不能證得阿羅漢果，是由於前面的原因，什麼原因呢？因為要對治最微細的非想非非想處下下品的我執煩惱，這是很難成就的，所應成就的阿羅漢果及六種神通內容非常廣大，若沒有金剛喻定不能成就。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由前因故者：謂住有學位中，金剛喻定猶未生故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於住有學位三果時，尚未成就能斷最後一品我執煩惱的金剛喻定，所以不能證得阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、明當證</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明當證，說明轉根以後可以證得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">轉根已後，一切皆證。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若修成功以後，轉變根器，就能夠證得阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、明轉根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明轉根，說明轉根的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4664"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故轉根？答：於薄少昇進不生喜足故，為植引發勝定力故，為植多聞力故，為植論議決擇力故，為植觀察甚深法忍力故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為何能夠轉根？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、對於鈍根少許昇進不生喜足；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、為了培植引發殊勝的禪定；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、為栽培多聞力的緣故，所謂的練根，還包括多聞不忘。《瑜伽論記》說：閱讀經律論三藏也是練根，使令根器能夠轉利，可見多聞熏習能夠轉根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、為了栽培論議決擇的能力，成就辯才無礙，也必須練根；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、為培植觀察甚深法的勝解力，也就是為了觀察甚深的法性，成就忍可的智慧，必須修練根。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三果聖人修練根，若成就這五種功德，轉變善根能證得阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、菩薩2　酉一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科菩薩，說明菩薩三無漏根，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸菩薩未知欲知等三根，云何建立？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：諸菩薩的未知欲知根、已知根、與具知根，如何建立？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、答3　戌一、建立初根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科建立初根，建立未知欲知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：於勝解行地，建立初根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：在勝解行地，還在加行位，建立未知欲知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、立第二根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科立第二根，建立已知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於淨增上意樂地等，立第二根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　淨增上意樂地就是初地以上到十地菩薩，因為已經證得出世聖道，內證清淨意樂的緣故，建立第二根已知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、立第三根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科立第三根，建立第三具知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於如來地，立第三根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　成佛就是證得具知根了，這是菩薩無漏的第三根具知根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、圓滿差別2　申一、有學2　酉一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科圓滿差別，圓滿的差別，分二科；第一科有學，說明有學的初果到四果向，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：由幾種滿，名學滿耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：有幾種圓滿稱為有學的圓滿呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、答2　戌一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科略標，要略標出有三種圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4665"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由三種滿。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有學的聖者有三種圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、列釋3　亥一、根滿</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列出三種並解釋，分三科；第一科根滿，說明根滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、根滿，謂利根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、根滿，利根的有學是第一種圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、定滿</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科定滿，說明定滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、定滿，謂八解脫定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、定滿，成就八解脫定的有學聖者，禪定的功德才圓滿。八解脫定就是得到四禪八定及滅盡定，其實最重要的是指滅盡定，如果得到滅盡定，才是定滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、果滿</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科果滿，說明果滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、果滿，謂不還果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、果滿，是指得不還果。初果、二果、三果的有學聖者，最高的果位就是三果。得了三果的聖人可以稱為有學果滿，得了三果永遠不會退失到欲界來了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、無學2　酉一、明得有</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無學，說明無學阿羅漢的圓滿，分二科；第一科明得有，無學阿羅漢得有二滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若諸無學，得有二滿。一、根滿，謂不動法。二、定滿，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若諸無學阿羅漢有二種圓滿， 第一是利根的不動法的無學聖者，稱為根滿；第二是定滿，已得八解脫，成就四禪八定及滅盡定的阿羅漢，稱作定滿，如前文所說應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、顯得名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯得名，顯示一切無學都是果滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一切無學，皆由果滿說名為滿。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一切無學都由果滿說名為滿，因為是聲聞乘最高果位。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若諸無學得有二滿等者：義顯無學，但由果滿說名為滿。根、定二滿義亦得有，然不由此說名為滿。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說無學得有二種圓滿，意思顯示阿羅漢由果滿說名為滿。但是不能說根滿與定滿二種是滿，最圓滿的還是果滿。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是以清淨諸根來分別二十二根，接下來是要分別雜染諸根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、雜染諸根攝2　午一、簡方便2　未一、不調伏2　申一、舉經問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科雜染諸根攝，說明凡夫的境界的雜染諸根，分二科；第一科簡方便，簡別調伏與不調伏的方便，又分二科；第一科不調伏，說明不調伏，又分二科；第一科舉經問，舉經典上說的不調伏相而問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4666"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如說諸根不調、不守、不護、不防，亦不修習，此差別名有何義耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如經典上說：凡夫的六根不調、不守、不護、不防，亦不修習，這麼多不同的名字有什麼不同的道理嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋義答2　酉一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋義答，解釋道理回答，分二科；第一科標，標示出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：略說由四因緣，諸根名不調伏。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：要略而言，根不調伏有四種因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》略說由四因緣等者：此四因緣，謂即前說不守、不護、不防，亦不修習，有是四種，總名不調。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這四種因緣，是前文所說不守、不護、不防，亦不修習，有這四種，總名不調伏。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋2　戌一、舉調伏2　亥一、依簡擇力2　天一、守</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉調伏，舉出調伏的相狀，又分二科；第一科依簡擇力，說明依簡擇力能守護諸根，又分二科；第一科守，說明守。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂簡擇力為依止故，於諸境界，若不應縱諸根之者，便起加行令不縱逸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　簡擇力是聞思慧的境界，聞思慧中主要是思慧，不過要經過聞慧才有思慧，以聞思慧的簡擇力為依止，對於境界，能夠簡擇得失，若不應該放縱六根時，就能如理作意，使六根不攀緣六塵，守住六根不令放縱奔逸於五欲中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、護</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科護，護的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若應縱者，便起加行縱彼諸根，護諸煩惱令不現起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　心境相對，若可以縱許六根去緣取六境時，應當如理作意之後，再令六根去緣取六境，保護這一念心，不要生起煩惱。為什麼有時候要縱許六根去緣取六境呢？有時俗務纏身應當暫時的縱許自己的六根去見聞覺知，但在見聞覺知時，不要讓自己生起煩惱，這是保護諸根。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷16說：若久防護根，多生勞倦，暫時的縱許自己的六根去見聞覺知，應當防護煩惱不令現起，是名保護諸根。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總之依簡擇力能夠守護諸根，守是內斂的，防守諸根不要去接觸外境；護就是於諸根去接觸外境時，保護這念心不要生起煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4667"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、依斷對治力</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依斷對治力，依止能斷煩惱的修慧，修慧才能夠斷除煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">斷對治力為依止故，即於如前所說境界，為性無著，為性煩惱不復現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止修慧斷除對治煩惱，面對色聲香味觸法的境界，能夠防護諸根，心不執著境界；由修慧斷除煩惱的種子，自然就會有根律儀，使得煩惱不再生起現行，這就是修諸根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、成不調</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科成不調，對於諸根沒有守、護、防、修，稱為諸根不調。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若無是四調諸根者，當知彼根名不調伏，由不守故、不護故、不防故、不修故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若沒有運用守、護、防、修這四種方法，令諸根不攀緣外境，或緣取境界時不生煩惱，此時諸根就是不調伏，這是由於不守持、不保護、不防止、不修習諸根的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、善調伏</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科善調伏，說明善調伏諸根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有是四調諸根者，當知與彼四種相違，名為調伏乃至修習。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若能善於運用守、護、防、修這四種方法，令諸根不攀緣外境，或緣取境界時不生煩惱，若與前文所說的沒有用四種方法調伏諸根的情形相反，就稱為於諸根善調伏、善防守、善保護、善防止、善修習。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於諸境界等者：謂於境界根不應縱，能令不縱，名守諸根。若應縱者，雖縱諸根，煩惱不起，名護諸根。如是二種，當知由簡擇力，此即資糧道攝。聲聞地說念防護意，及於非理分別起煩惱意能善防護。如彼別釋，應知其根。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/23.htm#46142:19162">陵本二十三卷二頁1946</a>）又於境界為性無著，名防諸根。為性煩惱不復現行，名修諸根。如是二種，當知由斷對治力，此即離欲地攝。聲聞地說：於境過患，除遣斷滅。又說：由修習力所攝根律儀故，於所緣境，煩惱隨眠不復生起、不復現前；一切時分，依附所依所有隨眠，亦能斷除、亦能永拔。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/23.htm#46142:19326">陵本二十三卷七頁1962</a>）此說為性無著，為性煩惱不復現行，如次配釋應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於境界，不應使令六根放縱在色聲香味觸法上，稱作守諸根。若身不由己，必須去面對色聲香味觸法境界時，守護令心不生起煩惱，就是護諸根。由聞思慧的簡擇力才能夠守持諸根與保護諸根，在資糧位的人是可以做得到的。〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷23，810頁說到念防護意，及於非理分別所起煩惱，意能善防護，如文有詳細的解釋，再讀一讀應該可以了解防護的相貌。該處文說：依於正念防護自己的心意，不要去放縱諸根，稱為念防護意。有時縱許諸根去接觸境界，不要有不如理分別生起煩惱，稱為善防護。對於境界，心沒有執著，這是防諸根。令煩惱種子不起現行，稱為修諸根，由離欲地有禪定功夫的斷對治力，即能防護諸根與修習諸根，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈聲聞地〉說：面對境界內心生起的煩惱，要知道這是有過失災患的，因此能夠除遣斷除消滅內心生起的煩惱；又說：由於有修慧的正念力，成就根律儀，對於所緣的色聲香味觸法境，煩惱種子不再生起，不再現前。一切時分，也能夠永遠拔除依附在阿賴耶識的所有煩惱種子。此處所說的性無著，如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷23，815頁所說次第配合起來解釋就可以知道。為性無著，可以配斷對治力所攝根律儀，是指於境過患，除遣斷滅；為性煩惱不復現行，可以配一切時分，依附所依所有煩惱種子，也能斷除、永拔。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、辨得果2　未一、不調伏攝2　申一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨得果，說明諸根不調伏與諸根調伏的人得到的果報差別，分二科；第一科不調伏攝，說明諸根不調伏的情況，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4668"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何不調伏者能引眾苦？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼說六根不調伏的人能引生種種的眾苦？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋2　酉一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標，標出能生六種苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂能生六種苦故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果不調伏六根，會有六種苦果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出六種苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、擾惱住所生苦，二、他所擯黜苦，三、他所譏毀苦，四、追悔所生苦，五、往生惡趣苦，六、生等諸苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不調伏六根的六種苦果：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、擾惱住所生苦：諸根不調，心裡有很多擾動煩惱產生的苦；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、他所擯黜苦：諸根不調造作惡事，有被他人擯出罷黜出去的苦；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、他所譏毀苦：諸根不調沒有修行的道味，有被他人譏嫌嘲笑的苦；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、追悔所生苦：諸根不調做錯事了，有常常令自己有追憶後悔的苦；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、往生惡趣苦：諸根不調造作惡業，來生還有墮到三惡道去的苦；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、生等諸苦：諸根不調不能斷除煩惱出離生死，會有愛別離苦生老病死等輪迴六道之苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、善調伏攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科善調伏攝，說明諸根善調伏者的結果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有諸根善調伏者，當知與此相違，斷六種苦，引諸快樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若有人能夠守護防修諸根的話，應當了知與諸根不調者相反，能夠斷除以上所說的六種苦，引生種種的快樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯四、相攝差別6　辰一、約三聚有情辨2　巳一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　決擇根善巧，廣分別第二嗢柁南，以長行說明，其中的第四科相攝差別，說明二十二根與其他法的相攝差別，分六科；第一科約三聚有情辨，以欲界、色界、無色界三聚有情分別，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：十四種根、三聚有情，為十四攝三，三攝十四耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中，如果除掉信進念定慧五善根與三無漏根，剩下十四根。十四種根及三聚（界）有情，是十四根攝三聚有情，還是三聚有情攝十四根呢？意指這十四根與三界的有情，三界的範圍廣，還是這十四根的範圍廣呢？如果範圍廣的，就能夠含攝另外一法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、答2　午一、標攝不攝2　未一、標簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標攝不攝，標出攝與不攝，又分二科；第一科標簡，簡別出某一個部分攝，某一個部分不攝的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：三攝十四，非十四攝三。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：是三聚有情含攝這十四根，不是十四根含攝三聚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4669"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、徵釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵釋，以問答的方式解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不攝何等？謂外處少分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼說不是十四根攝三聚，不攝是什麼意思？三界中的器世間，並沒有攝在十四根中，這是外處少分。所以說三聚有情含攝這十四根，不是十四根攝三聚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、隨釋三聚</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋三聚，接著解釋三聚有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三聚有情者，謂欲界、色界、無色界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三聚有情是指欲界、色界、無色界的有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》十四種根等者：二十二根中，除信等五、三無漏，所餘諸根總有十四。由彼繫屬三聚有情自體，由是故說三聚攝彼。然三聚中，外器世間諸所有色，此望有情自體，說名外處少分，由是說彼不攝十四。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二十二根中，除信進念定慧還有三無漏根，信進念定慧是通於有漏無漏，三無漏根唯是無漏，所餘諸根全屬於世間法的有十四個；七色根、意根、命根還有苦樂憂喜捨五受根，加起來有十四根。這十四根是屬於三界有情的自體，因此說三聚攝彼；然而三界當中的外器世間所有的色法，相對有情本身，是外處少分，因此說外處不含攝在這十四根中。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、約三受辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約三受辨，以苦受、樂受、捨受分別二十二根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：五根、三受，為五攝三，三攝五耶？答：更互相攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：苦、樂、憂、喜、捨的五受根及苦、樂、捨的三受，是五受根含攝三受呢，還是三受含攝五受根呢？答：五受根與三受的範圍其實是一樣，只是開合不同，稱為更互相攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》五根三受等者：此說五根，謂苦、樂、憂、喜、捨。三受，謂苦、樂、捨。開合無異，故互相攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處說五根是苦樂憂喜捨，三受是苦、樂、捨。諸受若開展而說就成五種，若合起來說就成三種，其中苦包括憂，樂包括喜，開合不同，因此說三受或五受都是一樣的，所以說更互相攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、約三十七覺品法辨2　巳一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約三十七覺品法辨，說明三十七菩提分法與二十二根相攝的情形，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：五根、三十七覺品法，為五攝三十七，三十七攝五耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：信進念定慧五根與三十七菩提分法，是五根攝三十七菩提分法，或是三十七菩提分法攝五根呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、答2　午一、標攝不攝2　未一、標簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標攝不攝，標出攝不攝，又分二科；第一科標簡，標示簡別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4670"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：三十七攝五，非五攝三十七。</span></strong></span></span></p>
