<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由三門、雜染資長識故，諸求有者，於無間生攝受餘有。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於段食、觸食、意思食三門以及雜染增長諸識，使令求有的有情，無間去取得另外一個生命體。《楞伽阿跋多羅寶經會譯》卷3，佛說：執著境界相是識，不執著境界相是智；根塵識三和合相應生是識，無礙相應自性相是智；有得相是識，無得相是智。又說採集業為識，不採集為智，觀察一切法，通達無所有，逮得自在力，是則名為慧。食是內心的分別，前三種食能增益攝受諸識，其實所有食都是內心的分別執取，當根塵和合生識時，識於食生貪等煩惱，又能採集造作諸業，造業之後又在三界五趣感得苦果，因此生死輪轉不休。有智慧的人應當觀察，受用段食就好像在曠野中不得已而吃自己孩子的肉，內心厭惡而不生樂想；觀觸食如被剝皮的牛為無量虫之所唼食；觀意思食如大火聚燃身；觀識食猶如三百矛鑽身，於食終不生貪樂想，才能出離三界，進一步觀四食由識所生，識依他緣生，空無所有，就能自在無礙，成就聖智。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、別廣段食2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別廣段食，各別廣泛解釋段食的體相，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：段食何時建立為食？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：眾生分段而食的段食，什麼時候才能夠建立為食？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答4　未一、標簡時</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，標出段食於變壞時建立為食，分四科；第一科標簡時，簡別受用時不名段食，而名觸食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：於變壞時。若受用時，建立觸食。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：食物嚼碎變壞進到胃裡面消化以後，才稱為食。若正在吞嚥受用時，是觸食，而不是段食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、出彼體</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出彼體，說明段食的體性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由彼攝受方得增益，</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有情在食物嚼碎變壞消化以後，能夠被攝受成營養，才能使令有情諸根大種獲得增益。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4683"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若受用時建立觸食者：謂諸段物，於吞咽時，令心歡喜，諸根悅豫，當於爾時不名段食，但名觸食。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於分段受用食物，在吞嚥時，心裡很歡喜，諸根喜悅安樂，這時不是段食，而是觸食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故段食三處所攝，謂香、味、觸建立為食，不立色處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所以說段食是香、味、觸三處所攝。以香、味、觸三法建立為食，不立色處為食。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷130：「問何故色處不立為食？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有作是說：無食相故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有說：色處取時麁重，若於取時細輕者名食，要微細轉滋養身故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有說：色處不至而取，食唯至取，非身不合成食事故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有說：色處至變壞位食事方成，謂水所浸爛，火所熟變，風所動搖，然後方成食。所作事，非色未變得名為食，故色非食，香等不爾。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有餘師說：若色是食，眼見色時應除飢渴，若然施主所費則為唐捐。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有餘復言：若色是食，諸出家者眼見色時應犯遠離非時食法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或有說者：若色是食，則色界天應受段食，取諸色故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　當知後三所說乖理，香觸亦有如斯過故，應知前四所說者好。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若色非食經云何通？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如世尊言：長者汝所施食，色香味具甚為妙好。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：色雖非食，為欲發起施主思故佛作是說。謂佛讚美所施食時，施主便發殊勝思願，快哉如來讚受我食，我當必獲殊勝福利。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若讚色具色非食者，亦讚香等俱應非食，彼既是食此亦應然。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：佛於此中不欲簡別是食非食，但欲發起施主思願說此契經，若此讚說即是食者，觸非所讚，便應非食。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、明損益2　申一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科明損益，說明段食的損害或利益，分二科；第一科總標，總相標出段食於變壞後，才對身體有所損益。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由彼要至味勢熟等變壞之位，方損益故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼段食到變壞後，才算是食呢？因為要等到食物嚼碎，香、味、觸變壞以後，才能被消化受用，方能有增益或損害身體的作用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、別辨2　酉一、攝益</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別辨，各別說明損益的相狀，分二科；第一科攝益，說明攝益身心的段食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有段物，於受用時有所損害，於變壞時方能攝益，如苦辛等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有些食物，在受用時感覺不好吃，可是吃下去變壞後就有好處。如苦辛等的藥，在吃藥時感覺很苦不好吃，但是吃下去以後病會好，這是對身體有好處的；若是比較不好吃的食物，但是對身體有幫助，也是要吃。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、損害</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科損害，說明損害身心的段物。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有段物，於受用時暫為攝益，於變壞時乃為損害，如有甘美所不宜物。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有些段食，在受用接觸時，很可口很高興，可是變壞受用時，對身體有損害，如糖或可樂，雖然甘美但對身體有所不宜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、結建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結建立，結說段食於變壞時才建立為食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">故變壞時方立為食，非受用時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　段食變壞後才建立為食，不是受用時建立為食。受用時，覺得好吃，不一定對身體有益。食物吃下去後能攝益增長諸識及諸根大種，才安立為食。因此對於食物的選擇不要以口味為重，應以能不能攝益身心為標準。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂香味觸建立為食等者：思所成慧地決擇中說：此中段食，當言香、味、觸處所攝。何以故？由香、味、觸，若正消變，便能長養；不正消變，乃為損減。色等餘法無有長養、損減消變，是故說彼非段食性。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/66.htm#46348:52583">陵本六十六卷四頁5259</a>）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈思所成慧地〉決擇中說：此處文中所說段食，應當說是香味觸處所攝。為什麼呢？由於有香、味、觸才受用這些食物，要等到食物正在被嚼碎變壞消化後，才能長養根身，如果不能消化、不能變壞，就會對身體有所損減。色與聲這二法對於身體沒有長養、損減、消變的功能，因此不說色與聲是屬於段食。在卷66，2109頁有說到這一段，可以參考能了解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、簡不說餘2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科簡不說餘，簡別不說其他令生命安住的因緣，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4684"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：更有所餘眾多行法住因可得，謂生、先業、神通、因緣合會、離障；何故但說此四為食？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：更有其他有為法能夠令生命安住的因緣，如出生、過去世的業力、神通、因緣合會、遠離種種的障礙，為什麼只有說這四種是食？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂生先業神通等者：思所成慧地決擇中說：有七因緣，任持諸行，令住不壞。今此除彼命根及食，故唯說五。彼云：生是諸行住因。由諸行生，方得有住，無有無生而有住者。又云：由善、不善、無記作意引發先業，能牽諸行令住不絕。所謂外分，共不共業之所生起。又云：心自在通。由彼勢力，增諸壽行，或住一劫、或住劫餘。又云：因緣和合是諸行住因。謂善、不善、無記諸法，乃至因緣猶未散壞，於爾所時相續而住，無有斷絕。又云：無諸障礙是諸行住因。由此能令諸行生時無障因緣，諸行生已相似相續而住，遠離相違敗壞因緣。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/66.htm#46352:52537">陵本六十六卷三頁5254</a>）此說五種，一、生，二、先業，三、神通，四、因緣合會，五、離障，如彼應釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷66，2107頁決擇中說：有七種因緣任持一切有為法，使一切有為法安住不壞。現在除了沒有說到命根與食之外，只說到其中五種。那裡的文說到：出生是諸行安住的原因，沒有未出生而有安住的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又說：由於善法、不善法或是無記法相應的作意心所，引發過去生所造的業力現前，使令自業引生的生命體，以及共業所引生的器世間相續不絕。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又說：如果有禪定心自在得到神通，由於神通的力量，也會使壽命增加，可以住世一劫，或者超過一劫以上，或多劫以上。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又說：因緣和合是這一切有為法安住的原因，由於有善法、不善法、或無記諸法，這些因緣還沒有散失破壞，在這些時候，有為法諸行能夠相續而住，無有斷絕。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如卷66，2107頁又說：沒有障礙是一切有為法安住的原因，由此能令諸行生時沒有障礙的因緣，諸行生了以後能夠相似相續的安住，遠離相違的因緣而暫時不會敗壞。這裡說五種是指：一、生，二、先業，三、神通，四、因緣合會，五、離障。如彼卷66決擇所說，應當如此解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答2　未一、略標義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科略標義，要略標出道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：以多分故，易覺知故，於諸念住易趣入故，於日日分易資養故，唯此四種應顯為食。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有這麼多原因可以使五蘊的生命體安住，為什麼只有說四食能夠令生命體相續安住呢？對於已經存在的生命體而言，四食是能夠使生命體安住的主要的因緣，而且容易感覺得到，於四念住中也容易趣入，因為依身念住觀段食，受念住觀觸食，法念住觀思食，心念住觀識食，每天都能夠資養諸識及諸根大種，因此唯此四種應當開顯為食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4685"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》以多分故等者：謂此四食是諸行住多分因緣，由種種門，能令諸行相續而住。又此諸食，能令有情相續而住，易取易入，乃至愚夫嬰兒等類亦能隨覺，非所餘法。又此諸食，令易入道，能修身等四種念住。謂一切有情食所住故。又有長壽諸有情類，若不得食，非時中夭。亦如思所成慧地決擇中說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/66.htm#46357:52559">陵本六十六卷四頁5256</a>）此中四種，如彼應釋。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這四種食是使五蘊身心能夠安住的主要的因緣，由種種方式，能令五蘊身心相續而住。又這四種食能令有情相續而住，容易取得及受用消化，乃至凡夫或者是嬰兒等類也知道要有食，不是要有其他的法。嬰兒什麼都不懂，就知道要吃，凡夫更是民以食為天，以食物滋養生命是有情的共業。又從觀察這四種食也容易入道，能夠修身、受、心、法四念住，身念住可以觀段食；受念住觀觸食，因為由觸生受，心念住觀識食，識就是心的別名，法念住要觀思食；又因為一切有情由食而得安住，所以依四種食修四念住，可以斷除煩惱出離生死。長壽的有情，如果沒有得到食物也會非時中夭，如〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷66，2108頁決擇中說，這四種食，應以該處所說而解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、別簡非2　申一、簡非多分</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別簡非，各別簡除沒有段食的情況，分二科；第一科簡非多分，簡別不是多分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">那落迦中無有段食，定地諸天亦復如是。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　地獄中的有情沒有段食。還有有禪定的諸天，色界天以上的天人，也是一樣沒有段食，他們以禪悅為食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、簡非易知</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡非易知，簡別不容易了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸那落迦，多由先業力所任持而得久住，雖有廣大諸根大種損害因緣，而不能死。然彼亦有諸微細風隨入身分，以之為食；難可了知，是故不說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　種種的地獄中的有情，多數由過去生的業力所任持而能久住，雖然有廣大的諸根大種受到損害的因緣，卻不能使他死掉。然而他的腑臟裡面有微動風，有這個風吹入他的身體，以之為食，只是微動風難可了知，所以不說有段食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4686"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》諸微細風隨入身分等者：本地分中有尋有伺地說：於那落迦受生有情，有微細段食。謂腑藏中有微動風，由此因緣，彼得久住。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/05.htm#46363:3306">陵本五卷五頁335</a>）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧有尋有伺地〉卷5，135頁說：在地獄受生的有情，有微細的段食，因為他的腑藏中有微動風，由這個因緣，使他們能夠久住，此處應該準照卷5的解釋而知。　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯六、諸句差別2　辰一、約所依辨2　巳一、依差別2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　決擇根善巧，廣分別第二嗢柁南，以長行來說明，其中的最後一科，第六科諸句差別，依二句、三句、四句等諸句問答決擇諸根的差別，分二科；第一科約所依辨，以所依身及諸受說二十二根的諸句差別，又分二科；第一科依差別，約所依差別說，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸根依身轉，亦依境界耶？設依境界者，亦依身轉耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根是依止著身而現前，還是依止著境界才會現前？或是依止境界，也依止身轉呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答2　未一、略標簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科略標簡，要略標示出來簡別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：若根依境界，必依身而轉。或有依身轉，而不依境界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：如果根是依止著境界而活動時，還必定要依止著身而轉，因為根是依附在身體上的。或者有時候這個根是依止於身體上，在身體上相續活動，而不在境界上活動，不是依止境界的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨難釋，接下來將困難的地方解釋一下。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂諸有色彼同分根，以諸大種為依止故，說彼依身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　根依止在身體上繼續現前，而不依止於境界，這是什麼情況？這是指諸有色根沒有識的作用，如於靜坐時眼根沒有識的作用，或視而不見，這時的眼根稱為彼同分根，只是有色根依止於地水火風四大種上，相似相續的現前，但沒有識的作用，因此說根依止於身；又由於沒有取境的功能，所以說不依境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂諸有色彼同分根者：如前已說：有識眼界，名為同分；所餘眼界，名彼同分。如眼界，乃至身界亦爾。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/56.htm#46370:44365">陵本五十六卷九頁4514</a>）今說有色彼同分根，即彼無識諸界應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面卷56，1851頁決擇已經說過，有識一起活動的眼界，稱為同分；其餘眼界，沒有識一起活動，稱為彼同分。如眼界如此，耳鼻舌身也是一樣。現在說有色彼同分根，是沒有識一起活動的眼界應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、依多寡2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依多寡，說明依多寡，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若諸根有所依而轉者，彼一切皆一依耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若是諸根有所依止而能夠現前的話，這一切都是一種依止的情況嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4687"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答3　未一、一依</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科一依，有一依、二依及三依的情況，舉出有色根只有一種依止的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：或有一依，謂諸有色彼同分根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：或者只有一種依止的情況；眼耳鼻舌身男女根，沒有與識一起活動，又稱為彼同分根，只有依止身而轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、二依</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科二依，有色根有二種依止的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有二依，謂即有色同分諸根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或有二種依止的情況，有色根是依止於身及境界；當眼耳鼻舌身男女根與識一起活動，稱為同分諸根，這時諸有色根就依止於身及境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、三依2　申一、出於有色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科三依，無色根有三依或二依，分二科；第一科出於有色，諸根在欲界和色界有三依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有三依，所謂意根及餘無色心法諸根，在有色界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或有三依的情況，意根與其餘無色的心所法諸根，如五受根、五善根的作用都是依止於心的。因此在有色的欲界和色界，意根及餘心法諸根必須依止身、境界、及心才能生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、簡於無色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡於無色，簡別於無色界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於無色，即此諸根唯有二依。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　意根及餘心法諸根，如果在無色界只有二種依，依止著心、與境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或有一依等者：謂依身轉，名有一依。依身、境界，名有二依。在有色界，意根及餘無色心法諸根，依身、境界及與心轉，名有三依。若於無色，即此諸根唯依於心及境界轉，名有二依。言餘無色心法諸根者，謂苦、樂、喜、憂、捨，及信等五應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　諸根如果依止著身而活動的話，稱作一依。依止著身及境界，稱作有二依。在有色界，意根及餘無色心法諸根，如五受根及五善根，依身、境界及與心轉，稱為有三依。若是在無色界，意根及餘無色心法諸根只有依止著心與境界轉，稱為有二依。說其餘無色心法諸根，是指苦、樂、喜、憂、捨五受根，及信進念定慧五善根應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、約諸受辨2　巳一、辨苦合等2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科約諸受辨，以諸受分別二十二根，分二科；第一科辨苦合等，分別苦合等，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4688"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸根是苦者，一切苦相合耶？設苦相合者，一切是苦耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：二十二根中有一些是苦根，一切苦根都是與苦相合的嗎？假設與苦相合的根，都是苦根嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答4　未一、是苦非苦相合</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，用四句來回答，分四科；第一科是苦非苦相合，第一句是有苦根非苦相合。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：或諸根是苦，而非苦相合，謂樂根、喜根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：或者有根的體性是苦，可是不與苦相合，這是樂根與喜根是屬於五受根，樂根通於五識、六識，喜根唯第六識相應。佛說諸受皆苦，受的體性是苦，可是樂根、喜根的相又不是與苦相合。所以樂根、喜根是苦，非苦相合。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、是苦亦苦相合</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科是苦亦苦相合，第二句是苦也與苦相合。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有是苦，亦苦相合，謂苦根、憂根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者有是苦，也與苦相合，這是苦根、憂根本身是苦，也是苦的相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、是苦非苦樂相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科是苦非苦樂相，第三句是苦非苦樂相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有是苦，非苦樂相，謂捨根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者有一種根是苦，非苦樂相，這是捨根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、非苦亦非苦相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科非苦亦非苦相，第四句非苦也不是苦相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有非苦，亦非苦相，謂後三根，苦對治故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者有一種根，體性不是苦，也不是苦相，是後三無漏根，未知欲知根、已知根及具知根，這三根能夠對治苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、辨引樂等2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨引樂等，分別能引生快樂等根的性質，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸根是善，彼根引樂耶？設根引樂，彼根是善耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：有一些根，本身體性是善的，這些根能夠引生快樂嗎？若是能夠引生快樂的根，這些根是屬於善性嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答4　未一、是善不引樂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，用四句回答，分四科；第一科是善不引樂，第一句是善根但不能夠引生快樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4689"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：或根是善，而不引樂，謂憂、苦俱而修梵行，彼諸善根於現法中不能引樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：或有一種情況，這些根的體性是善，可是不能引生快樂，那是心中有憂受、苦受，而修清淨的梵行，這時的信等善根於現在的生命體不能引生快樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、引樂非是善</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科引樂非是善，有一種根能夠引生快樂，可是不是善根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或根引樂，而非是善，謂諸無記及不善根，於現法中能引無記及染汙樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者有一種根能夠引生快樂，可是它不是善根，是指無記的根及不善相應的根，如無記的七色根或意根及五受根一分與不善法相應，在現在的色受想行識當中，能引生無記的快樂與染污的快樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、是善亦引樂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科是善亦引樂，有一種根是善，也能夠引生快樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或根是善，亦能引樂，謂喜、樂俱修諸梵行所有善根，於現法中能引其樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者有一種根是善，也能引生快樂，就是有喜、樂受相應修種種梵行的所有善根，在現在的生命體中能夠引生快樂。在欲界修梵行通常比較憂苦，如果得定以後，就有喜樂相應，身心自然輕快，這樣的善根，能夠引生快樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、非善不引樂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科非善不引樂，有一種根體性不是善，也不能引生快樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或根非善，亦不引樂，謂諸無記及不善根，於現法中能引諸苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者有一種體性不是善，也不能引生快樂，這是指種種的無記根及不善根，在現在的生命體中能引生諸苦。如無記的七色根或意根及五受根一分與不善法相應而有所造作，又能引生種種痛苦時。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、嗢柁南結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科嗢柁南結，用一個偈頌再將前面決擇過的幾科合起來作一個總結。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">中嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　義依處證得　攝食由諸句</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一大段文中間的偈頌說：義依處證得，攝食由諸句。分成六科；第一科決擇諸根境義差別，第二科決擇諸根依處差別，第三科決擇諸根證得等差別，第四科決擇諸根相攝差別；第五科決擇諸根由攝食所長養差別說明，第六科決擇諸根諸句差別。用義依處證得，攝食由諸句，就能了解所研習的二十二根的各種情況。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　卷51-57決擇〈五識身相應地〉、〈意地〉，分成五個部分，《披尋記》的作者分成五大科來討論，第一科是阿賴耶識；第二科是識身差別；第三科是三世四緣；第四科是心不相應行等；第五科是六善巧。六善巧又分成三科；第一科是指前生後；第二科是別釋一一。別釋一一又分二科；第一科是廣建立，是將蘊善巧、界善巧、處善巧、緣起善巧、處非處善巧與根善巧，很廣泛的說明了，直到上面的嗢柁南結為止，六善巧已經全部決擇過了，下面是第二大科略攝義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚二、略攝義2　辛一、別辨安立3　壬一、名義差別6　癸一、蘊3　子一、第一義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科略攝義，要略攝取六善巧的名義等差別，及總觀六善巧所攝的殊勝利益，分二科；第一科別辨安立，各別說明六善巧的安立，又分三科；第一科名義差別，說明六善巧能詮的名差別與所詮的義差別，又分六科；第一科蘊，說明蘊善巧的蘊的名義差別，又分三科；第一科第一義，以第一個義理說明蘊的名義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，具足攝持一切行義；具足攝持一切行義，是故名蘊。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，蘊具備圓滿攝持一切遷流不息的有為諸行的體性，因為具備圓滿攝持一切遷流不息的有為諸行的體性，所以說名為蘊。《瑜伽論記》說，重複二次這樣的句法，第一句是說蘊的體性，就是蘊本身的體性是這樣，這是以蘊的義而言；第二句是以蘊的名而言，因為這樣所以才稱為蘊。韓清淨居士解釋，以勝義諦而言一切諸法都沒有真實的體性，然而以世俗諦，為了方便讓世間人認識分別，簡別餘法而假名安立自性；由這種道理，說五蘊具足攝持一切行義為其自性，由自性義安立蘊的名稱。為了顯示這種道理，所以重說一次。第一句是以世俗諦中蘊的自性而言，第二句是由這個自性義，安立蘊的名稱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、第二義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二義，以第二義理說明蘊的名義，是以蘊能積聚增長諸業煩惱，能攝苦集而安立的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4690"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有別義。常能增長諸業煩惱；常能增長諸業煩惱，是故名蘊。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘊又有第二義，蘊的體性就是常常能夠增長種種的業及煩惱；又因為蘊能常常能夠增長種種的業及種種的煩惱積聚，假名安立為蘊，這都是以世俗諦而言。由於蘊是前生顛倒分別所生的顛倒境，依此顛倒境能生虛妄分別，生起種種煩惱而造業所生的果報。若以勝義諦而言，蘊及業、煩惱等都是內心的虛妄分別，了無實體可得，所以無蘊可得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、第三義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三義，以第三義理說明蘊的名義，是以蘊能常有所為及速滅壞而安立的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有別義。常有所為及速滅壞；常有所為及速滅壞，是故名蘊。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘊又有第三義，又因為蘊的體性就是常常有所造作，又很快的消滅破壞，這樣的無常法，假名安立為蘊，這是以世俗諦而言。若以勝義諦而言，蘊是內心的虛妄分別所現，如幻的心念是內心的造作，說名常有所為，如幻的心剎那無常，說名速滅壞。諸法本不生，眾緣生諸法，此有故彼有，此無故彼無，所以無蘊可得。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上蘊的第一種義說明蘊是有為法，蘊的第二種義說明蘊是有漏法，蘊的第三種義說明蘊是無常法，所以蘊能總攝有為、有漏、及無常三義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科界，說明界的名義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">發起諸法；發起諸法，是故名界，是牽引義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就世俗諦而言，界就是種子，由界才能夠現起種種的法，所以假名安立為界。又種子具有牽引諸法現行的作用，假名安立為牽引義。就勝義諦而言，種子是假安立法，由緣所生，本身了不可得，所以界不可得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、處</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科處，說明處的名義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能生能廣諸心心法；能生能廣諸心心法，是故名處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　處，梵文原意是指「所進入的場所」即內六根，及「進入的事物」即色、聲、香、味、觸、法外六塵。&nbsp;內六根又稱為六內處，外六塵就是六外處，內外各六處，合為十二處。依六根觸對六塵，能生起六識及相應心所，所以就世俗諦而言，處的體性就是能生長、增廣種種的心王與心所法，由於處能生長、增廣種種的心王與心所法，假名安立為處。就勝義諦而言，處是內心的虛妄分別唯識所現，識是依他緣生無實自性，所以處不可得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4691"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸四、緣起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科緣起，說明緣起的名義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由眾緣故速壞集起；由眾緣故速壞集起，故名緣起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就世俗諦而言，緣起的體性是依眾緣而生起，眾緣離散時法就立即壞滅，諸行壞滅後由於未斷無明和愛等煩惱，所以還會集聚下一期眾緣所生的苦果生起，假名安立為緣起。就勝義諦而言，眾緣無實自性，所以緣起的實性不可得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸五、處非處</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科處非處，處就是合於因果的道理；非處就是不合因果道理，說明處非處的名義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">等起理趣；等起理趣，是故名處。若非理趣，說名非處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就世俗諦而言，處的體性就是諸法的生起符合因果的道理，假名安立為處，如說善因得樂果，惡因得苦果等。如果不符合因果的道理，就稱為非處，如說善因得苦果，惡因得樂果等。就勝義諦而言，一切法本不可得，處非處亦不可得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸六、根</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科根，說明根的名義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於見等事自在相應；於見等事自在相應，是故名根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　根，梵語indriya，音譯因姪唎焰，具有最勝、自在、光顯、增上等義。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說於見等事自在相應，是說：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、眼根於見色之事最為自在有力，能與眼識見色所依、作事相應，同取色境為事（《大乘阿毘達磨集論》卷3：於一所作事展轉相攝，名作事相應。）；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、耳根於聞聲之事最為自在有力，能與耳識聞聲所依、作事相應，同取聲境為事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、鼻根於臭香之事最為自在有力，能與鼻識臭香所依、作事相應，同取香境為事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、根於嘗味之事最為自在有力，能與舌識嘗味所依、作事相應，同取味境為事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、身根於覺觸之事最為自在有力，能與身識嘗味所依、作事相應，同取觸境為事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、七、男女二根於習欲之事最為自在有力，主要能與身識習欲所依、作事相應，同取欲境為事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、意根於了法之事最為自在有力，能與意識了法所依、作事相應，同取法境為事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、命根於令五蘊存活之事最為自在有力，能與本有、中有、生有所依，與五蘊存活時，和合相應；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十～十四、苦等五受根於領納可意等境、引生愛恚等事最為自在有力，能與可意等境、愛恚等煩惱所依，與六根六識六觸作事相應，同取六境為事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十五～十九、信等五根於趣入善法等事最為自在有力，信根能與趣入善法所依、進根能與恆常修習善法所依、念根能與正知而行所依、定根能與智見清淨所依、慧根能與煩惱永斷所依，與意根意識作事相應，同取三寶、四諦、三學等境為事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二十、未知根通於有漏無漏，於趣入出世間善法之事最為自在有力，能與證初、二、三果所依，與意根（意識、根本智、後得智）、樂喜捨三根及五善根作事相應，同取四諦之理為事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二十一、已知根於趣入修道證果之事最為自在有力，能與修道乃至金剛喻定所依，與意根（無分別智、後得智）、樂喜捨三根及五善根作事相應，同取一切繫不繫法為義、為所作事；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二十二、具知根唯是無漏，於趣入修道證果之事最為自在有力，能與無間煩惱永斷作證、現法樂住、永滅所依，與意根（根本智、後得智）、樂喜捨三根及五善根作事相應，同取一切繫不繫法為義、為所作事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是二十二根隨其所對應的法都具有自在有力、功能相應的作用，因此名為「根」。這是約世俗諦而言，若約勝義諦而言，根是唯識所現，識又依他緣生，無實自性，所以根不可得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》具足攝持一切行義等者：此中蘊義，略由三種。一、由有為，二、由有漏，三、由無常。由有為者，謂彼五蘊通漏無漏，具足攝持一切行義，即由此義是故名蘊。由有漏者，謂五取蘊常能增長諸業煩惱，此唯有漏，即由此義是故名蘊。由無常者，有漏五蘊生滅無常，常有所為及速滅壞，即由此義是故名蘊。依勝義諦，一切諸法皆無自性，然約世俗，為簡餘法假立自性；由是道理，說彼五蘊具足攝持一切行義為其自性，即由如是自性義故，安立蘊名。為顯此義，是故重說。又有別義，及餘界、處、緣起、處非處、根，一切重說，道理亦爾。言是牽引義者，謂自種子能為牽引因故。能生能廣諸心心法者，謂是生長門義故。言由眾緣故速壞集起者，十二有支前為後緣，是名眾緣，由是積集純大苦蘊，生滅無常故。言於見等事自在相應者，如前已說二十二根建立。謂能取境增上義故，建立六根；乃至廣說出世清淨增上義故，建立三根。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/57.htm#46429:45096">陵本五十七卷五頁4576</a>）此總顯彼，故作是說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說蘊義，要略而言有三種。一、由有為，二、由有漏，三、由無常。由有為，是指五蘊通有漏與無漏有為，具備圓滿攝持一切諸行的道理，由這種道理稱為蘊。由有漏，是指五取蘊常常能夠增長種種的業和煩惱，這是指有漏五蘊，由這種道理，稱為蘊。由無常，是指有漏的五蘊常常生滅無常，常有所作為及迅速滅壞，由這種道理，稱為蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以勝義諦來說一切諸法都沒有真實的體性，然而以世俗諦，為了方便讓世間人認識分別，簡別餘法而假名安立自性；由這種道理，說五蘊具足攝持一切行義為其自性，由這個自性義，安立蘊的名稱。為了顯示這種道理，所以重說一次，而且還有其他的道理，其餘界、處、緣起、處非處、根，一切重說，道理也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說牽引的意思，是指自種子，能牽引諸法生起的緣故。說能生長增廣諸心心所法，是生長門的意思。說由眾緣故速壞集起，是指十二有支，前支為後支的增上緣，稱為眾緣，由此積集純大苦蘊，生滅無常。說能於見等事自在相應，如前已說的二十二根建立，各有各的作用，以有能力取得各種相應境界，建立六根，乃至廣說出世清淨增上力的緣故，建立三無漏根。如前本卷中的根善巧決擇，明建立科下，作業差別辨眼等六根所說，這是總相顯示那裡的道理，簡單的作這樣歸類。如本卷1873頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、立因差別2　癸一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科立因差別，說明安立蘊、界、處、緣起、處非處善巧的原因不同，分二科；第一科標，標示出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4692"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知蘊等略由六因而得建立。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知蘊、界、處、緣起、處非處及根善巧，這六種善巧要略而言由六種原因而建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出六種原因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂身體建立、彼因建立、身者建立、彼轉方便建立、即於彼轉勝劣方便建立、即彼受用增上建立。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身是積聚義，由依有情五蘊身的體性建立蘊善巧；以眼耳鼻舌身意等種子為因，而建立界善巧；身有內身義，由依身（五色根）、身者（染污意根）、受者識（無間滅意根）等六內處（六根）能領受外六處生長六識心心所，而建立處善巧。由於有情依眾緣流轉生死，建立緣起善巧；針對流轉因果法則有符不符合事理的勝劣差別，建立處非處善巧；針對有情受用境界的增上力，而建立根善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》略由六因而得建立等者：此中六因，如次配釋蘊乃至根。言身者建立者，攝大乘論說：身、身者、受者識，應知即是眼等六內界。（攝論二卷一頁）依此建立諸處善巧，由世俗諦義可得故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處所說六因，如其次第配蘊乃至根。說身者建立，《攝大乘論》卷2說：身（五色根）、身者（染污意根）、受者識（無間滅意根）等六內處，應當知道就是指眼耳鼻舌身意等六內界，由此能生能長諸心心所，因此依此建立諸處善巧，這是以世俗諦的道理而安立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、遣執差別3　癸一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科遣執差別，安立六善巧為了去除不同的執著，分三科；第一科標，標出顯示六種善巧，為遣六種邪執。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復略顯示六種善巧，當知為遣六種邪執。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，要略的顯示六種善巧，應當了知是為了遣除六種不正確的執著。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為六？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪六種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、依止邪執，二、自性自在等不平等因邪執，三、能持依止我邪執，四、彼死生轉邪執，五、彼淨不淨方便邪執，六、彼愛非愛境界受用主宰邪執。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、依止邪執：依止的是身體，對身體有錯誤的執著，認為那是我，所以安立蘊善巧，使有情通達有為、有漏、無常諸蘊是唯識所現，依他緣生，無實法實我，而破除依止邪執；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、自性自在等不平等因邪執：為了對治外道執著一切法由大自在天等不平等因所生的邪執，而安立界善巧，說明一切法由種子所生，十八界是諸法的正因，去除不平等因見，建立正確的因果觀；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、能持依止我邪執：為對治外道執著有我依根緣境生識，而安立處善巧，說明一切心法現前只是根境和合生識的作用，並沒有我住在根身中操作一切法，由此遣除能持依止我邪執；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、彼死生轉邪執：為了對治外道執著有情前八萬劫的生死是有始，後八萬劫的生死是有終，而安立緣起善巧，說明眾緣具足而有惑業苦的流轉，眾緣唯識所現，無實自性，流轉也無先後性，由此悟入真如，遣除外道對死生流轉的邪執；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、彼淨不淨方便邪執：淨就是正確的因果，不淨就是不正確的因果；淨就是處，不淨就是非處。為了對治外道執著不正確的因果，以為用不正確的方法修行可以出離生死輪迴，而安立處非處善巧，由此建立正確的因果觀，用正確的方法修行出離生死，遣除外道淨不淨方便邪執；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、彼愛非愛境界受用主宰邪執：為了對治外道執著有我主宰受用可愛的境界或不可愛的境界，而安立根善巧，說明於受用境界增上說名為根，是根在受用境界，不是我在受用境界，根也是唯識所現，無實無我，由此遣除外道愛非愛境界受用主宰邪執。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總之，眾生由於有種種徧計所執，而於諸法執著有實法實我，為了對治眾生的執著，佛菩薩慈悲從於我法二空真如相應之勝義智，依世俗諦善巧安立蘊、界、處、緣起、處非處善巧及根善巧，為眾生解粘去縛，遣除種種邪執。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4693"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知為遣六種邪執等者：此中六種邪執，依六善巧，如其次第能正除遣，故作是說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此中所說六種邪執，應知依止六種善巧，能夠次第的、正確的除遣這六種邪執，所以這樣說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、總觀勝利2　壬一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總觀勝利，總觀六善巧殊勝的利益，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：觀幾勝利，分別建立簡擇諸法、修習善巧？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：由觀察修習六種善巧而分別、建立、簡擇諸法，有哪些殊勝的利益呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、答3　癸一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科標，標出有十種好處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：略有十種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：要略而言有十種好處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、列4　子一、蘊界處善巧攝4　丑一、離增益執</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，分四科；第一科蘊界處善巧攝，列出蘊界處善巧所攝四種勝利；離增益執、離損減執、除自他疑、令教久住，又分四科；第一科離增益執，先說離增益執。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂當遍知薩迦耶見，分析一合之想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　薩迦耶見又譯作有身見，或譯作虛偽身見、移轉身見，是在自身五蘊和合之體上，執著我及我所的妄見。若通達蘊界處善巧，知道這個身體是五蘊的和合體，雖然五蘊的體性相狀各個不同，都是由阿賴耶識中前生所造業種子遇緣所生的現行，由眼等六內處執取外六處，才有種種受用境界，其中並沒有任何我的體相可得，我是自己的虛妄分別增加上去的執著，如此分析五蘊與我只是一合之想，其實五蘊中無我無我所，由此遠離增益執，斷除薩迦耶見，這是第一種勝利。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、離損減執</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科離損減執，第二種勝利是離損減執，知道於蘊等中沒有我，惟因緣所生的蘊、界、處還是存在的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於有法現有諦故、住故，便不誹謗。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於因緣所生的如幻的有法，現在是存在著，安住在這裡，因此就不會撥無因果。若通達蘊、界、處可以使令離損減執，這是第二種勝利。一切法依勝義是不真實的，可是依世俗並不是說完全沒有法，空不是沒有。空是一種很重要的智慧，唯識學為了避免有情執取斷滅空，而說：此中無有彼物稱為空，這裡沒有那件事情，稱為空，不是連這裡都沒有，不然就不用討論空了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《小空經》裡面說，鹿子母堂裡面，有比丘在這裡，可是沒有牛與羊，以鹿子母堂裡面沒有牛與羊，稱為空，不是說這裡什麼都沒有，稱為空。因此雖然說我是沒有，可是緣起的如幻的有法如蘊、界、處，因緣具足還是有的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、除自他疑</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科除自他疑，第三種勝利能除自他之疑。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4694"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自無疑惑，善答他問。未信令信，已信令增。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果通達蘊、界、處善巧，能令自己沒有疑惑，也能夠善巧回答他人的問題，遣除自己與他人的疑惑。使原來不相信佛法的人，能令其能相信佛法，已經相信佛法的人，會更加增長其信心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、令教久住</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科令教久住，第四種勝利能令聖教久住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亦令如來聖教久住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　學習蘊、界、處善巧或任何佛法，將來有機會可以弘揚佛法或者自修，都可以使如來聖教長久住世。以上是蘊、界、處善巧的四個好處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、緣起善巧攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科緣起善巧攝，說明緣起善巧所攝的殊勝利益。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又當悟入緣起道理，能了釋、梵、世主、自性及士夫等非作者，無實性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又應該悟入緣起的道理，了知無明緣行乃至生緣老死等，惑業苦的輪轉道理，就不會認為帝釋天、梵天王、世主：大自在天及士夫等，是創造出生命體的主宰者。生命只是惑業苦的輪轉，也沒有真實的體性，沒有所謂創世主的存在。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、處非處善巧攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科處非處善巧攝，說明處非處善巧所攝的殊勝利益。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又令慧根增長廣大，於善不善如實了知，廣說乃至緣生差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又通達處非處善巧，可以使令慧根增長廣大，對於善法與不善法，善因樂果，惡因苦果，能夠如實正確的了知，廣說乃至因緣所生法有種種的差別，因為有處非處善巧的智慧，就能夠正確的決擇通達。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、根善巧攝4　丑一、當善住念</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科根善巧攝，根善巧所攝的殊勝利益有四：當善住念、證心一境、生起聖慧、隨證漏盡，分四科；第一科當善住念，先說當善住念。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於善不善法廣說乃至緣生差別，當善住念。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又研讀根善巧，對於善不善法，與種種因緣所生的差別法，是染、是淨，是聖、是凡，就能善於安住正念，這是根善巧所攝的第一種殊勝利益。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、證心一境</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科證心一境，第二種殊勝利益，就是能證得禪定心一境性的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由有法隨法行故，即以住念為依止、為建立，當證善心一境之性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有法隨法行，法就是涅槃，隨法就是三十七道品，能知道最終的目標是什麼？也知道怎麼修行，就安住在正念中，以此正念能為依止、為建立，就能證得與善法相應的心一境性，成就禪定的功德。又在定中修觀，才能斷除煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、生起聖慧</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科生起聖慧，第三種殊勝利益，就是能生起聖慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="57p4695"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又即以此心一境性為依止、為建立，令聖慧根當得生起。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又以此心一境性，為依止、為建立，在定中修毗鉢舍那，使令不共於外道、無漏的聖慧可以生起。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、隨證漏盡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科隨證漏盡，第四種殊勝利益，就是能永斷顛倒，隨證漏盡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依聖慧根，永斷顛倒，隨證漏盡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止無漏的聖慧，能永遠斷除常樂我淨的顛倒，將無始劫來，執著諸法有我及諸法是實的煩惱種子斷除，隨順證得煩惱完全斷除的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由觀如是諸勝利故，分別建立簡擇諸法、修習善巧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於觀察蘊等善巧有這麼多殊勝的利益，應該分別、建立、簡擇諸法，修習這六種善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》略有十種等者：謂蘊、界、處三種善巧，總說有四勝利；緣起善巧有一勝利；處非處善巧有一勝利；根善巧有四勝利。如判應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘊、界、處三種善巧有離增益執、離損減執、除自他疑、令教久住四種勝利；緣起善巧有一種了知緣生與惑業苦輪轉道理，諸法沒有真實體性的勝利；處非處善巧有令慧根增長廣大的一種勝利；根善巧有當善住念、證心一境、生起聖慧、隨證漏盡的四種勝利，總共十種，就像文中所分科判定的這樣應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丁三、略不說餘</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科略不說餘，〈五識身相應地〉、〈意地〉決擇要略說到此，不再多說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">已略決擇五識身地、意地，於二地中餘決擇文，更不復現。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已經要略決斷簡擇〈五識身相應地〉與〈意地〉，於這個二地中其他決斷簡擇的文，不會再出現了。彌勒菩薩所說的，對我們學習來說很長很難，對佛菩薩來說，只是一點點而已。玅境長老常常鼓勵我們說：你們要修定，因為得了未到地定以後，記憶力跟一般人就不一樣了，如果得了陀羅尼，記憶是一片的，就是很快就記得。沒有定的人，心很散亂，記一點點都很難。這是我們的境界。本論是一部大的無我觀，大家在這裡學習，在每一段文中，藉由佛菩薩的聖慧，善巧觀察諸多緣起法的自相與共相，若能依教奉行，如理思惟、觀察、勤修止觀，對於諸法實相的通達，應當是指日可待。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第五十七</span></strong></span></span></p>
